
-----title
洛阳 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8b99801fdbb64e57805ba41157d4eefc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8b99801fdbb64e57805ba41157d4eefc");'><span id='8b99801fdbb64e57805ba41157d4eefc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=784')">772-784年</a>，1-13岁</div><div id='8b99801fdbb64e57805ba41157d4eefc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　是年出生。家族在洛阳有田产，当居洛阳。本年，其父吕渭任浙西观察支使，检校大理评事。浙西节度使治所润州，今江苏镇江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=774')">773-774年</a>　少居洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　少居洛阳。其父吕渭在浙西李涵幕，随李涵出使河北慰谕田承嗣，途中作《太行苦热行》诗寄赠同院僚友，李涵有和作，独孤及、刘长卿又从而和之，诗中咏及本年河北战事。今李涵、吕渭诗均已佚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　少居洛阳。本年，其父吕渭由监察御史入京为殿中侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　本年前后，吕温从父学习《诗》、《礼》。是年，弟吕恭生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=778')">778年</a>　少居洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　少居洛阳。本年，其父吕渭经由宰相崔祐甫上奏，迁司门员外郎，寻为谏议大夫崔河图弹劾，贬歙州司马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年</a>　少居洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　少居洛阳。本年，其父吕渭入淮南节度使陈少游幕，为节度使参谋。不久又为检校吏部员外郎，充观察判官，改吏部郎中兼侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=783')">782-783年</a>　少居洛阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=784&endYear=784')">784年</a>　少居洛阳。是年前后，吕温跟随族兄皋学习《春秋》及三传。作品：《与族兄皋请学春秋书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第23页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与族兄皋请学春秋书</a><span class='authorDate'>（784年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371909")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371909'>儒风不振久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371909_comment'></div>某生于百代之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371909_comment'></div>不顾昧劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371909_comment'></div>凛然有志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371909_comment'></div>翘企圣域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371909_comment'></div>莫知所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371909_comment'></div>如仰高山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371909_comment'></div>临大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371909_comment'></div>未获<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1371909", 1371909, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>梯航</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371909_comment'></div>而欲济乎深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371909_comment'></div>臻乎极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371909_comment'></div>凡学之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371909_comment'></div>严师为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371909_comment'></div>师资道丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371909_comment'></div>八百年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371909_comment'></div>自凤鸟不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371909_comment'></div>麒麟遇获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371909_comment'></div>血流战国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371909_comment'></div>火发暴秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371909_comment'></div>先王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371909_comment'></div>几陨于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371909_comment'></div>赖汉氏勃焉而拯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371909_comment'></div>酾糟粕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371909_comment'></div>扬煨烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371909_comment'></div>披云雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371909_comment'></div>揭日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371909_comment'></div>夫子文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371909_comment'></div>灭而复耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371909_comment'></div>与火德俱朗者四百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371909_comment'></div>当时大教中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371909_comment'></div>去圣未远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371909_comment'></div>学士非师说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371909_comment'></div>不敢辄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371909_comment'></div>鸿儒硕生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371909_comment'></div>乐以善诱宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371909_comment'></div>虽为公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371909_comment'></div>教授不辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371909_comment'></div>其徒大者至千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371909_comment'></div>小者亦数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371909_comment'></div>或升乎堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371909_comment'></div>或入于室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371909_comment'></div>洋洋济济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371909_comment'></div>有古风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371909_comment'></div>夫学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371909_comment'></div>岂徒受章句而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371909_comment'></div>盖必求所以化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371909_comment'></div>日日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371909_comment'></div>又日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371909_comment'></div>以至乎终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371909_comment'></div>夫教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371909_comment'></div>岂徒博文字而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371909_comment'></div>盖必本之以忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371909_comment'></div>申之以礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371909_comment'></div>敦之以信让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371909_comment'></div>激之以廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371909_comment'></div>过则匡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371909_comment'></div>失则更之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371909_comment'></div>如切如磋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371909_comment'></div>如琢如磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371909_comment'></div>以至乎无瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371909_comment'></div>故两汉多名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371909_comment'></div>谏诤之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371909_comment'></div>同乎三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371909_comment'></div>盖由其身受师保之教诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371909_comment'></div>朋友之箴诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371909_comment'></div>既知己之损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371909_comment'></div>不忍观人之成败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371909_comment'></div>魏晋之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371909_comment'></div>其风大坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371909_comment'></div>学者皆以不师为夭纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371909_comment'></div>独学为生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371909_comment'></div>译疏翻音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371909_comment'></div>执疑护失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371909_comment'></div>率乃私意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371909_comment'></div>攻乎异端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371909_comment'></div>以讽诵章句为精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371909_comment'></div>以穿凿文字为奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371909_comment'></div>至于圣贤之微旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371909_comment'></div>教化之大本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371909_comment'></div>人伦之纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371909_comment'></div>王道之根源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371909_comment'></div>则荡然莫知所措矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371909_comment'></div>其先进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371909_comment'></div>亦以教授为鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371909_comment'></div>公卿大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371909_comment'></div>耻为人师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371909_comment'></div>至使乡校之老人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371909_comment'></div>呼以先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371909_comment'></div>则勃然动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371909_comment'></div>痛乎风俗之移人也如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371909_comment'></div>是以今之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371909_comment'></div>事君者不谏诤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371909_comment'></div>与人交者无切磋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371909_comment'></div>盖由其身不受师保之教诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371909_comment'></div>朋友之箴规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371909_comment'></div>既不知已之损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371909_comment'></div>恶肯顾人之成败乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371909_comment'></div>而今而后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371909_comment'></div>乃知不师不友之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371909_comment'></div>不可与为政而论交矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371909_comment'></div>且不师者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371909_comment'></div>废学之渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371909_comment'></div>恐数百年后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371909_comment'></div>又不及于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371909_comment'></div>则我先师之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371909_comment'></div>其陨于深泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371909_comment'></div>是用终日不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371909_comment'></div>终夜不寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371909_comment'></div>驰古今而慷慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1371909_comment'></div>抱文籍而太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1371909_comment'></div>吾兄亦曾以是为念乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1371909_comment'></div>小子狂简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1371909_comment'></div>实有微志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1371909_comment'></div>蕴童蒙求我之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1371909_comment'></div>立朝闻夕死之誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1371909_comment'></div>所与者不唯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1371909", 1371909, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>鸿硕</span>之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1371909_comment'></div>博洽之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1371909_comment'></div>与我同志者则为吾师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1371909_comment'></div>与兄略言其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1371909_comment'></div>其所贵乎道者六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1371909_comment'></div>其诗书礼乐大易春秋欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1371909_comment'></div>人皆知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1371909_comment'></div>鄙尚或异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1371909_comment'></div>所曰礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1371909_comment'></div>非酌献酬酢之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1371909_comment'></div>周旋裼袭之容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1371909_comment'></div>必可以经乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1371909_comment'></div>运阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1371909_comment'></div>管人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1371909_comment'></div>措天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1371909_comment'></div>所曰乐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1371909_comment'></div>非缀兆屈伸之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1371909_comment'></div>铿锵鼓舞之节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1371909_comment'></div>必可以厚风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1371909_comment'></div>仁鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1371909_comment'></div>熙元精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1371909_comment'></div>茂万物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1371909_comment'></div>所曰易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1371909_comment'></div>非揲蓍演数之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1371909_comment'></div>画卦举繇之能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1371909_comment'></div>必可以正性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1371909_comment'></div>观化元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1371909_comment'></div>贯众妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1371909_comment'></div>贞夫一者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1371909_comment'></div>所曰书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1371909_comment'></div>非古今文字之舛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1371909_comment'></div>大小章句之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1371909_comment'></div>必可以辩帝王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1371909_comment'></div>稽道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1371909_comment'></div>补大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1371909_comment'></div>建皇极者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1371909_comment'></div>所曰诗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1371909_comment'></div>非山川风土之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1371909_comment'></div>草木鸟兽之名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1371909_comment'></div>必可以警暴虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1371909_comment'></div>刺淫昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1371909_comment'></div>全君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1371909_comment'></div>尽忠孝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1371909_comment'></div>所曰春秋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1371909_comment'></div>非战争攻伐之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1371909_comment'></div>聘享盟会之仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1371909_comment'></div>必可以尊天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1371909_comment'></div>讨诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1371909_comment'></div>正华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1371909_comment'></div>绳贼乱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1371909_comment'></div>某愿学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1371909_comment'></div>此外非圣人所论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1371909_comment'></div>不与于君臣父子之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1371909_comment'></div>虽欲博闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1371909_comment'></div>不敢学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1371909_comment'></div>吾兄达者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1371909_comment'></div>可不曰然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1371909_comment'></div>尝阅雅论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1371909_comment'></div>深于春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1371909_comment'></div>其间所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1371909_comment'></div>实曰渊正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1371909_comment'></div>窃不自揣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1371909_comment'></div>愿以春秋三传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1371909_comment'></div>执抠衣之礼于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1371909_comment'></div>童蒙求我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1371909_comment'></div>兄得辞乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1371909_comment'></div>朝闻夕死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1371909_comment'></div>某可逆乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1371909_comment'></div>无以流俗所轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1371909_comment'></div>而忽贤圣之所重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1371909_comment'></div>其馀五经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1371909_comment'></div>当今孰可为某师者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1371909_comment'></div>幸详鄙志而与择焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_192_1371909_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0e9e35e160ee44a58d33985e4a3c7d0a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e9e35e160ee44a58d33985e4a3c7d0a");'><span id='0e9e35e160ee44a58d33985e4a3c7d0a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>，21岁</div><div id='0e9e35e160ee44a58d33985e4a3c7d0a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>　继祖母祖，在洛与父一起守制。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='03ebe1b1adb946909e716626cb0df59a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("03ebe1b1adb946909e716626cb0df59a");'><span id='03ebe1b1adb946909e716626cb0df59a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>，23岁</div><div id='03ebe1b1adb946909e716626cb0df59a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在洛阳应河南府试，有限韵应试之作。作品：《黄龙负舟赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第2页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span>《白云起对中诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第3页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。据复旦大学2009年博士学位论文白盛友《吕温研究》后附《吕温年谱》，本年，弟吕让出生。）</span><div id='poem_1371861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄龙负舟赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以克已勤物大川效灵为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371861")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371861'>夏后氏奠山疏滞。拯溺开泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371861_comment'></div>元圭锡命。既成天下之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371861_comment'></div>黄龙发祥。始耀域中之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371861_comment'></div>当其驻轸江甸。𫇢舟洪川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371861_comment'></div>天行健而时有未济。地设险而瞻之在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371861_comment'></div>思利涉以抚俗。遂精诚而告虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371861_comment'></div>于是云气滃起。神光烂然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371861_comment'></div>奋角于勿用之窟。骧首于或跃之泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371861_comment'></div>安波澄澜。奉天意以禺若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371861_comment'></div>拖尾垂鬣。夹王舟而负焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371861_comment'></div>合灵符于百代。表圣运于千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371861_comment'></div>徒伟夫出无情。驰不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371861_comment'></div>如驱风雷。若有羽翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371861_comment'></div>观竭诚以效用。似就列而陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371861_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1371861", 1371861, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>电目</span>流光。金鳞耀色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371861_comment'></div>天吴奔走。阳侯屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371861_comment'></div>巨险汔济。孰假剡木之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371861_comment'></div>潜怪莫逢。宁资画鹢之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371861_comment'></div>应变化以昭盛。出沈潜而刚克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371861_comment'></div>其庆惟大。赖祉福者兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371861_comment'></div>其观惟荣。执玉帛者万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371861_comment'></div>若非平土堙水。泣辜罪已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371861_comment'></div>菲饮食以昭俭。卑宫室而思理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371861_comment'></div>德掩乎生成之初。功齐乎开辟之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371861_comment'></div>安有非常之神物。不召而萃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371861_comment'></div>济其不通。而彰其具美者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371861_comment'></div>至若汉横汾水。秦抵沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371861_comment'></div>实逞心欲。匪崇德馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371861_comment'></div>苍生之虚瘁靡念。方士之空言是听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371861_comment'></div>始幸免于覆溺。夫何望乎炳灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371861_comment'></div>于戏。动罔轨模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371861_comment'></div>言非善教。则人虽愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371861_comment'></div>或使之而不效。其志惟纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371861_comment'></div>其德孔殷。则龙虽神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371861_comment'></div>将不役而自勤。信矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371861_comment'></div>国家俾人其苏。在理无郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371861_comment'></div>超乎大禹。不务舟车之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371861_comment'></div>蜿彼黄龙。但为宫沼之物而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371861_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1371861_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_18470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白云起封中诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（题中用韵，六十字成。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18470")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_18470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18470'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18470'>封开白云起，汉帝坐斋宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18470'>望在泥金上，疑生秘玉中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18470'>攒柯初缭绕，布叶渐蒙笼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18470'>日观祥光合，天门瑞气通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18470'>无心已出岫，有势欲凌风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18470'>倘遣成膏泽，从兹遍大空。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18470'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_18470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在洛阳应河南府试，以第一名举送。作品：《河南府试赎帖赋得乡饮酒》<span class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河南府试赎帖赋得乡饮酒诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18448")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18448_comment'></div><div id='poem_allusion_18448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18448'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18448'>酌言修旧典，刈楚始登堂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18448'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_18448", 18448, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>百拜</span>宾仪尽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_18448", 18448, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>三终</span>乐奏长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18448'>想同<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1728, "poem_sentence_2_18448")'>莺出谷</span>，看似雁成行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18448'>礼罢知何适，随云入帝乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18448'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18448_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_18460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赋得失群鹤</a><span class='authorDate'>（794年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18460")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18460_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_18460'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_0_18460'>杳杳冲天鹤，风排势暂违。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18460'>有心长自负，无伴可相依。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18460'>万里宁辞远，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(125, "poem_sentence_2_18460")'>三山</span>讵忆归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18460'>但令毛羽在，何处不翻飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18460'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18460_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d778ed060dff46beb312e11d03fefff5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d778ed060dff46beb312e11d03fefff5");'><span id='d778ed060dff46beb312e11d03fefff5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>，25岁</div><div id='d778ed060dff46beb312e11d03fefff5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>　再次出关至洛阳，投卷河南尹齐抗，并呈书启。作品：《上族叔齐河南书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第25页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上族叔齐河南书</a><span class='authorDate'>（796年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371908")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371908'>大尹叔父閤下。某闻水官修而龙至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371908_comment'></div>官失其方。物乃坻伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371908_comment'></div>以文章而言。则先进为后进之官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371908_comment'></div>亦宜正褒贬。别雅郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371908_comment'></div>宣六义。合三变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371908_comment'></div>以修其官。使后进之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371908_comment'></div>靡然向风。皦然知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371908_comment'></div>能者劝。不能者止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371908_comment'></div>于是乎文章之可见也。如扫除氛昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371908_comment'></div>澄定波涛。穹天清而日月耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371908_comment'></div>沧海晏而蓬壶出。今夫先进之废官久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371908_comment'></div>文犹龙也。其可见乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371908_comment'></div>伏惟叔父蕴特进之明。哀雅颂之缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371908_comment'></div>常欲以三代制度训斯文。前罢镇南服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371908_comment'></div>入侍东掖。词林耸仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371908_comment'></div>如日登观。莫不结辙连驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371908_comment'></div>怀编捧轴。差池道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371908_comment'></div>奔走光尘。人人自以为齐公之遇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371908_comment'></div>及乎昌言金马。高议承明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371908_comment'></div>悬大雅之衡。以权后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371908_comment'></div>则乃以小子为称首。达勾萌而茂以柯叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371908_comment'></div>翼雏●8766而使之颉颃。先达改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371908_comment'></div>同类骇听。誉动朝端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371908_comment'></div>声驰毂下。循顾反覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371908_comment'></div>诚非所堪。窃料叔父之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371908_comment'></div>岂不欲使滥音窃吹者。闻士会而西逃秦境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371908_comment'></div>敦行守正者。望郭隗而北首燕路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371908_comment'></div>夫如是。则小子敢贺天下文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371908_comment'></div>废而复兴。不敢自当其遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371908_comment'></div>然大匠虽哲。不能化拥肿之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371908_comment'></div>大风虽壮。不能起凝滞之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371908_comment'></div>曩充乡赋。荐辱公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371908_comment'></div>昨诏贤良。猥尘清举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371908_comment'></div>叔父以唱高寡和。小子以名浮易丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371908_comment'></div>间关堙郁。卒用无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371908_comment'></div>取笑薄徒。贻羞左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371908_comment'></div>虽失鹄而知反。终胡颜而敢安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371908_comment'></div>愧惧惭惶。夙夜若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371908_comment'></div>叔父蹈中庸之德。遭兼济之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371908_comment'></div>荷深知于明主。悬大望于苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371908_comment'></div>一朝秉唐之钧。埏埴万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371908_comment'></div>而高明不夺于独见。鄙分克彰于日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371908_comment'></div>茫茫前途。未敢自料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371908_comment'></div>岂遽以一第为得丧哉。由是思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371908_comment'></div>勃焉增气。遂欲摄迹声利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371908_comment'></div>潜心道艺。穷六籍之统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371908_comment'></div>尽三变之形容。使学通天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371908_comment'></div>文正雅俗。然后抗衡当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371908_comment'></div>为叔父之荣。虽知其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371908_comment'></div>志不可夺。谨献近文七首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371908_comment'></div>徒跂圣人之域。未臻作者之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371908_comment'></div>姑务自强。式酬与进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371908_comment'></div>伏愿特纡省览。光赐教诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371908_comment'></div>指以远踪。责以大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371908_comment'></div>惠何加焉。非敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371908_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1371908_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a20025bf39e6482e979a0cb7603c4584_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a20025bf39e6482e979a0cb7603c4584");'><span id='a20025bf39e6482e979a0cb7603c4584_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>，27岁</div><div id='a20025bf39e6482e979a0cb7603c4584' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　在洛阳，见上官婉儿手迹，感而作歌咏叹之。作品：《上官昭容书楼歌》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第18页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上官昭容书楼歌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18477")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18477_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_18477_0'>① 贞元十四年，友人崔仁亮于东都买得《研神记》一卷，有昭容列名书缝处，因用感叹而作是歌。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18477'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18477'>汉家婕妤唐昭容，工诗能赋千载同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18477'>自言才艺是天真，不服丈夫胜妇人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18477'>歌阑舞罢闲无事，纵恣优游弄文字。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18477'>玉楼宝架中天居，缄奇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_18477", 18477, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>秘异</span>万卷馀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18477'>水精编帙录钿轴，云母捣纸黄金书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18477'>风吹<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作飘）</span>花露清旭时，绮窗高挂红绡帷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18477'>香囊盛烟绣结络，翠羽拂案青<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作碧）</span>琉璃。<div id='poem_sentence_6_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_18477'>吟披啸卷终<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作纷）</span>无已，皎皎渊机破<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作碎）</span>研理。<div id='poem_sentence_7_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_18477'>词萦彩翰紫鸾回，思耿寥天碧云起。<div id='poem_sentence_8_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_18477'>碧云起，心悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_18477'>境深转苦坐自摧<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作催）</span>，金<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作王）</span>梯珠履声一断。<div id='poem_sentence_10_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_18477'>瑶阶日夜生青苔，青苔秘空<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作闭九）</span>关。<div id='poem_sentence_11_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_18477'>曾比群玉山，神仙杳何许。<div id='poem_sentence_12_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_18477'>遗逸满人间，君不见洛阳南市卖书肆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_18477'>有人买得研神记，纸上香多蠹不成。<div id='poem_sentence_14_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_18477'>昭容题处犹分明，令人惆怅难为情。<div id='poem_sentence_15_18477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_18477'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_18477_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1da69c5921504ea9a20c4e447dedcc6f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1da69c5921504ea9a20c4e447dedcc6f");'><span id='1da69c5921504ea9a20c4e447dedcc6f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=802')">800-802年</a>，29-31岁</div><div id='1da69c5921504ea9a20c4e447dedcc6f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年12月</a>　十二月，与弟吕恭护送父母灵柩归袝于洛阳邙山清风原之大茔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　在洛阳居丧守制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　为母作墓志铭。作品：《东平吕府君河东郡君柳氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷7第79页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　为父作墓志铭。作品：《吕府君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此文。）</span><div id='poem_1371960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故唐太子舍人李府君夫人荥阳郑氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371960")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371960'>夫人讳字荥阳人。郑于姬姓最亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371960_comment'></div>为天下著族。自秦汉至于皇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371960_comment'></div>萎蕤轩冕。耿曜图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371960_comment'></div>如洪河东导江汉。其源流不待问而可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371960_comment'></div>高祖守元。朝散大夫袭丹徒公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371960_comment'></div>曾祖嘉会。朝散大夫雅州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371960_comment'></div>大父曔。正议大夫金衢二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371960_comment'></div>严考钦英。朝议郎杭州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371960_comment'></div>皆以天爵。屈于人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371960_comment'></div>滋庆羡美。实生夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371960_comment'></div>夫人始生。辨物而智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371960_comment'></div>能言而信。既笄而知礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371960_comment'></div>有行而制义。性与天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371960_comment'></div>质无表饰。冲灵虚寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371960_comment'></div>和气交畅。不严厉而妇道自著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371960_comment'></div>不整峻而母仪有俨。实柔德之黄中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371960_comment'></div>壸闱之尽善者。中舍府君出自我睿宗让皇帝之孙汉中王之予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371960_comment'></div>乃于钟鼎宝玉之间杰立。雅尚文学政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371960_comment'></div>龟龙搢绅。而夫人躬蘋藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371960_comment'></div>服浣濯。去华斲雕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371960_comment'></div>激清守素。辅佐将顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371960_comment'></div>实有力焉。昼哭之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371960_comment'></div>训成诸子。长曰景俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371960_comment'></div>负王佐之才。探圣人之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371960_comment'></div>磅礡秀气。拔乎其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371960_comment'></div>次曰景儒景信景仁。皆文敏絜修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371960_comment'></div>保家良主。有以见夫人明裕善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371960_comment'></div>继成义方。宜其及公侯必复之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371960_comment'></div>享春秋以贵之庆。闻天子叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371960_comment'></div>见公卿升堂。而时命不偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371960_comment'></div>与善茫昧。景俭有捧檄之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371960_comment'></div>夫人从养于越州。以贞元十九年终于官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371960_comment'></div>降生五十有四。景俭等以某年十一月一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371960_comment'></div>号奉裳帷。祔于京兆富平县万寿原之旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371960_comment'></div>从周礼也。以某辱久要之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371960_comment'></div>俾稽懿实。敬为铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371960_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1371960'>周受成命。郑为戚藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371960_comment'></div>以国命氏。郁闻德门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371960_comment'></div>缁衣垂芳。荥波发源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371960_comment'></div>为为梓。为兰为荪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371960_comment'></div>梓惟何。卿材克绍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371960_comment'></div>兰荪惟何。女德之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371960_comment'></div>抑抑夫人。自他有耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371960_comment'></div>玉度旁达。泉心内照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371960_comment'></div>和顺积中。高明有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371960_comment'></div>辅佐君子。与道始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371960_comment'></div>族姻成化。慈俭为宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371960_comment'></div>让帝之后。门生素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371960_comment'></div>宜及子贵。以荣教义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371960_comment'></div>如何高堂。奄忽违弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371960_comment'></div>万岁原上。松楸永秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371960_comment'></div>惟命罕言。德音无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371960_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1371960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=802')">801-802年</a>　在洛阳居丧守制。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a39eee58eac4ba5938c08bbb36ef1e8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a39eee58eac4ba5938c08bbb36ef1e8");'><span id='4a39eee58eac4ba5938c08bbb36ef1e8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=789')">785-789年</a>，14-18岁</div><div id='4a39eee58eac4ba5938c08bbb36ef1e8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年</a>　寓居广陵。是年或稍后，与友人薛大信一同就读于灵岩寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=786&endYear=786')">786年</a>　寓居广陵，与元洪讨论《春秋》大义。其父吕渭在舒州刺史任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=787&endYear=787')">787年</a>　仍留居扬州学习。其父吕渭至京赴吏部员外郎任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=788&endYear=788')">788年</a>　在扬州与摇兼济、李该游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=789&endYear=789')">789年</a>　在扬州，有文。作品：《地志图序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第29页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。是年八月吕温从广陵回长安前作，姑系此年。）</span>《汉舆地图序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此诗。是年八月吕温从广陵回长安前作，姑系此年。）</span><div id='poem_1371912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>地志图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（789年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371912")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371912'>广陵李该。博达之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371912_comment'></div>学无不通。尤好地理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371912_comment'></div>患其书多门。历世浸广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371912_comment'></div>文词浩荡。学者疲老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371912_comment'></div>由是以独见之明。法先圣之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371912_comment'></div>黜诸子之传记。述仲尼之职方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371912_comment'></div>会源流。考同异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371912_comment'></div>务该畅。从体要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371912_comment'></div>倬然勒成一家之说。犹惧其奥未足以昭启后生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371912_comment'></div>乃裂素为方仪。据书而图画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371912_comment'></div>随方面以区别。拟形容而训解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371912_comment'></div>命之曰地志图。观其粉散百川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371912_comment'></div>黛凝群山。元气剖判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371912_comment'></div>成乎笔端。任土之毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371912_comment'></div>有生之类。大钧变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371912_comment'></div>不出其意。然后列以城郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371912_comment'></div>罗乎陬落。内自五侯九伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371912_comment'></div>外洎要荒蛮貊。禹迹之所穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371912_comment'></div>汉驿之所通。五色相宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371912_comment'></div>万邦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1371912", 1371912, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>错峙</span>。毫釐之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371912_comment'></div>而下正乎封略。方寸之界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371912_comment'></div>而上当乎分野。乾象坤势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371912_comment'></div>炳焉可观。与夫聚米拟其端倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371912_comment'></div>画地陈乎梗槩。固不可同年而语其详略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371912_comment'></div>每虚室燕居。薄帷晴褰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371912_comment'></div>普天之下。尽在屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371912_comment'></div>户纳四海。窗笼八极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371912_comment'></div>名山大川。随顾奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371912_comment'></div>殊方绝域。举意而到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371912_comment'></div>高视华裔。坐横古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371912_comment'></div>观帝王之疆理。见宇宙之寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371912_comment'></div>出遐入幽。曾不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371912_comment'></div>与夫役形神于岁月。穷辙迹于区外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371912_comment'></div>又不可并轨而论劳逸也。且夫删百代之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371912_comment'></div>综群言之首。繁而不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371912_comment'></div>疏而不漏。才识以润之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371912_comment'></div>丹青以炳之。使嗜学之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371912_comment'></div>未披文而见义。不由户而观奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371912_comment'></div>斯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1371912", 1371912, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>训导</span>之明也。穷地而述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371912_comment'></div>举世而载。事极鸿纤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371912_comment'></div>理通皦昧。混一家之文轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371912_comment'></div>张大国之襟带。覈人物之虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371912_comment'></div>总山川之要会。表皇威之有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371912_comment'></div>明王道之无外。斯乃功用之大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371912_comment'></div>见苍梧涂山。则思舜禹恤民之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371912_comment'></div>睹穷边大漠。则悟秦汉劳师之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371912_comment'></div>览齐墟晋壤。则见桓文勤王之霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371912_comment'></div>观洞庭荆门。则知苗蜀恃险之败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371912_comment'></div>王者于是明乎得失。诸侯于是鉴于兴替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371912_comment'></div>斯又惩劝之远也。然则本之所以广学流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371912_comment'></div>申之足以赞鸿业。垂之可以示后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371912_comment'></div>岂徒由近观远。以智自乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371912_comment'></div>为室中之一物哉。而时无知音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371912_comment'></div>道不虚行。举地成图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371912_comment'></div>闻天无路。此志士儒林所以为之叹息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371912_comment'></div>某久从君游。辱命序述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371912_comment'></div>庶明作者之意。俾好事君子知其所以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371912_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1371912_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1275504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1275504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1275504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉舆地图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（789年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1275504")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1275504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1275504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1275504'>舆地之有图，古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1275504_comment'></div>自成周大司徒掌天下土地之图，以周知广轮之数，而职方氏之图复加详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1275504_comment'></div>迨汉灭秦，萧何先收其图书，始具知天下阸塞户口多少之差，然则尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1275504_comment'></div>武帝元狩六年，将立三子为王，御史大夫奏舆地图，请所立国名，乃开齐、燕、广陵之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1275504_comment'></div>舆地图之名，至是始见，史迁之所载可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1275504_comment'></div>光武皇帝之徇河北，邓禹杖策而从之，说以大策，有「天下不足定」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1275504_comment'></div>其后帝登城楼，披舆地图指示禹曰：「天下郡国如是，今始乃得其一，子前言天下不足定，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1275504_comment'></div>禹复申其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1275504_comment'></div>盖光武志在天下，当神州赤县未入经略之际，其君臣更相激厉如此，故能兼制六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1275504_comment'></div>司空之所掌，无寸地尺天不归于封域，按图分封，并建诸子，以为藩屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1275504_comment'></div>呜呼盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1275504_comment'></div>用敢䌷绎其意而为之序曰：自古合天下于一者，必以拨乱之志为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1275504_comment'></div>志之所向，可以排山岳，倒江海，开金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1275504_comment'></div>一念之烈，无能御之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1275504_comment'></div>光武之在河北，崎岖于封豕长蛇之间，瞋目裂眦，更相长雄，积甲成山，积血成川，积气成云，积声成雷，九流浑淆，三纲反易，虽十家之市无宁居者，则光武果何所恃哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1275504_comment'></div>亦恃其拨乱之志而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1275504_comment'></div>光武之志，以皇天全付所覆于我有汉，今乃瓜分幅裂，沦于盗贼，此子孙之责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1275504_comment'></div>责之所在，虽有登天之难不敢辞，虽有暴虎之厄不敢避，虽有蹈水火之危不敢回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1275504_comment'></div>奋然直前，以偿吾祖宗之所负，必使吾祖宗之旧物咸复其初，然后吾责始塞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1275504_comment'></div>此志一立，故虽处一郡之地，而视天下之广，皆吾囊中物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1275504_comment'></div>蚤夜以谋之，反复以思之，其披舆地图之际，慷慨愤悱，气干云霄，拨乱之志，盖肇于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1275504_comment'></div>方其志之未立，则一郡至小，而群贼之地奚翅十倍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1275504_comment'></div>吾众至少而群贼之兵奚翅十倍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1275504_comment'></div>恢复之功，犹捕风系影，若不可期者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1275504_comment'></div>及既有其志，则规模先定，机谋先立，兆之于前而必之于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1275504_comment'></div>若青若齐，若陇若蜀，若楚若越，皆吾志中之一物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1275504_comment'></div>若盆子，若王昌，若嚣若述，若步若丰，皆吾志中之臣仆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1275504_comment'></div>彼方缮塞置戍而不知吾已破之于堂上，彼方峨冠被衮而不知吾已缚之于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1275504_comment'></div>是以论光武克复郡县之迹，则有难易焉，有先后焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1275504_comment'></div>若夫光武恢复之志则一，披舆地图而三万里之幅员皆入于灵府，岂尝得一邑而始思得一州，得一州而始思得一部哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1275504_comment'></div>大矣，光武之志也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1275504_comment'></div>斯其所以祀汉配天，不失旧物欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1275504_comment'></div>厥后建武二十二年，匈奴右薁鞬日逐王比遣使奉匈奴地图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1275504_comment'></div>二十四年，比款五原塞愿为藩蔽，乃立之为南单于，俾预藩臣之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1275504_comment'></div>是知光武有一天下之志，非特舆地图之所纪皆为臣妾，而匈奴地图之所纪亦为臣妾焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1275504_comment'></div>则志也者，其拨乱济世之枢极欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1275504_comment'></div>故述之以告来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1275504_comment'></div>谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1275504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=789&endYear=789')">789年8月</a>　八月，从广陵赴京师长安，经广陵郡六合县棠邑乡，为处士陈融作墓表。作品：《广陵陈先生墓表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷7第81页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广陵陈先生墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（789年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371957")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371957'>有唐贞晦先生广陵郡棠邑乡陈君曰融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371957_comment'></div>无字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371957_comment'></div>享年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371957_comment'></div>游不出乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371957_comment'></div>考终厥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371957_comment'></div>呜呼至哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371957_comment'></div>良玉虽白不受采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371957_comment'></div>醴泉自甘非有和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371957_comment'></div>真色缜密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371957_comment'></div>丹青无自入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371957_comment'></div>灵味天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371957_comment'></div>曲糵无所资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371957_comment'></div>故先生长而不学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371957_comment'></div>大朴不通乎轮辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371957_comment'></div>至音不谐乎宫商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371957_comment'></div>曲直浑成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371957_comment'></div>巧匠莫能材也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371957_comment'></div>清浊一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371957_comment'></div>伶伦莫能器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371957_comment'></div>故先生老而不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371957_comment'></div>地虚而践则有迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371957_comment'></div>器疏而扣则成声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371957_comment'></div>我践惟实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371957_comment'></div>迹不可得而见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371957_comment'></div>我扣惟密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371957_comment'></div>声不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371957_comment'></div>故先生没而不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371957_comment'></div>若夫为养克孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371957_comment'></div>居丧致毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371957_comment'></div>事亡如存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371957_comment'></div>朋友孜孜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371957_comment'></div>兄弟怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371957_comment'></div>于乡恂恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371957_comment'></div>与物熙熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371957_comment'></div>天性人道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371957_comment'></div>其尽于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371957_comment'></div>何必读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371957_comment'></div>然后为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371957_comment'></div>知命是达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371957_comment'></div>怡神为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371957_comment'></div>乐天忘忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371957_comment'></div>自宠不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371957_comment'></div>贵我以道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371957_comment'></div>此非爵乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371957_comment'></div>富我以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371957_comment'></div>此非禄乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371957_comment'></div>何必入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371957_comment'></div>然后为仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371957_comment'></div>我有信顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371957_comment'></div>自天祐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371957_comment'></div>我有正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371957_comment'></div>神之听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371957_comment'></div>谓天盖高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371957_comment'></div>亦既知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371957_comment'></div>谓神盖幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371957_comment'></div>亦既闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371957_comment'></div>何必俗声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371957_comment'></div>然后为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371957_comment'></div>大哉先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371957_comment'></div>行不学之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371957_comment'></div>据不仕之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371957_comment'></div>负不称之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371957_comment'></div>达人观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371957_comment'></div>斯亦极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371957_comment'></div>子贞元初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371957_comment'></div>寓居是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371957_comment'></div>言归京国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371957_comment'></div>道出其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371957_comment'></div>始见一乡之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371957_comment'></div>父义子孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371957_comment'></div>长惠幼敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371957_comment'></div>见乎词气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371957_comment'></div>发乎颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371957_comment'></div>不闻忿争之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371957_comment'></div>不见傲慢之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371957_comment'></div>雍雍穆穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371957_comment'></div>甚足异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371957_comment'></div>因揣之而叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371957_comment'></div>芳兰所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371957_comment'></div>其草皆香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371957_comment'></div>美玉所积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371957_comment'></div>其山有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371957_comment'></div>此乡之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371957_comment'></div>岂必尽仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371957_comment'></div>其必有贤者生于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371957_comment'></div>遂停车累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371957_comment'></div>周访故老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371957_comment'></div>果曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371957_comment'></div>吾里尝有陈融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371957_comment'></div>孝慈仁信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371957_comment'></div>不学不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371957_comment'></div>乡人见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371957_comment'></div>皆自欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1371957", 1371957, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>迁善远罪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371957_comment'></div>亦不知其所以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371957_comment'></div>今也则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371957_comment'></div>清风犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371957_comment'></div>予于是慨然痛先生以纯德至行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371957_comment'></div>沉落光耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371957_comment'></div>官阙轼庐之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371957_comment'></div>士无表墓之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371957_comment'></div>知而不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371957_comment'></div>我执其咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371957_comment'></div>乃披典校德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371957_comment'></div>谥曰贞晦先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371957_comment'></div>穷徵其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371957_comment'></div>建石于路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371957_comment'></div>用告将来之有识者云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1371957_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=789&endYear=789')">789年8月</a>　八月，从广陵赴长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=790')">790年</a>　居长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>　本年前后，师陆质学《春秋》，从梁肃学文章。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>　秋，与友人游少陵原，感叹作诗。作品：《登少陵原望秦中诸川太原王至德妙有水术因用感叹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第12页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。复旦大学2009年博士学位论文白盛友《吕温研究》后附《吕温年谱》系此诗于贞元十七年。）</span><div id='poem_18495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登少陵原望秦中诸川太原王至德妙用<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本无用字）</span>有水术因用感叹</a><span class='authorDate'>（791年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18495")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18495_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_18495'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(43, "poem_allusion_18495")'>哭途穷</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6699, "poem_allusion_18495")'>平水土</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_18495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18495'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18495'>少陵最高处，旷望极秋空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18495'>君山喷清源，脉散秦川中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18495'>荷锸自<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作动）</span>成<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作成云）</span>雨，由来非鬼工。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18495'>如何盛明代，委弃伤豳风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18495'>泾灞徒络绎，漆沮虚会同。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18495'>东流滔滔去，沃野飞秋蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18495'>大禹<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6699, "poem_sentence_6_18495")'>平水土</span>，吾人得其宗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_18495'>发机回地势，运思与天通。<div id='poem_sentence_7_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_18495'>早欲献奇策，丰财叙西戎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_18495'>岂知年三十，未识大明宫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_18495'>卷尔出岫云，追吾入冥鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_18495'>无为学惊俗，狂醉<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(43, "poem_sentence_11_18495")'>哭途穷</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_18495_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_18495'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年</a>　服丧期满。吕渭除太子右庶子，加通议大夫。吕温亦返长安。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6ed01e2a7abb43ed9cd79f19b685042c_label'><a href='javascript:
