ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=795')">794-795年</a>，23-24岁</div><div id='6ed01e2a7abb43ed9cd79f19b685042c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年10月</a>　十月，赴长安举贤良方正制举，被黜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>　在长安与至源、王玄运游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　其父吕渭以礼部侍郎知贡举，作为主司直系亲属，吕温照制应“别头试”，然落第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　在长安，有限韵之律赋。作品：《管窥豹赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此诗。姑系此年。）</span>《乐出虚赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此诗。故系此年。）</span><div id='poem_1371867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>管窥豹赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以管中窥豹时见一班为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371867")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371867'>管实圆通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371867_comment'></div>豹称奇质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371867_comment'></div>将窃窥以无视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371867_comment'></div>果遇文而得一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371867_comment'></div>言如立信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371867_comment'></div>初云必有可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371867_comment'></div>美在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371867_comment'></div>终荷守而勿失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371867_comment'></div>奚执虚而莫见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371867_comment'></div>谅衡空而有窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371867_comment'></div>注目每思夫破竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371867_comment'></div>专心常切于主皮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371867_comment'></div>故得精神靡怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371867_comment'></div>盼睐无亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371867_comment'></div>辨或未分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371867_comment'></div>岂敢因小人所视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371867_comment'></div>言如有准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371867_comment'></div>安得谓童子何知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371867_comment'></div>事不可轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371867_comment'></div>智难相短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371867_comment'></div>瞻夫隐雾之兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371867_comment'></div>乃用窥天之管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371867_comment'></div>岂文质之不伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371867_comment'></div>独孤明之所满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371867_comment'></div>分形既内识规规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371867_comment'></div>视远惟中央坦坦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371867_comment'></div>然后知虚心可达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371867_comment'></div>小智攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371867_comment'></div>毫釐必远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371867_comment'></div>长短皆通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371867_comment'></div>投迹傥遇于东周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371867_comment'></div>孰辨犬羊之鞟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371867_comment'></div>有文而比夫西伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371867_comment'></div>岂殊缧绁之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371867_comment'></div>是谓祈进奚为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371867_comment'></div>求知不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371867_comment'></div>将希国士之察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371867_comment'></div>用当君子之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371867_comment'></div>罗因一目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371867_comment'></div>期所视之无偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371867_comment'></div>利绝一源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371867_comment'></div>专向明之独见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371867_comment'></div>乃知蔚文者道不足攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371867_comment'></div>俯视者智或防闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371867_comment'></div>何微明之有辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371867_comment'></div>果偶中之无难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371867_comment'></div>谓容止可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371867_comment'></div>且殊窒隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371867_comment'></div>同邂逅相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371867_comment'></div>更喜通班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371867_comment'></div>信专美之独嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371867_comment'></div>谅生知而何教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371867_comment'></div>流睇已假夫观止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371867_comment'></div>审像乃知其是效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371867_comment'></div>十年之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371867_comment'></div>自分西晋之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371867_comment'></div>一管之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371867_comment'></div>更识南山之豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371867_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371867_comment'></div>则履中不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371867_comment'></div>应手无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371867_comment'></div>冀觊觎之有以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371867_comment'></div>得专精而所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371867_comment'></div>亦何必誇久视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371867_comment'></div>骋一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371867_comment'></div>然后知求仁之可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371867_comment'></div>惟智者之念兹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1371867_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐出虚赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以声从响际出自虚中为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371864")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371864'>和而出者乐之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371864_comment'></div>虚而应者物之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371864_comment'></div>或洞尔以形受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371864_comment'></div>乃泠然而韵生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371864_comment'></div>去默归喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371864_comment'></div>始兆成文之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371864_comment'></div>从无入有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371864_comment'></div>方为饰喜之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371864_comment'></div>其始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371864_comment'></div>因妙有而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371864_comment'></div>向无间而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371864_comment'></div>披洪纤清浊之响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371864_comment'></div>满丝竹陶匏之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371864_comment'></div>根乎寂寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371864_comment'></div>故难辨于将萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371864_comment'></div>率尔熙熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371864_comment'></div>亦不知其所自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371864_comment'></div>故圣人取象于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371864_comment'></div>观民以风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371864_comment'></div>辟嗜欲之由塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371864_comment'></div>决形神之未通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371864_comment'></div>欲使和气潜作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371864_comment'></div>元关暗空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371864_comment'></div>与吹万而皆唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371864_comment'></div>起生三而尽同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371864_comment'></div>自我及人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371864_comment'></div>托物于未分之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371864_comment'></div>蟠天极地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371864_comment'></div>开机于方寸之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371864_comment'></div>于是澹以无倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371864_comment'></div>留而不滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371864_comment'></div>有非象之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371864_comment'></div>生无际之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371864_comment'></div>是故实其想而道升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371864_comment'></div>窒其空而声蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371864_comment'></div>洞乎内而笙竽作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371864_comment'></div>刳其中而琴瑟制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371864_comment'></div>波腾悦豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371864_comment'></div>风行于有道之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371864_comment'></div>派别商宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371864_comment'></div>雷动于无为之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371864_comment'></div>杳杳徐徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371864_comment'></div>周流六虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371864_comment'></div>信阗尔于始寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371864_comment'></div>乃哗然而戒初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371864_comment'></div>铿锵于百姓之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371864_comment'></div>于斯已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371864_comment'></div>鼓舞于一人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371864_comment'></div>知彼何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371864_comment'></div>是则垂其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371864_comment'></div>有其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371864_comment'></div>乐因之祖述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371864_comment'></div>究其形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371864_comment'></div>实其质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371864_comment'></div>声因之洞出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371864_comment'></div>理在无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371864_comment'></div>情归得一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371864_comment'></div>塞云谷而响绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371864_comment'></div>疏天籁而音逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371864_comment'></div>未随于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371864_comment'></div>絪缊乎七政八风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371864_comment'></div>忽变其和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371864_comment'></div>剖判于五声六律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371864_comment'></div>由是迁为草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371864_comment'></div>散作笙镛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371864_comment'></div>群分自此而焱起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371864_comment'></div>九奏因之而景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371864_comment'></div>道薄风漓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371864_comment'></div>莫究箫韶之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371864_comment'></div>声消韵息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371864_comment'></div>空传干戚之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371864_comment'></div>今则素扆垂休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371864_comment'></div>清悬继响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371864_comment'></div>平心已立于皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371864_comment'></div>率舞犹虚于睿想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371864_comment'></div>如是则薰然泄泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371864_comment'></div>将生于象罔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_76_1371864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年8月</a>　八月，在京送薛大信归乡，作序文。作品：《送薛大信归临晋序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第31页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送薛大信归临晋序</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371910")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371910'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371910'>先师曰。益者三友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371910_comment'></div>吾能得之。岂惟直谅多闻而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371910_comment'></div>可以旁魄天人。谈尧舜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371910_comment'></div>则有吾族兄皋。可以根本性情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371910_comment'></div>语颜夷之行。则有太原王师简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371910_comment'></div>可以发扬古训。论三代之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371910_comment'></div>则有河东薛大信。此三君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371910_comment'></div>或道以乐我。或行以约我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371910_comment'></div>或文以博我。遭时则有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371910_comment'></div>遁世则无闷。其为益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371910_comment'></div>不亦大乎。大信与予最旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371910_comment'></div>始以孝弟馀力。皆学于广陵之灵岩寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371910_comment'></div>云卷其身。讨论数岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371910_comment'></div>常见大信述作。必根乎六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371910_comment'></div>取礼之简。乐之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371910_comment'></div>诗之比兴。书之典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371910_comment'></div>春秋之褒贬。大易之变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371910_comment'></div>错落混合。峥嵘特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371910_comment'></div>不离圣域。而逸轨绝尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371910_comment'></div>不易雅制。而瑰姿万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371910_comment'></div>有若云起日观。尽成丹霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371910_comment'></div>峰折灵掌。无非峻势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371910_comment'></div>皆天光朗映。秀气<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1371910", 1371910, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>孤拔</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371910_comment'></div>岂藻饰而削成者哉。圣上方欲观人之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371910_comment'></div>润色鸿业。秉笔者如三光得天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371910_comment'></div>每贺大信有其时矣。无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371910_comment'></div>予被乡曲之誉。赋于阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371910_comment'></div>以文乖时体。行失俗誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371910_comment'></div>再为有司所黜。此时大信亦与计偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371910_comment'></div>知机全高。匣刃不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371910_comment'></div>昔赵杀鸣犊。仲尼临河而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371910_comment'></div>予之见黜。子亦逡巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371910_comment'></div>事虽不同。其所感一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371910_comment'></div>岁八月。以岵屺之感告予于归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371910_comment'></div>予思古人有处有赠。乃语之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371910_comment'></div>吾闻贤者志其大者。文为道之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371910_comment'></div>道为文之本。专其饰则道丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371910_comment'></div>反其本则文存。且使不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371910_comment'></div>又何伤矣。彼邦是尧舜之遗俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371910_comment'></div>唐叔之所理。必有忠信如君者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371910_comment'></div>问安之暇。可与之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371910_comment'></div>琢磨仁义。浸润道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371910_comment'></div>考皇王治乱之迹。求圣哲行藏之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371910_comment'></div>达可以济乎天下。穷可以摅其光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371910_comment'></div>无为矻矻笔砚间也。行矣大信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371910_comment'></div>苟非同志。勿矢予言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371910_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1371910_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　本年前后，灵彻上人西游京师，吕渭与其游，作诗以赠。作品：《戏赠灵彻上人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第9页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏赠灵澈上人</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18408")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_18408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18408'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18408'>僧家亦有芳春兴，自是禅心<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作心源）</span>无滞境。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18408'>君看池水湛然时，何曾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作时）</span>不受花枝影。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18408'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_18408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　在京师与灵彻上人游，有序文。作品：《张荆州画赞并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷9第101页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张荆州画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371947")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371947_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371947'>中书令始兴文献公。有唐之鲠亮臣也。开元二十年后。玄宗春秋高矣。以太平自致。颇易天下。综覈稍怠。推纳寖广。君子小人。摩肩于朝。直声遂寝。邪气始胜。中兴之业衰焉。公于是以生人为身。社稷自任。抗危言而无所避。秉大节而不可夺。小必谏。大必诤。攀帝槛。历天阶。犯雷霆之威。不霁不止。日月之蚀。为公却明。虎而冠者。不敢猛视。群贤倚赖。天下仰息。凛乎千载之望矣。不虞天将启幽蓟之祸。俾奸臣负乘。以速致戎。诈成谗胜。圣不能保。褫我公衮。寘于侯服。身虽远而谏愈切。道既塞而诚弥坚。忧而不怨。终老南国。于戏。功业见乎变。而其变有二。在否则通。在泰则穷。开元初。天子新出艰难。久愤荒政。乐与群下励精致理。于是乎有否极之变。姚宋坐而乘之。举为时要。动中上急。天光照身。宇宙在手。势若舟楫相得。当洪流而鼓迅风。崇朝万里。不足怪也。开元末。天子倦于勤而安其安。高视穆清。霈然大满。于是乎有泰极之变。荆州起而扶之。举为时害。动咈上欲。日与谗党抗衡于交戟之中。势若微阳战阴。冲密云而吐丹气。歘耀而灭。又何难乎。所痛者。逢一时。事一圣。践其迹。执其柄。而有可有不可。有成有不成。况乎差池草茅。沈落光耀者。复何言哉。复何言哉。曹溪沙门灵澈。虽脱离世务。而犹好正直。得其图像。因以示予。睹而感之。乃作赞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371947'>唐有栋臣，往矣其邈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371947'>世传遗像，以觉后学。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371947'>德容恢异，天骨峻擢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371947'>波澄东溟，日照太岳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371947'>具瞻崇崇，起敬起忠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371947'>貌与神会，凛然生风。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371947'>气蕴逆鳞，色形匪躬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371947'>当时曲直，如在胸中。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371947'>鲲鳞初脱，激海以化。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371947'>羊角中颓，摩天而下。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371947'>无喜无愠，亦如此画。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371947'>呜呼为臣，儆尔夙夜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1371947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1371947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1371947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　在京师，有诗赠友人。作品：《赠友人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第8页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠友人</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", id='poem_sentence_0_18506'>南山双乔松，擢本皆千寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18506'>夕流膏露津，朝被青云阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18506'>负雪出深涧，摇风倚高岑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18506'>明堂久不构，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_18506", 18506, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>云干</span>何森森。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18506'>匠意方雕巧，时情正誇淫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18506'>生材会有用，天地岂无心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18506'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>，24岁</div><div id='4571ef0ea1904e14af65290d2f1b345d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　本年底返回京师，有序文送友人至源游蜀。作品：《送友人游蜀序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第30页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送友人游蜀序</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371911")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371911'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371911'>始吾挹至源之貌。若陇底积雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371911_comment'></div>耸寒木于云溪。次吾览至源之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371911_comment'></div>若骊龙相追。弄明月于泉窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371911_comment'></div>末吾听至源之论。若泰山欲雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371911_comment'></div>倒云气于沧溟。如其貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371911_comment'></div>可以振肃周行。如其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371911_comment'></div>可以光润石渠。如其论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371911_comment'></div>可以感动宣室。而沦荡江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371911_comment'></div>垂二十年。则不知天所以生之之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371911_comment'></div>贞元甲乙岁。以亲故劝勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371911_comment'></div>来游京师。时然后言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371911_comment'></div>无辩以动众。乐然后笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371911_comment'></div>无欢以接物。义然后取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371911_comment'></div>无食以宁居。慨然悔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371911_comment'></div>决策长往。因登紫阁峰而指曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371911_comment'></div>西南青冥。色连岷峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371911_comment'></div>吾行何归。山尽则住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371911_comment'></div>翌日告别于友人。太原王元运顾谓予曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371911_comment'></div>高云出岫。无时雨之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371911_comment'></div>与风悠扬。转远而散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371911_comment'></div>若至源者。其犹云耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371911_comment'></div>盍亦赠之。序予和汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371911_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1371911_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='919f5a9e1b6543468b65e1bb4fdaded1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("919f5a9e1b6543468b65e1bb4fdaded1");'><span id='919f5a9e1b6543468b65e1bb4fdaded1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=798')">796-798年</a>，25-27岁</div><div id='919f5a9e1b6543468b65e1bb4fdaded1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>　年底返回长安，经华山下拜祭王猛墓，有文。作品：《华山下酹王景略墓文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第86页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华山酹王景略墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（796年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371964")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371964'>唐贞元十五年十一月六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371964_comment'></div>河东男子吕温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371964_comment'></div>敬酹于苻秦丞相王公景略之墓曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371964_comment'></div>昔马氏暴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371964_comment'></div>世不及三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371964_comment'></div>拔根河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371964_comment'></div>遗蘖东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371964_comment'></div>锯牙霆声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371964_comment'></div>争逐婪婪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371964_comment'></div>天下为血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371964_comment'></div>晋犹清谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371964_comment'></div>帝命景略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371964_comment'></div>被兹文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371964_comment'></div>秉心无亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371964_comment'></div>用则为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371964_comment'></div>惟秦悼世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371964_comment'></div>求我草莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371964_comment'></div>振衣投畚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371964_comment'></div>乃作雷雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371964_comment'></div>雨莫不润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371964_comment'></div>雷莫不震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371964_comment'></div>吸凉吞燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371964_comment'></div>嚼魏含晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371964_comment'></div>海荡风扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371964_comment'></div>天临岳镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371964_comment'></div>功存生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371964_comment'></div>是曰大顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371964_comment'></div>武功成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371964_comment'></div>文理定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371964_comment'></div>晏开太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371964_comment'></div>垂及三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371964_comment'></div>子也无寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371964_comment'></div>秦其不祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371964_comment'></div>日沉天昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371964_comment'></div>水竭龙死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371964_comment'></div>时更运改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371964_comment'></div>道历消长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371964_comment'></div>屹彼壮骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371964_comment'></div>沉为朽壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371964_comment'></div>烈气犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371964_comment'></div>英风可想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371964_comment'></div>云开华山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371964_comment'></div>若见精爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371964_comment'></div>乐毅佐燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371964_comment'></div>功负其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371964_comment'></div>汉犹求后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371964_comment'></div>宠号华成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371964_comment'></div>曷如夫子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371964_comment'></div>翊运而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371964_comment'></div>廓定八州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371964_comment'></div>泽流群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371964_comment'></div>历代王者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371964_comment'></div>迨我圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371964_comment'></div>盛德未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371964_comment'></div>荒坟欲平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371964_comment'></div>我行于东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371964_comment'></div>税驾酾酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371964_comment'></div>才何敢望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371964_comment'></div>数亦未偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371964_comment'></div>终期自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371964_comment'></div>窥子户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371964_comment'></div>灵魂若存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371964_comment'></div>死为冥友。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1371964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　在京师，准备来年省试。九月，其父吕温贬潭州刺史，兼御史中丞、湖南观察使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　秋，在京师，有序送琴客摇兼济东归。作品：《送琴客摇兼济东归便道谒王虢州序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第30页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送琴客摇兼济东归便道谒王虢州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371916")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371916'>东海摇兼济。年十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371916_comment'></div>从淮南大军。有奇童之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371916_comment'></div>岁既冠。历泗上剧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371916_comment'></div>振能吏之声。而尚气节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371916_comment'></div>重言诺。临财廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371916_comment'></div>见义勇。蕴崇具美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371916_comment'></div>发以雅琴。琅琅然若佩玉之有冲牙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371916_comment'></div>贞元丁丑岁。观艺京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371916_comment'></div>冲宇罕窥。正声寡听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371916_comment'></div>道不苟合。浩然东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371916_comment'></div>水流无心。遇用则止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371916_comment'></div>宏农守御史中丞王公得子最深。且东诸侯之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371916_comment'></div>傥羽翼吾道。铿锵尔音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371916_comment'></div>飞而鸣之。一日千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371916_comment'></div>则何公门不可曳长裾乎。大丈夫风波未始有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371916_comment'></div>生死且不足问。况能离忧乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371916_comment'></div>白露降。秋云起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371916_comment'></div>仰见太华。壮心勃兴若不激徵变商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371916_comment'></div>是孤慷慨吾季恭也。诗有逸气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371916_comment'></div>盍韵钟律。播于丝桐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371916_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1371916_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　在京师，与柳茂直联句，有序文。作品：《联句诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第31页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>联句诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371915")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371915'>河东柳茂直与予有潘杨之睦。且道义相得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371915_comment'></div>予兄弟志守拙默。不交当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371915_comment'></div>晨昏之外。靖专一室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371915_comment'></div>顾我者唯茂直而已。以为切磋盖常事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371915_comment'></div>讨论有宴息。导志气徒然起愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371915_comment'></div>议世事予欲无言。其或晴天旷景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371915_comment'></div>浩荡多思。永夜高月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371915_comment'></div>耿耿不寐。或风露初晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371915_comment'></div>恍若有得。或烟雨如晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371915_comment'></div>缅怀所思。则何以节宣惨舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371915_comment'></div>畅达情性。其有易于诗乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371915_comment'></div>乃因翰墨之馀。琴酒之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371915_comment'></div>属物命篇。联珠迭唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371915_comment'></div>审韵谐律。同声相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371915_comment'></div>研情比象。造境皆会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371915_comment'></div>亦犹众壑合注。浸为大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371915_comment'></div>群山出云。混成一气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371915_comment'></div>朗宣五色。微阐六义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371915_comment'></div>虽小道必有可观。其在兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371915_comment'></div>茂直命予序述。存以编简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371915_comment'></div>俾后之观者。知吾党所立之滥觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371915_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1371915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　登进士第，尚书左丞顾少连知贡举，试赋。作品：《礼部试鉴止水赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第4页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　自梁州返京后，代齐抗为文祭襄州刺史樊泽。作品：《代齐常侍祭樊襄阳文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第87页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代齐常侍祭樊襄阳文</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371966")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371966'>维年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371966_comment'></div>某官某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371966_comment'></div>以清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371966_comment'></div>敬祭于故襄阳节度使右仆射赠司空南阳樊公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371966_comment'></div>惟公直方忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371966_comment'></div>沉敏肃给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371966_comment'></div>通如川流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371966_comment'></div>守若山立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371966_comment'></div>精气方运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371966_comment'></div>垂天难戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371966_comment'></div>建中旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371966_comment'></div>策名帝聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371966_comment'></div>昌言右掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371966_comment'></div>高步南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371966_comment'></div>爰膺使选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371966_comment'></div>将命序戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371966_comment'></div>信在言前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371966_comment'></div>知行诚中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371966_comment'></div>消息其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371966_comment'></div>车书以同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371966_comment'></div>寇逼汉南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371966_comment'></div>乃佐戎律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371966_comment'></div>偏师靖难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371966_comment'></div>全功受钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371966_comment'></div>兵荒之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371966_comment'></div>政克画一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371966_comment'></div>直绳威奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371966_comment'></div>柔辔惠物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371966_comment'></div>一临荆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371966_comment'></div>再抚岘阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371966_comment'></div>积德逾纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371966_comment'></div>闇然弥彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371966_comment'></div>天不慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371966_comment'></div>人之云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371966_comment'></div>朝野震悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371966_comment'></div>岂惟一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371966_comment'></div>清永之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371966_comment'></div>获同王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371966_comment'></div>相府之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371966_comment'></div>谬厕公议。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371966_comment'></div>备归精义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371966_comment'></div>交以义合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371966_comment'></div>情由道至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371966_comment'></div>循躬虽虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371966_comment'></div>望古无愧。<div id='poem_sentence_54_1371966_comment'></div>谁其问夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371966_comment'></div>日月将葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371966_comment'></div>哀荣式备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371966_comment'></div>歆此精意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371966_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1371966_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　在长安，有感作诗。作品：《闻砧有感》<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371878_comment'></div>伏见今月十四日制命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371878_comment'></div>以尊尊亲亲之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371878_comment'></div>虔祔献祖懿祖于德明兴圣庙室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371878_comment'></div>正太祖景皇帝东向之尊者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371878_comment'></div>称情靡忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371878_comment'></div>合敬有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371878_comment'></div>百神得受职之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371878_comment'></div>万国知来敬之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371878_comment'></div>中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371878_comment'></div>臣闻国有事莫大于严祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371878_comment'></div>礼有经莫大于尊祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371878_comment'></div>夏殷得之以繁祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371878_comment'></div>周汉用之以休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371878_comment'></div>爰自魏晋。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>　春，浮屠文畅从京城将行东南，韩愈作序送之，吕温与白居易、权德舆亦有诗相送。作品：《送文畅上人东游》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第14页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送文畅上人东游</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18453")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18453'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18453'>随缘聊振锡，高步出东城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18453'>水止<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作月上）</span>无恒地，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_18453", 18453, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>云行</span>不计程。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18453'>到时为彼岸，过处即前生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18453'>今日临岐别，吾徒自有情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18453'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>　在京任左拾遗。翰林待诏王伾与山阴王叔文俱娱侍太子，吕温、柳宗元、刘禹锡、李景俭等与之交往密切，其中，吕、柳、李三人尤为王叔文所重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年11月</a>　十一月，为李景俭之母作墓志铭。作品：《唐故太子舍人李府君夫人荥阳郑氏墓志铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷7第75页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故唐太子舍人李府君夫人荥阳郑氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（800年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371960")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371960'>夫人讳字荥阳人。郑于姬姓最亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371960_comment'></div>为天下著族。自秦汉至于皇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371960_comment'></div>萎蕤轩冕。耿曜图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371960_comment'></div>如洪河东导江汉。其源流不待问而可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371960_comment'></div>高祖守元。朝散大夫袭丹徒公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371960_comment'></div>曾祖嘉会。朝散大夫雅州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371960_comment'></div>大父曔。正议大夫金衢二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371960_comment'></div>严考钦英。朝议郎杭州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371960_comment'></div>皆以天爵。屈于人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371960_comment'></div>滋庆羡美。实生夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371960_comment'></div>夫人始生。辨物而智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371960_comment'></div>能言而信。既笄而知礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371960_comment'></div>有行而制义。性与天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371960_comment'></div>质无表饰。冲灵虚寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371960_comment'></div>和气交畅。不严厉而妇道自著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371960_comment'></div>不整峻而母仪有俨。实柔德之黄中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371960_comment'></div>壸闱之尽善者。中舍府君出自我睿宗让皇帝之孙汉中王之予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371960_comment'></div>乃于钟鼎宝玉之间杰立。雅尚文学政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371960_comment'></div>龟龙搢绅。而夫人躬蘋藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371960_comment'></div>服浣濯。去华斲雕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371960_comment'></div>激清守素。辅佐将顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371960_comment'></div>实有力焉。昼哭之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371960_comment'></div>训成诸子。长曰景俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371960_comment'></div>负王佐之才。探圣人之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371960_comment'></div>磅礡秀气。拔乎其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371960_comment'></div>次曰景儒景信景仁。皆文敏絜修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371960_comment'></div>保家良主。有以见夫人明裕善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371960_comment'></div>继成义方。宜其及公侯必复之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371960_comment'></div>享春秋以贵之庆。闻天子叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371960_comment'></div>见公卿升堂。而时命不偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371960_comment'></div>与善茫昧。景俭有捧檄之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371960_comment'></div>夫人从养于越州。以贞元十九年终于官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371960_comment'></div>降生五十有四。景俭等以某年十一月一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371960_comment'></div>号奉裳帷。祔于京兆富平县万寿原之旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371960_comment'></div>从周礼也。以某辱久要之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371960_comment'></div>俾稽懿实。敬为铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371960_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1371960'>周受成命。郑为戚藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371960_comment'></div>以国命氏。郁闻德门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371960_comment'></div>缁衣垂芳。荥波发源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371960_comment'></div>为为梓。为兰为荪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371960_comment'></div>梓惟何。卿材克绍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371960_comment'></div>兰荪惟何。女德之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371960_comment'></div>抑抑夫人。自他有耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371960_comment'></div>玉度旁达。泉心内照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371960_comment'></div>和顺积中。高明有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371960_comment'></div>辅佐君子。与道始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371960_comment'></div>族姻成化。慈俭为宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371960_comment'></div>让帝之后。门生素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371960_comment'></div>宜及子贵。以荣教义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371960_comment'></div>如何高堂。奄忽违弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371960_comment'></div>万岁原上。松楸永秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371960_comment'></div>惟命罕言。德音无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371960_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1371960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>　在京官左拾遗，有文。作品：《凌烟阁勋臣颂并序》<span showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝亲庶政颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371868")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371868_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371868'>臣闻光宅大宝。茂育群生。神而明之。必在上圣。然则所同者道。所异者时。或以垂拱仰成。或以励精自致。及乎俗跻仁寿。理洽时邕。弛张之政不殊。劳逸之功则倍。我皇帝体至化。含元精。苞乾刚。履坤顺。诞膺骏命。恢纂鸿休。宣八圣之重光。集百灵之奥祉。如天之焘。如地之容。鼓义为雷霆。奋仁为风雨。干璇衡而转七曜。悬金镜而纳九围。廓氛沴而川澄。沓祯祥而山委。昔轩辕氏斩蚩尤。灭火帝。功至大矣。若非仗风后之助。受元女之符。未能尅也。陶唐氏诛四罪。定水灾。德至厚矣。若非大舜之登庸。伯禹之尽力。未能成也。汤以伊尹为相。始定殷功。武以太公为师。乃康周道。高宗绍复。资傅说启沃之言。宣王中兴。赖山甫将明之政。今陛下太康四海。雄轶二纪。百姓不知其日用。群臣无望于清光。而乃业迈乎前王。功高乎古烈。圣作物睹。孰知其源。窃以管窥天倪。蠡挹溟量。庶乎大略。可得而言焉。陛下自代天统物之初。则以屈已济人为意。虔临庶政。穷总万枢。四册贤良。六亲郊祀。勤恤于理本。尽瘁于生灵。详旷代之所未详。虑列辟之所未虑。夏景赅而方食。寒星在而求衣。寸阴不舍于论思。子夜犹观乎启事。除一物之患而品类以安。伸匹夫之冤而庶狱自直。弃瑕而录用。含垢而宥过。小善可纪。必拔于宸衷。片言有孚。不忘于睿听。至如天时之丰约。地利之险夷。邦赋之盈虚。师律之贞暴。闾阎之疾苦。稼穑之艰难。人风之情伪。吏理之得失。莫不密归神算。潜纳皇明。虽阴阳不能以气欺。虽神鬼不能以形遁。何细而不及。何大而不苞。何秘而不彰。何难而不就。犹复登台念在险之惨。闻乐思向隅之情。御裘感裋褐之寒。临膳忧箪食之馁。日慎一日。既泰而不自泰。既安而不自安。兢兢乎。业业乎。此其所以广运而有成。全功之克举者也。然而感覆焘之恩者。欲天之弥高。荷容载之德者。欲地之弥厚。仰照临之明者。欲日月之弥光。微臣被淳风。饮元泽。亲挹行事。亲睹升平。忧劳诚难。愿陛下勉之而已。美善诚尽。愿陛下保之而已。若夫虽休勿休。元默优柔。君上之体也。遹观厥成。蹈舞颂声。臣下之职也。为而不有。德莫至焉。知而不称。罪莫大焉。臣某敢昧死再拜稽首。献皇帝亲庶政颂一首。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371868'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371868'>士师迈德，元元储庆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371868'>幽而复曜，高祖受命。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371868'>贞观致理，开元殷盛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371868'>艰而复康，皇帝亲政。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371868'>受命维何，邈万斯年。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371868'>亲政维何，夕惕朝乾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371868'>天道福谦，我则奉天。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371868'>生人在勤，我则率先。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371868'>忧尧之心，劳禹之形。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371868'>求人之瘼，思国之经。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371868'>年亦丰止，御膳不馨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371868'>夜如何其，皇寝未宁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1371868'>修文偃武，太和氤氲。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1371868'>海不扬波，天无纤氛。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1371868'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1371868", 1371868, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鸟章</span>之长，椎吉之君。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1371868'>会朝明庭，其从如云。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1371868'>巍巍崇崇，于穆昭融。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1371868'>宜播大乐，以宣皇风。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1371868'>铿锵盛德，蹈厉神功。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1371868'>下臣作颂，永示无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1371868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1371868'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1371868_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狄梁公立卢陵王传赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371944")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371944_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371944'>梁公以武氏篡盗。国命如缀。翊安宗社。非我而谁。是用蒙大耻。履大险。耸节振美。以持世心。闲高祖天下于方寸之地。盗力虽盛。莫之敢窥。唐复为唐。繄公是赖。后代昧者。颇归功于五臣。殊不知五臣之功。公所授也。客有以李北海所传示予者。述卢陵王废立之际。见公如生。贻诸将来。可以不惑。敢摅愤而赞之。词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371944'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371944'>于休梁公，社稷之臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371944'>濡迹应变，与唐屈伸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371944'>妖虹横天，鸣牝专晨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371944'>独立大道，指南生人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371944'>阖辟有期，命先我时。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371944'>乃建国本，代天张机。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371944'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1371944", 1371944, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>取日</span>虞渊，洗光咸池。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371944'>潜授五龙，夹之以飞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371944'>临终指麾，皇业再基。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371944'>运起身后，功成不知。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371944'>穆若清风，嶷然宏规。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371944'>凡为臣者，可不度思。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>续羊叔子传赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371945")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371945'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371945'>天厌鼎峙，蜀灭魏改。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371945'>锡晋羊公，以同四海。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371945'>儒衣登坛，岳镇荆蛮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371945'>十万之众，从公而闲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371945'>逍遥岘阳，傲视勍敌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371945'>用仁为间，出入无迹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371945'>吴国虽守，吴心已降。<div
