id='poem_sentence_14_1371945'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1371945_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>功臣恕死议</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371901")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371901'>昔卫蒯聩以窃国之诈。盟其陪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371901_comment'></div>服冕乘轩。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1371901", 1371901, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>三死</span>无与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371901_comment'></div>近代惑者。因为口实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371901_comment'></div>于是乎有功臣恕死之典。考诸古训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371901_comment'></div>其异端欤。稽诸时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371901_comment'></div>其乱本欤。何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371901_comment'></div>有国之柄。莫大乎刑赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371901_comment'></div>人生有欲。不可以不制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371901_comment'></div>天讨有罪。不可以不刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371901_comment'></div>盖刑者。圣王所以佐道德而齐天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371901_comment'></div>功济乎物。不可以不赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371901_comment'></div>赏劝乎功。不可以不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371901_comment'></div>盖信者。圣人所以一号令而惇天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371901_comment'></div>然则恕死之典。弃信而废刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371901_comment'></div>何以言之。夫立功者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371901_comment'></div>自八元十乱之后。非尽能贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371901_comment'></div>或有起屠贩垄亩行阵之间。乘帝王应天顺人之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371901_comment'></div>用力无几。遂贪天功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371901_comment'></div>超腾风云。各得变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371901_comment'></div>率劳怙宠。崛强自负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371901_comment'></div>僭冒无厌。见利忘义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371901_comment'></div>是宜崇威峻法。大为之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371901_comment'></div>而反丹书铁券。许以不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371901_comment'></div>其功大者。可以五作乱而十犯上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371901_comment'></div>孰不以暴为无伤乎。且人君之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371901_comment'></div>如涣汗不反。既与之要天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371901_comment'></div>誓山河。卒一旦失驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371901_comment'></div>有黥韩之罪。神怒人怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371901_comment'></div>不得已而诛。是弃信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371901_comment'></div>若恣行凶险。隳突宪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371901_comment'></div>或奸锋将发。衅逼宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371901_comment'></div>乃念斯言之玷。忍而不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371901_comment'></div>是废刑也。向者才得其尘涓之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371901_comment'></div>萤烛之助。而信弃刑废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371901_comment'></div>将焉用之。使贤而有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371901_comment'></div>惊宠惧满。自居无过之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371901_comment'></div>何恕死为。使愚而有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371901_comment'></div>小人不幸。又告以无死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371901_comment'></div>是增骄而启奸。适所谓赏之祸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371901_comment'></div>虽恕之死。其能免乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371901_comment'></div>夫其贤如太公。忠如伊尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371901_comment'></div>惟君知臣。可以勿贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371901_comment'></div>而遽宥以罪死。是逆其不忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371901_comment'></div>非所以待之以诚。而尽君子之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371901_comment'></div>若乃猾如狗盗。庸如黥徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371901_comment'></div>未有罪而先恕之死。是不许其慕生廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371901_comment'></div>自固名节。非所以道之以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371901_comment'></div>而劝小人之善也。以为明君之处劳臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371901_comment'></div>安之以爵禄。拘之以纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371901_comment'></div>明之以好恶。耸之以祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371901_comment'></div>使得迁善远罪。保勋全名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371901_comment'></div>剖符传庆。与国终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371901_comment'></div>恩斯勤斯。是亦极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371901_comment'></div>奈何挠权乱法。以罪宠人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371901_comment'></div>坠信赏必罚之典。亏昭德塞违之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371901_comment'></div>恐非哲王经邦轨物之制也。谨议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371901_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1371901_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复汉以粟为赏罚议</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371902")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371902'>议曰。先王赏以饰喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371902_comment'></div>罚以饰怒。喜必待功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371902_comment'></div>而赏不僭行。怒必得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371902_comment'></div>而罚无轻赦。其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371902_comment'></div>汉室杂霸道而隳王制。昧宏规而狃小利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371902_comment'></div>俾人纳粟。除罪拜爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371902_comment'></div>以罚人则废法。以赏人则废功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371902_comment'></div>以储蓄则废本。是阻劳惠奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371902_comment'></div>而怠弃南亩也。何以言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371902_comment'></div>惟名与器。不可假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371902_comment'></div>而班爵于兼并之家。析圭于滞积之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371902_comment'></div>使屠沽贱隶。陵驾英豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371902_comment'></div>苟有怀廉耻之心。岂复致患难之死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371902_comment'></div>虽月要天地。日誓山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371902_comment'></div>而赏不足以劝矣。天讨有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371902_comment'></div>刑兹无赦。而挠权于残贼之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371902_comment'></div>屈法于奸宄之党。使凶人酷吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371902_comment'></div>言暴无伤。苟开必免之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371902_comment'></div>孰惩罔极之恶。虽临以斧钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371902_comment'></div>驱于鼎镬。而刑不足以威矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371902_comment'></div>且朝縻好爵。以粟授受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371902_comment'></div>国有常刑。以粟出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371902_comment'></div>贪利爱生之夫。孰不愿空垄亩而货圭组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371902_comment'></div>竭仓廪而救死亡。拜爵者坐等封君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371902_comment'></div>遂忘其本业。免罪者室如悬磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371902_comment'></div>曷保其生聚。虽使三公九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371902_comment'></div>躬执耒耜。而啬不可以务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371902_comment'></div>于戏。赏罚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371902_comment'></div>君人之大柄。农啬者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371902_comment'></div>为国之永图。忽而弃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371902_comment'></div>曾不是念。而利乎国储之暂实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371902_comment'></div>兵食之仅济。其何补欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371902_comment'></div>然而汉承秦弊。中国耗弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371902_comment'></div>高惠务厥完辑。孝文守以恭俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371902_comment'></div>德未浃于海外。威未行于四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371902_comment'></div>边候犹闻击柝。戎士不得解甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371902_comment'></div>晁错是以有权宜之对。救弊之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371902_comment'></div>偷利于当代。幸成于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371902_comment'></div>虽曰有因而为。终贻识者之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371902_comment'></div>国家体元御极。继天而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371902_comment'></div>腾轶殷周。绍休唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371902_comment'></div>率我蒸人。登于寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371902_comment'></div>王一变至于帝。帝一变至于皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371902_comment'></div>非大道之谟不听。非圣德之猷不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371902_comment'></div>焉有袭近古之失策。采庸臣之诡论者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371902_comment'></div>必患国廪犹虚。边馈未继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371902_comment'></div>莫若兴李悝之平籴。务充国之屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371902_comment'></div>练将简兵。以省军费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371902_comment'></div>轻徭薄赋。以悦人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371902_comment'></div>东作一兴。西成再秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371902_comment'></div>则太仓之蓄如京矣。塞下之稼如云矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371902_comment'></div>亦何必亏昭德塞违之道。坠信赏必罚之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371902_comment'></div>恐非圣唐经邦轨物之制也。谨议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371902_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1371902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>人文化成论</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371922")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371922'>易曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371922_comment'></div>观乎人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371922_comment'></div>以化成天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371922_comment'></div>能讽其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371922_comment'></div>盖有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371922_comment'></div>未有明其义者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371922_comment'></div>尝试论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371922_comment'></div>夫一二相生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371922_comment'></div>大钧造物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371922_comment'></div>百化交错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371922_comment'></div>六气节宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371922_comment'></div>或阴阖而阳开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371922_comment'></div>或天经而地纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371922_comment'></div>有圣作则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371922_comment'></div>实为人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371922_comment'></div>若乃夫以刚克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371922_comment'></div>妻以柔立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371922_comment'></div>父慈而教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371922_comment'></div>子孝而箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371922_comment'></div>此室家之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371922_comment'></div>君以仁使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371922_comment'></div>臣以义事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371922_comment'></div>予违汝弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371922_comment'></div>献可替否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371922_comment'></div>此朝廷之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371922_comment'></div>三公论道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371922_comment'></div>六卿分职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371922_comment'></div>九流异趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371922_comment'></div>百揆同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371922_comment'></div>此官司之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371922_comment'></div>宽则人慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371922_comment'></div>纠之以猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371922_comment'></div>猛则人残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371922_comment'></div>施之以宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371922_comment'></div>宽以济猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371922_comment'></div>猛以济宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371922_comment'></div>此刑政之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371922_comment'></div>乐胜则流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371922_comment'></div>遏之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371922_comment'></div>礼胜则离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371922_comment'></div>和之以乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371922_comment'></div>与时消息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371922_comment'></div>因俗变通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371922_comment'></div>此教化之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371922_comment'></div>文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371922_comment'></div>盖言错综庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371922_comment'></div>藻绘人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371922_comment'></div>如成文焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371922_comment'></div>以致其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371922_comment'></div>然则人文化成之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371922_comment'></div>其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371922_comment'></div>而近代谄谀之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371922_comment'></div>特以时君不能则象乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371922_comment'></div>祖述尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371922_comment'></div>作化成天下之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371922_comment'></div>乃以旂常冕服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371922_comment'></div>章句翰墨为人文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371922_comment'></div>遂使君人者浩然忘本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371922_comment'></div>沛然自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371922_comment'></div>盛威仪以求至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371922_comment'></div>坐吟咏而待升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371922_comment'></div>流荡因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371922_comment'></div>败而未悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371922_comment'></div>不其痛欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371922_comment'></div>必以旂常冕服为人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371922_comment'></div>则秦汉魏晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371922_comment'></div>声明文物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371922_comment'></div>礼缛五帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371922_comment'></div>仪繁三王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371922_comment'></div>可曰焕乎其有文章矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371922_comment'></div>何衰乱之多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371922_comment'></div>必以章句翰墨为人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371922_comment'></div>则陈后主隋炀帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371922_comment'></div>雍容绮靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371922_comment'></div>洋溢编简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371922_comment'></div>可曰文思安安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371922_comment'></div>何灭亡之速也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371922_comment'></div>覈之以名义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371922_comment'></div>研之以情实既如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371922_comment'></div>较之以今古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371922_comment'></div>质之以成败又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371922_comment'></div>传不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371922_comment'></div>经纬天地曰文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371922_comment'></div>礼不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371922_comment'></div>文王以文治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371922_comment'></div>则文之时义大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371922_comment'></div>焉可以名数末流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371922_comment'></div>雕虫小伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371922_comment'></div>厕杂其间乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1371922_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三不欺先后论</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371923")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371923'>昔宓子贱为单父也。人不忍欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371923_comment'></div>国侨为郑也。人不能欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371923_comment'></div>西门豹为邺也。人不敢欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371923_comment'></div>此皆为政不同。同归于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371923_comment'></div>作干事之称首。贻牧人之经范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371923_comment'></div>汪洋古今。辉焯图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371923_comment'></div>穷理而语。固有优劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371923_comment'></div>择善而行。岂无先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371923_comment'></div>请试论之。子贱仕衰乱之鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371923_comment'></div>而邑偪强齐。仗义为城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371923_comment'></div>倚仁为干橹。当鲸吞之大敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371923_comment'></div>鸠狼顾之遗黎。涣离形检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371923_comment'></div>妙用心术。惠训不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371923_comment'></div>乃无得而称。视民如伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371923_comment'></div>而不有其爱。感而动之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371923_comment'></div>阴阳运于无言。诚而明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371923_comment'></div>日月悬于方寸。是则不求不欺于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371923_comment'></div>而人不忍欺矣。子产摄晋楚之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371923_comment'></div>而靖恭尔位。役智利物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371923_comment'></div>饬躬励俗。守之以信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371923_comment'></div>行之以礼。告之以慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371923_comment'></div>临之以明察。如镜洞照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371923_comment'></div>如衡诚悬。是则求人不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371923_comment'></div>而人亦不能欺矣。西门豹当战国之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371923_comment'></div>而克修茂绩。身为纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371923_comment'></div>言有典章。刚包其柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371923_comment'></div>威克厥爱。权之以法制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371923_comment'></div>董之以刑罚。火烈人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371923_comment'></div>霜清物心。是则责人不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371923_comment'></div>而人固不敢欺矣。夫不忍欺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371923_comment'></div>至诚潜感。是曰上德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371923_comment'></div>尧舜之吏也。不能欺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371923_comment'></div>明智旁达。是曰有政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371923_comment'></div>三王之吏也。不敢欺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371923_comment'></div>严威允济。是曰能刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371923_comment'></div>五霸之吏也。诚不足至于智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371923_comment'></div>智不足至于威。大小之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371923_comment'></div>朗然可见。然而事在折衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371923_comment'></div>理资渐致。德宜全举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371923_comment'></div>道贵兼通。必也修诚而弃智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371923_comment'></div>诚未至而致理或亏。任智而废威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371923_comment'></div>智未周而暴乱将起。不若兼而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371923_comment'></div>迭收其效。一之日二之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371923_comment'></div>刑明威立。使人畏而不敢欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371923_comment'></div>三之日四之日。智达政成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371923_comment'></div>使人敬而不能欺。五之日六之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371923_comment'></div>志孚诚格。使人感而不忍欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371923_comment'></div>以宽济猛。同二气之和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371923_comment'></div>自迩陟遐。比三才之具美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371923_comment'></div>苟非全德大器。其孰能至于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371923_comment'></div>若不暇会其源流。统其宗极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371923_comment'></div>而姑定优劣。直论先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371923_comment'></div>则尧舜之吏。与王霸不同年而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371923_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1371923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年</a>　齐抗卒。五月前，吕温在京代宰相作文以祭。作品：《代宰相祭故齐相公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第87页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰相祭故齐相公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（804年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371965")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371965'>维年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371965_comment'></div>某官某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371965_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371965_comment'></div>敬祭于中书侍郎平章事太子宾客赠户部尚书齐公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371965_comment'></div>古人所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371965_comment'></div>有道有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371965_comment'></div>唯公挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371965_comment'></div>克叶昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371965_comment'></div>云引乔干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371965_comment'></div>雷起幽姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371965_comment'></div>礼义诚衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371965_comment'></div>文章元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371965_comment'></div>学睹儒奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371965_comment'></div>政为吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371965_comment'></div>金锵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1371965", 1371965, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>遐音</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371965_comment'></div>玉立清仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371965_comment'></div>始践南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371965_comment'></div>洎在左掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371965_comment'></div>麾幢符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371965_comment'></div>礼乐图籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371965_comment'></div>萎蕤焜耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371965_comment'></div>出入扬历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371965_comment'></div>晦而逾明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371965_comment'></div>虚乃受益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371965_comment'></div>爰登大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371965_comment'></div>光赞庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371965_comment'></div>栋材斯全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371965_comment'></div>鼎味以适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371965_comment'></div>道始交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371965_comment'></div>志惟匪躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371965_comment'></div>方尽嘉猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371965_comment'></div>以奉时雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371965_comment'></div>疾罢私室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371965_comment'></div>宠宾储宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371965_comment'></div>日冀勿药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371965_comment'></div>再谐至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371965_comment'></div>如何忽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371965_comment'></div>降命不融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371965_comment'></div>竟孤宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371965_comment'></div>谁问苍穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371965_comment'></div>佑早辱见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371965_comment'></div>深契风义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371965_comment'></div>耽获同枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371965_comment'></div>备得纯懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371965_comment'></div>珣瑜三河交代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371965_comment'></div>郢侧两掖联事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371965_comment'></div>气以正合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371965_comment'></div>情由道至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371965_comment'></div>视孤有怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371965_comment'></div>恸寝无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371965_comment'></div>龟兆叶吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371965_comment'></div>素车东辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371965_comment'></div>喉舌追命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371965_comment'></div>股肱殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371965_comment'></div>魂留魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371965_comment'></div>形返周原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371965_comment'></div>凡我寮旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371965_comment'></div>举觞以言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371965_comment'></div>神听不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371965_comment'></div>知余所敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371965_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1371965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年</a>　五月前，吕温在京作文祭座主顾少连。作品：《祭座主故兵部尚书顾公文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此文。）</span><div id='poem_1371968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭座主故兵部尚书顾公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（804年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371968")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371968'>维贞元十年岁次甲申月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371968_comment'></div>门生侍御史王播监察御史刘禹锡陈讽柳宗元左拾遗吕温李逢吉右拾遗卢元辅剑南西川观察支使李正叔万年县主簿谈元茂集贤殿校书郎王启秘书省校书郎李建京兆府文学李逢渭南县尉席夔鄠县尉张隶初奉礼郎独孤郁协律郎萧节奉礼郎时元佐荥阳主薄李宗衡前乡贡进士郑素等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371968_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371968_comment'></div>祭于座主故兵部尚书东都留守顾公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371968_comment'></div>峨峨灵山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371968_comment'></div>时雨将泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371968_comment'></div>眈眈大厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371968_comment'></div>崇构巳设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371968_comment'></div>岁旱方极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371968_comment'></div>川流遽阏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371968_comment'></div>宏栋待施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371968_comment'></div>梁木斯折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371968_comment'></div>玉碎清莹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371968_comment'></div>芝焚酷烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371968_comment'></div>贞方独留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371968_comment'></div>千古不灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371968_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371968_comment'></div>伏惟公神气辅质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371968_comment'></div>天降英灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371968_comment'></div>刚健中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371968_comment'></div>内外和明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371968_comment'></div>岐嶷之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371968_comment'></div>不教而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371968_comment'></div>敦敏之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371968_comment'></div>确然巳贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371968_comment'></div>霭霭孤云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371968_comment'></div>逸我高情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371968_comment'></div>昭昭白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371968_comment'></div>悬我明诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371968_comment'></div>志励意深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371968_comment'></div>心融气清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371968_comment'></div>靖若翔隼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371968_comment'></div>蔼若芳英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371968_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371968_comment'></div>立人成身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371968_comment'></div>忠孝一美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371968_comment'></div>自古全者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371968_comment'></div>一人而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371968_comment'></div>明君得臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371968_comment'></div>贤父知子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371968_comment'></div>公独兼备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371968_comment'></div>敢陈终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371968_comment'></div>厥初知礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371968_comment'></div>柔顺义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371968_comment'></div>年未逾丱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371968_comment'></div>道行于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371968_comment'></div>盈庭之戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371968_comment'></div>众稚且狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371968_comment'></div>觿管在身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371968_comment'></div>我独矜庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371968_comment'></div>沐浴风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371968_comment'></div>盥漱雪霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371968_comment'></div>未荐甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371968_comment'></div>未敢衣裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371968_comment'></div>斯惟至性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371968_comment'></div>厥有大孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371968_comment'></div>乃扬儒风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371968_comment'></div>乃奉文教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371968_comment'></div>服勤之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371968_comment'></div>焕饰之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371968_comment'></div>金石成声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371968_comment'></div>缛丽开照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371968_comment'></div>越国山秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371968_comment'></div>吴门水深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_18472'>虚室唯生白，闲情<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作门）</span>却草玄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18472'>迎霜红叶早，过雨碧<span id='poem_1371967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭陆给事文</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年10月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371967")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371967'>维贞元元年岁次乙酉十月景申朔十日乙巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371967_comment'></div>将仕郎守尚书户部员外郎赐绯鱼袋吕某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371967_comment'></div>絜樽寘诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371967_comment'></div>敬祭于故给事中吴郡陆公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371967_comment'></div>呜呼噫嚱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371967_comment'></div>道之难行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371967_comment'></div>古人所悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371967_comment'></div>有时无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371967_comment'></div>有人无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371967_comment'></div>时可人可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371967_comment'></div>则命夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371967_comment'></div>公初负道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371967_comment'></div>年志俱壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371967_comment'></div>已任致君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371967_comment'></div>指掌太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371967_comment'></div>德宗旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371967_comment'></div>始宾明庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371967_comment'></div>拔乎其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371967_comment'></div>聿骏有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371967_comment'></div>实欲以至公大当之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371967_comment'></div>沃明主之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371967_comment'></div>简能易知之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371967_comment'></div>大明主之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371967_comment'></div>难得易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371967_comment'></div>怡然退保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371967_comment'></div>或僶俛从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371967_comment'></div>或栖迟却扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371967_comment'></div>二十年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371967_comment'></div>为郎而老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371967_comment'></div>尝言吾虽已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371967_comment'></div>道不可已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371967_comment'></div>永怀其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371967_comment'></div>见而后死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371967_comment'></div>某以弱龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371967_comment'></div>获谒于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371967_comment'></div>旷代之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371967_comment'></div>一言而同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371967_comment'></div>且曰子非入吾之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371967_comment'></div>入尧舜之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371967_comment'></div>子非观吾之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371967_comment'></div>睹宣尼之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371967_comment'></div>良时未来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371967_comment'></div>吾老子少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371967_comment'></div>异日河图出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371967_comment'></div>凤鸟至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371967_comment'></div>天子咸临泰阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371967_comment'></div>清问理本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371967_comment'></div>其能以生人为重社稷次之之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371967_comment'></div>发吾君聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371967_comment'></div>跻盛唐于雍熙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371967_comment'></div>子若不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371967_comment'></div>吾有望焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371967_comment'></div>某也不佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371967_comment'></div>谬纳大贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371967_comment'></div>其何以充塞所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371967_comment'></div>克当斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371967_comment'></div>姑用绅而书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371967_comment'></div>牍而藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371967_comment'></div>传于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371967_comment'></div>为门户光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371967_comment'></div>既而各沦风波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371967_comment'></div>秦吾索居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371967_comment'></div>某非出处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371967_comment'></div>迫屑无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371967_comment'></div>公高翔海郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371967_comment'></div>与道虚徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371967_comment'></div>犹念垂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371967_comment'></div>研覃若初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371967_comment'></div>作君臣得失之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371967_comment'></div>成春秋不刊之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371967_comment'></div>今年太皇继天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371967_comment'></div>元圣在震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371967_comment'></div>徵公夕拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371967_comment'></div>侍讲古训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371967_comment'></div>皇王秘宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371967_comment'></div>造膝而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371967_comment'></div>以石投水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371967_comment'></div>至诚无朕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371967_comment'></div>讨论未竟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371967_comment'></div>公则既病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371967_comment'></div>重光升矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371967_comment'></div>公病不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371967_comment'></div>河海晏而航楫自隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371967_comment'></div>礼乐作而龟玉先毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371967_comment'></div>与其时而夺其寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371967_comment'></div>吾未知夫所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371967_comment'></div>呜呼惜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371967_comment'></div>某奉使无状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371967_comment'></div>闭留昆夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371967_comment'></div>再换炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371967_comment'></div>言归未期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371967_comment'></div>公方沉瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371967_comment'></div>忘已之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371967_comment'></div>念我否隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371967_comment'></div>发言涟洏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371967_comment'></div>悉所著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371967_comment'></div>付子稚儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371967_comment'></div>曰道之将兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371967_comment'></div>而父其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371967_comment'></div>惧不果待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371967_comment'></div>寓心于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371967_comment'></div>似有明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371967_comment'></div>感公所敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371967_comment'></div>穷荒生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371967_comment'></div>仅及公存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371967_comment'></div>绵顿在床。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371967_comment'></div>深堂昼昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371967_comment'></div>举烛开目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371967_comment'></div>握手无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1371967_comment'></div>自此及终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1371967_comment'></div>曾未浃辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1371967_comment'></div>凡曰识者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1371967_comment'></div>孰堪酸辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1371967_comment'></div>况予之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1371967_comment'></div>岂云他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1371967_comment'></div>涕尽一哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1371967_comment'></div>痛缠百身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1371967_comment'></div>礼不忘本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1371967_comment'></div>卜归江滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1371967_comment'></div>躬执薄酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1371967_comment'></div>心摧气堙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1371967_comment'></div>傥见期之言可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1371967_comment'></div>平生之志获申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1371967_comment'></div>吕氏陆氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1371967_comment'></div>戚休惟均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1371967_comment'></div>魂而有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1371967_comment'></div>歆之听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1371967_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1371967_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_128_1371967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年</a>　冬，在长安遇疾，有诗。作品：《冬日病中即事》<span id='poem_sentence_1_18444_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18444'>背喜朝阳满，心怜暮鸟还。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18444_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年</a>　在长安，代陆质进《春秋集注》，有表文。作品：《代国子陆博士进集注春秋表》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371892'>臣某言。臣闻惟睿作圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371892_comment'></div>观乎人文。达则化成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371892_comment'></div>穷则垂训。先师所以祖述尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371892_comment'></div>志在春秋。悬衡百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371892_comment'></div>拨乱三季。正大当之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371892_comment'></div>清至公之源。通群方以诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371892_comment'></div>贞天下于一。动无不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371892_comment'></div>道德之要机。断无不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371892_comment'></div>帝王之利器。而梁木既坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371892_comment'></div>生知盖寡。三传得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371892_comment'></div>索隐未周。群儒异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371892_comment'></div>致远皆泥。没微言于滋蔓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371892_comment'></div>亡要旨于多岐。奥室不开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371892_comment'></div>漫逾千祀。天其或者将有俟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371892_comment'></div>伏惟陛下德合乾坤。明并日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371892_comment'></div>气和物茂。远至迩安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371892_comment'></div>欲以人情为田。讲学而耨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371892_comment'></div>镇定皇极。耀光时雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371892_comment'></div>道之将行。实在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371892_comment'></div>臣不揣蒙陋。斐然有志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371892_comment'></div>思窥圣奥。仰奉文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371892_comment'></div>以故润州丹阳县主簿臣啖助为严师。以故洋州刺史臣赵匡为益友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371892_comment'></div>考左氏之疏密。辨公谷之善否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371892_comment'></div>务去异端。用明本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371892_comment'></div>助或未尽。敢让当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371892_comment'></div>匡有可行。亦刈其楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371892_comment'></div>辄集注春秋经文。勒成十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371892_comment'></div>上下千载。研覃三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371892_comment'></div>元首虽白。浊河巳清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371892_comment'></div>微臣何幸。与道偕遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371892_comment'></div>窃以德之匪邻。骨肉无应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371892_comment'></div>道苟䜣合。古今相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371892_comment'></div>然则尧舜之心。非宣尼不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371892_comment'></div>宣尼之志。非陛下不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371892_comment'></div>庶因仪凤之辰。永洗获麟之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371892_comment'></div>臣官忝国学。思非出位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371892_comment'></div>以为家宝。罪实欺天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371892_comment'></div>谨昧死写前件书。诣东上阁门奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371892_comment'></div>伏候圣旨。轻黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371892_comment'></div>魂爽飞越。无任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371892_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1371892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=805&endYear=805')">805年</a>　在长安，有文。作品：《古东周城铭》<span id='poem_title_1371951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古东周城铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（805年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371951")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371951_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371951'>鲁昭公三十二年。周苌宏合诸侯之大夫城成周。晋女叔宽曰。天之所坏。不可支也。苌宏违天。必受其咎。异岁。周人杀苌宏。左氏明徵。以为世规。俾持颠之臣。沮其胜气。非所以励尊王垂大顺也。予经其地。而作是铭。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371951'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371951'>文武受命，肇兴西土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371951'>周公作洛，始会风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371951'>居中正本，拓统开祚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371951'>盛则骏奔，衰则夹辅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371951'>平王东迁，九鼎巳轻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371951'>二伯之后，时无义声。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371951'>大夫苌宏，言抗其倾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371951'>坐召诸侯，廓崇王城。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371951'>虽微远猷，实被令名。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371951'>宜福而祸，何伤于明。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371951'>立臣之本，委质定分。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371951'>为仁不卜，临义不问。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1371951'>无天无神，惟道是信。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1371951'>国危必扶，国灭必振。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1371951'>求而不获，乃以死徇。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1371951'>兴亡理乱，在德非运。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1371951'>罪之违天，不可以训。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1371951'>升墟览古，慨焉遐愤。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1371951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1371951'>勒铭颓隅，以劝大顺。<div class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371946")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371946_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371946'>药师如来像者。予妻兰陵萧氏之所绣也。贞元二十年。予奉德宗皇帝之命。西使吐蕃。辞高堂而出万死。介单车而驰不测。国故遽至。戎情猜闭。坎险一遇。星霜再周。夫人盥馈之馀。膏铅不御。日乱蓬首。坐销蕣华。异域无期。良时自晚。始怨冬釭之久。而红芳巳阑。方苦夏景之长。而碧树将落。书委尘箧。迹沦苔阶。渐昧音容。孰知存没。黩龟不告。因梦难徵。触虑成端。沿情多绪。黄昏望绝。见偶语而生疑。清旭意新。闻疾行而误喜。循环何极。刻舟靡寻。浩隔理求。窅非计得。如闻西方有金界极乐药师大雄。散琉璃之宝光。照河沙之国土。能度群品。出诸幽厄。一念必应。万感皆通。是用浚发慧根。妙求真相。断鸣机躬织之素。染懿筐手绩之丝。尽瘁庄严。彰施䌽绣。缠苦心于香缕。注精意于针锋。指下而露洗青莲。思尽而云开白日。然后练时洁室。华设珍供。夕炬传照。晨炉续烟。齐献至诚。泣敷恳愿。遂得慈舟密济。觉路潜引。当道场发念之日。是荒裔来归之辰。幽赞冥符。一何昭焯。乃知织回文之锦。无补离忧。登望归之台。空为废日。与夫心谐妙理。手结胜因。进则有济度之功。退不离清净为本。从长择善。岂同日而言哉。予感其志效。爰用赞叙。虽在妻子。亦无愧词。藏诸闺门。永以传信。赞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371946'>地万理兮天一极。往无由兮来不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371946_comment'></div>解脱愿兮慈悲力。五色绣兮黄金饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371946_comment'></div>澄氛昏兮圆相开。湛水月兮莲花台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371946_comment'></div>慈眼眷兮犷心回。死别离兮生归来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371946_comment'></div>海为田兮劫为灰。身念念兮无穷哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371946_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1371946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年</a>　吕温卧病三月。本年初春，病中自户部员外郎转司封员外郎。作品：《病中自户部员外郎转司封》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第19页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中自户部员外郎转司封</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18457")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18457'>羸卧承新命，优容获所安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18457'>遣儿迎贺客，无力拂尘冠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18457'>偃仰晴轩暖，支离晓镜寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18457'>那堪报恩去，感激对衰兰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18457'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18457_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年1月</a>　正月二日，改元元和，大赦天下。吕温代司徒杜黄裳作贺赦表。作品：《代杜司徒贺赦表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第44页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代杜司徒贺大赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371872")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371872'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371872_comment'></div>伏奉今月二日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371872_comment'></div>改元元和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371872_comment'></div>大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371872_comment'></div>新云雷之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371872_comment'></div>重日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371872_comment'></div>仁被幽遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371872_comment'></div>庆覃动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371872_comment'></div>三元经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371872_comment'></div>万化惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371872_comment'></div>臣某诚欢诚忭顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371872_comment'></div>臣闻羲轩驭宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371872_comment'></div>尧舜为君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371872_comment'></div>德莫盛于好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371872_comment'></div>政莫宏于在宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371872_comment'></div>然而事资体要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371872_comment'></div>理极精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371872_comment'></div>百王所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371872_comment'></div>千载斯遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371872_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下纂临大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371872_comment'></div>光启睿图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371872_comment'></div>当献岁之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371872_comment'></div>顺阳和之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371872_comment'></div>朝前殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371872_comment'></div>御正门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371872_comment'></div>发德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371872_comment'></div>布慈旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371872_comment'></div>明大孝之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371872_comment'></div>褒至忠之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371872_comment'></div>省役轻税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371872_comment'></div>以清疾苦之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371872_comment'></div>荡累涤瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371872_comment'></div>以厚廉耻之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371872_comment'></div>往典之所未举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371872_comment'></div>前代之所未该。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371872_comment'></div>莫不悉出宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371872_comment'></div>咸归圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371872_comment'></div>坐开仁寿之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371872_comment'></div>行见雍熙之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371872_comment'></div>凡在生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371872_comment'></div>孰不庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371872_comment'></div>况臣陈力滋久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371872_comment'></div>受恩最深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371872_comment'></div>而蒲柳馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371872_comment'></div>犬马多疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371872_comment'></div>不获奉觞丹陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371872_comment'></div>蹈咏康衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371872_comment'></div>犹蒙天眷留圣慈曲至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371872_comment'></div>特降中使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371872_comment'></div>俯加慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371872_comment'></div>衰惫增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371872_comment'></div>枯朽生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371872_comment'></div>施重邱山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371872_comment'></div>感深骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371872_comment'></div>阖门<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1371872", 1371872, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>灰粉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371872_comment'></div>岂足上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371872_comment'></div>无任喜忭屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1371872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年1月</a>　正月，仆射伊慎子宥为安州刺史，吕温代伊慎作谢表。作品：《代伊仆射谢男宥官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第51页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代伊仆射谢男宥授安州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371887")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371887'>臣慎言。伏奉某月日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371887_comment'></div>授臣男宥安州刺史兼侍御史充武昌军兵马留后仍赐紫金鱼袋者。雷惊里巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371887_comment'></div>日照闺门。宠命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371887_comment'></div>战跼无地。臣诚惧诚感顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371887_comment'></div>臣闻惟君任臣。固无虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371887_comment'></div>知子者父。敢私不才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371887_comment'></div>臣顷者伏以圣政惟新。时清无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371887_comment'></div>遂绝指踪之望。求申恋主之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371887_comment'></div>陛下以臣统兵岁深。周涉艰险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371887_comment'></div>长三军之子弟。积百战之疮痍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371887_comment'></div>将有去留。念其情义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371887_comment'></div>理资感励。事贵便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371887_comment'></div>爰敕臣男。试总戎务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371887_comment'></div>臣虽训之以义。教之以忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371887_comment'></div>而钝拙有涯。策磨靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371887_comment'></div>童儿代斲。每怀伤手之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371887_comment'></div>小子在边。曾无折屐之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371887_comment'></div>将何遽膺宠数。荐沐恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371887_comment'></div>真授竹符。就加金组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371887_comment'></div>且祁午之为军尉。父已悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371887_comment'></div>陆抗之将父兵。子非䌽服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371887_comment'></div>岂比臣身居端右。男领方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371887_comment'></div>鸣玉会朝。朱轓行县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371887_comment'></div>焜耀中外。超冠古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371887_comment'></div>名数之乐何加。人臣之事斯极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371887_comment'></div>千载至公之运。独被殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371887_comment'></div>万物咸遂之辰。先蒙曲泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371887_comment'></div>沥肝呈胆。莫尽微诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371887_comment'></div>毁族灭身。宁足上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371887_comment'></div>臣无任感恩陨越之至。谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_18446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18446'>九天飞势在，六月目睛寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_18441'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18441'>年过潘岳才三岁，还见星星两鬓中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18441'>纵使他时能早达，定知不作黑头公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18441_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18441'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_18441_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_18400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18400?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_18400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18400'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_18400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年3月</a>　三月，代司徒杜佑作谢表以上。作品：《代杜司徒谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第44页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代杜司徒让平章事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371879")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371879'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371879_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371879_comment'></div>授臣检校司徒充度支使兼盐铁转运等使依前同中书门下平章事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371879_comment'></div>恩奖殊常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371879_comment'></div>授任非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371879_comment'></div>承旨庆忭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371879_comment'></div>省躬惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371879_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371879_comment'></div>臣素无异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371879_comment'></div>幸逢昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371879_comment'></div>顷因人举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371879_comment'></div>累荷国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371879_comment'></div>声绩靡闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371879_comment'></div>尘忝增惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371879_comment'></div>陛下丕承景命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371879_comment'></div>光阐鸿猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371879_comment'></div>理财阜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371879_comment'></div>尤所注意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371879_comment'></div>臣窃位时久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371879_comment'></div>妨贤愧深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371879_comment'></div>柄用之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371879_comment'></div>甘心自绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371879_comment'></div>岂谓大明私照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371879_comment'></div>元造曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371879_comment'></div>俾参论道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371879_comment'></div>兼领经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371879_comment'></div>当至化鼎新之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371879_comment'></div>在微臣迟暮之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371879_comment'></div>将何以上副宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371879_comment'></div>外弭官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371879_comment'></div>负乘为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371879_comment'></div>冰炭在怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371879_comment'></div>庶遵周任之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371879_comment'></div>敢饰范宣之让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371879_comment'></div>伏惟睿鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371879_comment'></div>俯亮愚诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371879_comment'></div>特降殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371879_comment'></div>赐寝严命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371879_comment'></div>则圣朝无虚授之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371879_comment'></div>微臣遂审己之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371879_comment'></div>遐迩之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371879_comment'></div>孰不知劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371879_comment'></div>无任恳迫屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1371879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年5月</a>　五月中，为韦夏卿撰神道碑铭。作品：《故太子少保赠尚书左仆射京兆韦府君神道碑铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷6第60页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故太子少保赠尚书左仆射京兆韦府君神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371955")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371955'>山之大者。匿峰峦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371955_comment'></div>含气象。积高无倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371955_comment'></div>而不见其险。孕粹有物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371955_comment'></div>如不知其神。此其所以为大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371955_comment'></div>德之全者。毁圭方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371955_comment'></div>黜皎厉。灵机密运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371955_comment'></div>而智不惊愚。遐标特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371955_comment'></div>而迹无变俗。此其所以为全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371955_comment'></div>然则泰山高而可陟。全德近而难知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371955_comment'></div>我求其伦。见之于少保公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371955_comment'></div>公讳某。字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371955_comment'></div>京兆杜陵人。其先帝尧光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371955_comment'></div>让德储庆。建国命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371955_comment'></div>列于夏商。相冑卿族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371955_comment'></div>繁于汉魏。代济不殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371955_comment'></div>焕焉盛门。大王父讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371955_comment'></div>皇朝主客郎中莱济商三州刺史。王父讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371955_comment'></div>仓部郎中太原少尹。赠秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371955_comment'></div>烈考讳某。检校都官郎中岭南节度行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371955_comment'></div>赠同州刺史。或以瑚琏之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371955_comment'></div>才施郡政。或以岩廊之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371955_comment'></div>仅及戎佐。与时俱息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371955_comment'></div>从道而污。屈不试于当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371955_comment'></div>启莫京于身后。公生而岐嶷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371955_comment'></div>弱而老成。浑粹不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371955_comment'></div>清明虚映。朱弦遗音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371955_comment'></div>而宫商自韵。大圭不琢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371955_comment'></div>而符彩溢发。邈矣天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371955_comment'></div>烂乎人文。鼓钟之声日远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371955_comment'></div>乡曲之誉来逼。释褐太子正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371955_comment'></div>与仲弟正卿以贤良偕徵。策入异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371955_comment'></div>冥鸿双举。当代荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371955_comment'></div>授高陵主簿。迁监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371955_comment'></div>改殿中内供奉东都留守判官。即拜东台殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371955_comment'></div>参画惟允。持绳不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371955_comment'></div>河洛之间。风声尚在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371955_comment'></div>德宗躬决庶政。本于尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371955_comment'></div>责成曹郎。综练材实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371955_comment'></div>荐出方伯。时超贰卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371955_comment'></div>二十年间。斯为极选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371955_comment'></div>公由是前后迁刑部吏部员外郎吏部郎中。奏议推美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371955_comment'></div>弥纶成绩。南宫之故事存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371955_comment'></div>于时戡复日近。勋勤者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371955_comment'></div>都市惰游。尽垂金组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371955_comment'></div>邦畿豪夺。半赐丹书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371955_comment'></div>轻禽逸于疏网。悍马骇于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1371955", 1371955, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>柔辔</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371955_comment'></div>上思惩抑。必假良能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371955_comment'></div>公由是前后历奉天长安二县令。仁护鳏茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371955_comment'></div>智钤豪右。舆人之道咏在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371955_comment'></div>望由实济。任以望重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371955_comment'></div>选曹未几。迁给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371955_comment'></div>既居駮正之司。不挠当官之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371955_comment'></div>属东南岁歉。俾乂惟难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371955_comment'></div>出为常州刺史。天宝之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371955_comment'></div>中原释耒。辇越而衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371955_comment'></div>漕吴而食。一隅重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371955_comment'></div>五纪于兹。公临之清贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371955_comment'></div>结以忠恕。固存惠寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371955_comment'></div>务啬勤分。一法以去其侵渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371955_comment'></div>多方以备其灾患。以逸道而使缮完允济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371955_comment'></div>以与道而取赋入先期。声闻天朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371955_comment'></div>考绩连最。转苏州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371955_comment'></div>二境之间。百里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371955_comment'></div>灵源自出。殊派共清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371955_comment'></div>膏泽所沾。异壤同润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371955_comment'></div>下车期月。报政如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371955_comment'></div>加秩赐金。借留累岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371955_comment'></div>无何。彭沛丧师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371955_comment'></div>兵骄地偪。安危所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371955_comment'></div>朝论难之。乃以公检校秘书监兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371955_comment'></div>赐紫金鱼袋。充徐泗节度行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371955_comment'></div>重其威望。将委旄钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371955_comment'></div>而未命程伯。徐方之轨既同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371955_comment'></div>不见贾生。宣室之徵遽至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371955_comment'></div>擢吏部侍郎。伦品甄明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371955_comment'></div>通简节适。势有探汤之热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371955_comment'></div>我以静濯。众有鼓簧之喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371955_comment'></div>我以心听。驯致其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371955_comment'></div>闇然日彰。不求无失职之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371955_comment'></div>人自以为不失职矣。辍拜京兆尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371955_comment'></div>德刑交修。宽猛相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371955_comment'></div>匪设钩距。物无遁情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371955_comment'></div>匪曜锋铓。机无滞断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371955_comment'></div>浩穰之理。不肃而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371955_comment'></div>不求无不欺之吏。吏自以为不能欺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371955_comment'></div>俄改太子宾客。辞剧就閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371955_comment'></div>图南之势一息。选德求旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371955_comment'></div>居东之命惟重。迁检校工部尚书兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371955_comment'></div>充东都留守东都畿汝州都防御使。自盗起幽陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371955_comment'></div>兵屯诸夏。涉淮而北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371955_comment'></div>军国异容。分陕以东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371955_comment'></div>古今殊寄。公讲信修睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371955_comment'></div>外张保釐之政。完备训戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371955_comment'></div>内寓折冲之令。矛戟不露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371955_comment'></div>德耀蔼然。遐迩顿首以承风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371955_comment'></div>强暴革心而知惧。今上嗣统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371955_comment'></div>就加检校吏部尚书。方入谐佥属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371955_comment'></div>毗赞大化。不幸婴疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371955_comment'></div>表求退颐。优诏除太子少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371955_comment'></div>冀其休复。将有后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371955_comment'></div>神祇竟昧。药祷无真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371955_comment'></div>以元和元年三月十二日。薨于东都履信里之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371955_comment'></div>享年六十有四。宠赠尚书左仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371955_comment'></div>輤车西归。制使赙吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371955_comment'></div>太常褒议。谥曰某公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371955_comment'></div>哀荣备矣。夫人河东裴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371955_comment'></div>侍中耀卿之孙。给事中皋之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371955_comment'></div>德门钟美。淑问充塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371955_comment'></div>蕣华早落。蓍兆叶期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1371955_comment'></div>即以是年五月二十一日。合葬于万年县高平乡少陵原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1371955_comment'></div>礼也。公孝悌天至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1371955_comment'></div>行有馀力。仁义性德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1371955_comment'></div>匪俟服膺。不饰表以近明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1371955_comment'></div>每纵心如中矩。清虚简淡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1371955_comment'></div>而应物不倦。通旷夷易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1371955_comment'></div>而及门无杂。不尚意气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1371955_comment'></div>而然诺笃志。不好臧否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1371955_comment'></div>而鉴识超伦。与故相国齐江西映穆宣州赞赞弟侍御史员为文章道义之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1371955_comment'></div>可以视其所亲矣。今吏部郎中扶风窦群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1371955_comment'></div>抗迹毗陵。退身进道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1371955_comment'></div>公三揖郡榻之上。一振天墀之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1371955_comment'></div>不数岁间。蔚为重器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1371955_comment'></div>可以视其所与矣。分正东郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1371955_comment'></div>开府辟土。则有今右司郎中燉煌段平仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1371955_comment'></div>仓部员外郎安定皇甫镈。礼部员外郎清河张贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1371955_comment'></div>洎京兆尹韦词。陇西李景俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1371955_comment'></div>中山卫中行。平阳路随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1371955_comment'></div>皆群彦之秀出。一时之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1371955_comment'></div>可以观其所任矣。加以志尚幽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1371955_comment'></div>冥搜好古。所居第必有松石之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1371955_comment'></div>退公暇日。常以图籍自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1371955_comment'></div>一字惬心。金玉不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1371955_comment'></div>片言同趣。布褐无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1371955_comment'></div>亹亹然若见道之所存。陶陶然不知岁之云晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1371955_comment'></div>于戏。策名从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1371955_comment'></div>四十馀年。朋友罕闻得丧之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1371955_comment'></div>家人莫见喜愠之色。坦怀以处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1371955_comment'></div>推分而行。无怨于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1371955_comment'></div>人亦无怨。无猜于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1371955_comment'></div>物亦无猜。履信顺以优游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1371955_comment'></div>保福禄而终始。其名教之大雅者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1371955_comment'></div>有九子。长曰元贸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1371955_comment'></div>前常州义兴县尉。次曰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1371955_comment'></div>前邠州司仓。次曰璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1371955_comment'></div>乡贡进士。能修词立诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1371955_comment'></div>克家致美。茂扬风训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1371955_comment'></div>休有令闻。其次某某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1371955_comment'></div>皆殊资异识。登于童龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1371955_comment'></div>庆善之馀也。以某获窥墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1371955_comment'></div>见托篆述。究贤人之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1371955_comment'></div>信而无愧。申孝子之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1371955_comment'></div>直而不文。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1371955_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_152_1371955'>利建于商。介圭作宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1371955_comment'></div>爰立于汉。缁衣改造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1371955_comment'></div>克昌厥允。奕世载考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1371955_comment'></div>亚尹擅名。郎中怀道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1371955_comment'></div>莫跻贵仕。莫享难老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1371955_comment'></div>蕴灵储休。以启少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1371955_comment'></div>丕显少保。其德愔愔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1371955_comment'></div>有绰遐姿。旷哉灵襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1371955_comment'></div>显仁山立。藏用渊沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1371955_comment'></div>煦如冬阳。蔼若春阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1371955_comment'></div>白圭三复。克保明心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1371955_comment'></div>黄钟九变。莫匪和音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1371955_comment'></div>静专动直。谦进柔克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1371955_comment'></div>宜践公辅。以桢王国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1371955_comment'></div>促路顿轨。中天堕翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1371955_comment'></div>少陵右原。拱树寒色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1371955_comment'></div>穷壤可敝。唯名不失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1371955_comment'></div>金石垂之。以慰罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1371955_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_170_1371955_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年7月</a>　七月，顺宗葬于丰陵，吕温作歌以挽。作品：《顺宗至德大圣大安孝皇帝挽歌词三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第16页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_sentence_0_18454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18454'>尧功终有待，文德本无忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
