id='poem_sentence_3_18454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18454'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18454_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_18455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18455?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（806年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18455'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18455'>监抚垂三纪，声徽洽万方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18455'>礼因驰道著，明自垦田彰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18455'>积渐承鸿业，从容守太康。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18455'>更留园寝诏，恭听有馀芳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18455'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18455_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_18456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18456?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（806年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18456'>早秋同轨至，晨旆露华滋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18456'>挽度千夫咽，笳凝六马迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18456'>剑悲长闭日，衣望出游时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18456'>风起西陵树，凄凉满孝思。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18456_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年8月</a>　七八月间，代兵部侍郎李巽作表贺德政。作品：《代李侍郎贺德政表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第36页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李侍郎贺德政表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371876")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371876'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371876'>臣某言。臣闻上苍垂象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371876_comment'></div>当分野者先知。元后用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371876_comment'></div>奉职司者方见。是以尧称光被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371876_comment'></div>四岳得于畴咨。舜号文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371876_comment'></div>九官禀其分命。岂非随方表志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371876_comment'></div>因事立言。陈力自参于化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371876_comment'></div>造膝难迷于日用。伏惟皇帝陛下睿图浚发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371876_comment'></div>元德广运。恢纂鸿绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371876_comment'></div>允升大猷。振十圣之遗休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371876_comment'></div>复百王之坠典。至如崇陵尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371876_comment'></div>率礼无违。长信归尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371876_comment'></div>因心则感。内成则仁叙九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371876_comment'></div>外平则义协万邦。厚俗则宠及高年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371876_comment'></div>广孝则荣加锡类。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1371876", 1371876, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>能刑</span>则朝无隐慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371876_comment'></div>善任则野不遗才。修文则戎蛮来威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371876_comment'></div>整武则南北继捷。此皆事悬日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371876_comment'></div>声洽寰区。黔首之所讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371876_comment'></div>搢绅之所抃蹈。其或机参造物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371876_comment'></div>意兆先天。事隔于人谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371876_comment'></div>功隐于朝听者。若非奉职之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371876_comment'></div>官业所及。谅无得而称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371876_comment'></div>臣以庸劣。谬膺寄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371876_comment'></div>调盈虚而驭轻重。关成败而系安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371876_comment'></div>职思其忧。夕惕若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371876_comment'></div>每因罄率。披竭愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371876_comment'></div>出奉温颜。累承睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371876_comment'></div>有以知造化之意。有以见天地之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371876_comment'></div>旷若发蒙。析如愈疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371876_comment'></div>管窥所至。可得而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371876_comment'></div>昨者臣以潮州刺史李璿放纵私盐。耗散公利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371876_comment'></div>请从免职。以儆慢官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371876_comment'></div>陛下以为法令改更。且当申谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371876_comment'></div>道涂悠远。容或未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371876_comment'></div>俾为后图。用缓前责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371876_comment'></div>宏恕包于广大。明察贯于精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371876_comment'></div>此则群臣不可望清光者一也。江南西道观察使杨凭奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371876_comment'></div>以支郡旱歉。经赋不充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371876_comment'></div>请征居地之羡。且循税茶之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371876_comment'></div>陛下以为天灾流行。有时而息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371876_comment'></div>人怨滞结。贻患则深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371876_comment'></div>纵无日新之美。忍复已除之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371876_comment'></div>特令寝奏。姑务通商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371876_comment'></div>有司知画一之方。负贩有昭苏之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371876_comment'></div>此又群臣不可望清光者二也。臣尝使推官殿中侍御史崔太素奉使淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371876_comment'></div>臣以太素名秩甚卑。浚决务重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371876_comment'></div>徵令郡县。釐训役徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371876_comment'></div>须示等威。请赐章服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371876_comment'></div>陛下以为职任伊始。勤效未成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371876_comment'></div>必有可观。乃申后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371876_comment'></div>臣再陈所切。方可其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371876_comment'></div>虽事从权与。且符济物之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371876_comment'></div>而赏不僭行。已见永图之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371876_comment'></div>此又群臣不可望清光者三也。臣对扬之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371876_comment'></div>亲奉德音。知臣使司支计阙少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371876_comment'></div>必拟昭明俭德。振起素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371876_comment'></div>率身为天下之先。节用自中宫而始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371876_comment'></div>又曰。台殿旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371876_comment'></div>己当惕虑。经营改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371876_comment'></div>非所措怀。将不崇三尺之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371876_comment'></div>岂复议十家之产。发自宸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371876_comment'></div>形于天颜。意开而河海自清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371876_comment'></div>言出而神祇知感。此又群臣不可望清光者四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371876_comment'></div>陛下光临大宝。星岁将周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371876_comment'></div>贵戚之赐与无闻。恩倖之沾霈殆绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371876_comment'></div>至于赡军供国。行赏报功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371876_comment'></div>则必鸿毛府库。粪土金玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371876_comment'></div>遂使夏州诸将。恨效浅而恩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371876_comment'></div>剑外三军。知生轻而义重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371876_comment'></div>此又群臣不可望清光者五也。夫唐虞盛烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371876_comment'></div>文武馀风。莫不传诵声诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371876_comment'></div>布在方册。且匹夫匹妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371876_comment'></div>片善必书。飞羽沈鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371876_comment'></div>一祥皆纪。况陛下动关教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371876_comment'></div>言在政刑。理参至道之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371876_comment'></div>躬行盛德之事。而冲虚谦让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371876_comment'></div>郁而未发。将何以光扬艺祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371876_comment'></div>昭示后昆。伏请宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371876_comment'></div>永为大法。臣幸蒙恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371876_comment'></div>获奉昌期。言必亲闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371876_comment'></div>事皆目睹。分深骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371876_comment'></div>义激血诚。轻黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371876_comment'></div>魂宇飞越。无任屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371876_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1371876_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年9月</a>　九月，高崇文奏收成都。吕温代兵部侍郎李巽作贺表。作品：《代李侍郎贺收西川表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第47页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年9月</a>　九月底，代兵部侍郎李巽作表，论伐剑南更发兵事。作品：《代李侍郎论伐剑南更发兵表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第35页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李侍郎论兵表</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371894")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371894'>臣某言。臣伏见某月日诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371894_comment'></div>发更太原凤翔及神策诸镇兵赴剑南东川者。陛下睿算无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371894_comment'></div>神武必断。与人除害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371894_comment'></div>顺天行诛。奋如霆之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371894_comment'></div>乘破竹之势。期于久逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371894_comment'></div>无惮一劳。大正国经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371894_comment'></div>永清时祲。百王盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371894_comment'></div>千古英声。天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371894_comment'></div>然或时事之可否。兵家之利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371894_comment'></div>道途之险易。将帅之宜称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371894_comment'></div>不可不深图远计。原始要终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371894_comment'></div>狂夫有可择之言。愚者有一得之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371894_comment'></div>管窥所至。愿效微诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371894_comment'></div>臣窃以为古今用兵。皆在将勇师和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371894_comment'></div>政齐计胜。不必多兵广众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371894_comment'></div>然后成功。今高崇文等诸将所统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371894_comment'></div>已约一万五千馀人。以整击乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371894_comment'></div>以顺讨逆。授以庙算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371894_comment'></div>假之天威。馘丑挫凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371894_comment'></div>霈有馀力。若更多徵征镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371894_comment'></div>广命师旅。臣窃计之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371894_comment'></div>其患有五。一则高崇文素非大将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371894_comment'></div>拔自偏镇。忠勇虽著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371894_comment'></div>威声未振。本兵既少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371894_comment'></div>兼统则多。将皆权隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371894_comment'></div>士非素抚。虽是锐师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371894_comment'></div>势同乌合。居常则犹可胁致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371894_comment'></div>临敌则何以指挥。非惟崇文才分有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371894_comment'></div>此亦自古兵家所难。臣不敢广引载籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371894_comment'></div>上烦圣听。请直以近事明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371894_comment'></div>哥舒翰潼关之守。郭子仪相州之围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371894_comment'></div>韩全义激水之役。皆以兵多将杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371894_comment'></div>而致败衄。许叔冀之保灵昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371894_comment'></div>李光弼之全河阳。李晟之收复京邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371894_comment'></div>皆以兵少将一。而建大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371894_comment'></div>成败昭然。布在人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371894_comment'></div>二则贞元以来。天下无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371894_comment'></div>四方节将。人各怀安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371894_comment'></div>陛下覆焘惟新。理先清静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371894_comment'></div>今以西南小丑。久稽天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371894_comment'></div>自春徂夏。徵发已广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371894_comment'></div>见在兵力。破贼有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371894_comment'></div>若更务济师。屡闻动众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371894_comment'></div>山崄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1371894", 1371894, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>深阻</span>。暑湿为沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371894_comment'></div>北人南役。谁不惮行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371894_comment'></div>去土离家。动生愁怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371894_comment'></div>往年泾州叛卒。职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371894_comment'></div>事系安危。不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371894_comment'></div>三则吐蕃约盟未定。窥伺在心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371894_comment'></div>间谍往来。急于邮传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371894_comment'></div>又必持两端之计。与刘辟交通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371894_comment'></div>若闻发兵西南。多取边镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371894_comment'></div>秋风即至。虏马已肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371894_comment'></div>冒隙乘虚。必有侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371894_comment'></div>事出万一。悔何可追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371894_comment'></div>四则刘辟穷寇。保险逃死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371894_comment'></div>虽祸淫助顺。天道甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371894_comment'></div>而兵凶战危。人事难必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371894_comment'></div>脱或貔武之师。少不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371894_comment'></div>蜂蚁犹聚。假息旬时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371894_comment'></div>攻守之间。动须应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371894_comment'></div>固当潜锋养锐。以逸待劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371894_comment'></div>今便息兵。后将何继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371894_comment'></div>五则剑川硗塉。居人食且不充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371894_comment'></div>蜀路险艰。饷运无由多致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371894_comment'></div>今屯兵日费。何啻万金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371894_comment'></div>数州麦粟。贵籴将尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371894_comment'></div>千里飞挽。所济几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371894_comment'></div>若更加兵。实难供赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371894_comment'></div>一夫脱有菜色。三军无复斗心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371894_comment'></div>幸可少以成功。何必多而为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371894_comment'></div>今太原及神策等军已上道者。其数颇多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371894_comment'></div>足办戎事。其凤翔等镇未发之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371894_comment'></div>伏乞圣恩。且勒权停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371894_comment'></div>续候事宜。以议行止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371894_comment'></div>臣谬膺重任。过蒙恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371894_comment'></div>辄率狂瞽。轻黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371894_comment'></div>苟利国家。甘心鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371894_comment'></div>无任兢遑恳迫之至。谨奉表陈奏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371894_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1371894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年10月</a>　十月间，代兵部侍郎李巽撰书信。作品：《代李侍郎与山南严仆射书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第26页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李侍郎与山南严仆射书</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371904")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371904'>仆射禀天全才。受国重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371904_comment'></div>控全蜀咽喉之地。当狂寇奔侮之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371904_comment'></div>治瘠土而其材甚丰。训羸师而其武可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371904_comment'></div>少分麾下。潜运掌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371904_comment'></div>再开剑阁之扃。继献盐亭之捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371904_comment'></div>应接制使先假地征。犄角王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371904_comment'></div>且为乡道。削叛臣之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371904_comment'></div>释梓州之围。劳实居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371904_comment'></div>功无与让。圣上神武睿断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371904_comment'></div>注意西南。一校之善否必知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371904_comment'></div>一夫之劳逸必察。况阁下效彰朝论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371904_comment'></div>事布人谣。精诚贯于神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371904_comment'></div>茂伐悬于日月。岂复听簿书之微巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371904_comment'></div>诋笙簧之滥音。来示所虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371904_comment'></div>无足介意。某以寡薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371904_comment'></div>谬膺重任。举关国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371904_comment'></div>动属军期。夙夜忧惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371904_comment'></div>未知所济。过蒙称奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371904_comment'></div>愧惕良深。惟托方岳至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371904_comment'></div>共守王度。物估小事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371904_comment'></div>固无二三。许共遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371904_comment'></div>亦如受赐。佩荷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371904_comment'></div>无喻下情。某再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371904_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1371904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年11月</a>　十一月，代兵部侍郎李巽撰书信。作品：《代李侍郎与徐州张尚书书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第26页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李侍郎与徐州张尚书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371905")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371905'>奉别纸示谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371905_comment'></div>眷待殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371905_comment'></div>规略端明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371905_comment'></div>究忠义之苦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371905_comment'></div>畅经通之雅旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371905_comment'></div>皆足以感动朝野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371905_comment'></div>光映古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371905_comment'></div>一字之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371905_comment'></div>可悬于千金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371905_comment'></div>终身佩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371905_comment'></div>何啻于三复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371905_comment'></div>甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371905_comment'></div>伏以尚书才膺间出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371905_comment'></div>识蕴生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371905_comment'></div>地承勋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371905_comment'></div>行在诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371905_comment'></div>自家达国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371905_comment'></div>移孝为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371905_comment'></div>受任先朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371905_comment'></div>克荷崇构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371905_comment'></div>控喉襟之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371905_comment'></div>成节制之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371905_comment'></div>动必勤王。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371886_comment'></div>今月十三日面奉进旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371886_comment'></div>其南郊赏设钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371886_comment'></div>恐度支支计阙少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371886_comment'></div>以库内钱充者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371886_comment'></div>臣闻王者以四海为家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371889_comment'></div>极其幽赜。冠以睿文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371889_comment'></div>恩示具寮。庆昭万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371889_comment'></div>中谢。臣闻清浊既判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371889_comment'></div>象数相生。一元起于帝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371889_comment'></div>三统成于人道。形器之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371889_comment'></div>推步而得。恍惚之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371889_comment'></div>锱铢不差。有开必先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371889_comment'></div>圣作物睹。伏惟皇帝陛下诞膺骏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371889_comment'></div>敬授人时。爰诏日官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371889_comment'></div>厎定历法。启开元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371889_comment'></div>节宣群生。役五行于文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371889_comment'></div>贯七曜于珠璧。仰观俯察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371889_comment'></div>允协于神休。东作西成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371889_comment'></div>永贞于农候。感动夷夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371889_comment'></div>鼓舞飞沈。天子之大政行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371889_comment'></div>圣人之能事毕矣。臣等幸备朝序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371889_comment'></div>亲奉昌期。窃见天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371889_comment'></div>敢迷日用。无任蹈咏之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371889_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1371889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年2月</a>　二月，代仆射伊慎作状文。作品：《代伊仆射奏请女正度状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第54页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代伊仆射奏请女正度状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（807年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371898")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371898_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1371898_0'>① 光禄大夫尚书右仆射南充郡王臣女请度尼某乙</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371898'>右。臣伏以陛下降诞之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371898_comment'></div>率土蒙幸。臣于含气之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371898_comment'></div>独受深恩。思所以称庆南山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371898_comment'></div>献心北极。遂割骨肉之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371898_comment'></div>俾归空寂之门。结幽愿于金仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371898_comment'></div>奉胜因于宝寿。冒昧上请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371898_comment'></div>精诚匪他。陛下以釐革初行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371898_comment'></div>涣汗无反。怜臣罄至之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371898_comment'></div>事与恩违。念臣愚鲁之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371898_comment'></div>贷于法外。特降中使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371898_comment'></div>俯加慰谕。臣忝居端右之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371898_comment'></div>首干画一之科。诚虽奉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371898_comment'></div>义乖率下。合当严谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371898_comment'></div>忽被殊私。震惊失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371898_comment'></div>惭跼罔据。荷降鉴之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371898_comment'></div>原情斯在。蒙曲全之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371898_comment'></div>为感则深。辄渎宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371898_comment'></div>伏增陨越。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371898_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1371898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年3月</a>　三月，窦群由吏部郎中迁御史中丞，吕温代其上书襄州刺史于頔。作品：《代窦中丞与襄阳于相公书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第28页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代窦中丞与襄阳于相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371903")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371903'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371903'>某经术无取。丘园自屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371903_comment'></div>所期全拙。岂敢近名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371903_comment'></div>二十五丈汎爱博容。不遗孤陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371903_comment'></div>申以通家之好。遇以国士之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371903_comment'></div>分惭入堂。契辱忘年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371903_comment'></div>猥蒙吹嘘。谬假鳞翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371903_comment'></div>遂得价重江左。名闻天朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371903_comment'></div>起家拾遗。再命柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371903_comment'></div>时丁变故。命偶屯艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371903_comment'></div>孤鳞方困于蹄涔。穷鸟思归于仁德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371903_comment'></div>果蒙奏领列郡。擢倅三军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371903_comment'></div>不汝疵瑕。见容于岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371903_comment'></div>同我休戚。每形于话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371903_comment'></div>身计皆奉良规。家事悉资全力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371903_comment'></div>然后表达宸听。推致周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371903_comment'></div>南宫剧曹。践不终岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371903_comment'></div>宪府雄秩。拔于常伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371903_comment'></div>内顾庸虚。敢云自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371903_comment'></div>魏贤子夏。宣尼之道弥彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371903_comment'></div>汉用淮阴。相国之言始重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371903_comment'></div>徒以才负知已。名悬古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371903_comment'></div>致远之效莫彰。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1371903", 1371903, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>贻羞</span>之责斯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371903_comment'></div>敢不砥砺微分。激昂前途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371903_comment'></div>以明主今日之恩。资大贤积时之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371903_comment'></div>庶乎有立。少答所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371903_comment'></div>岂敢以尺素为荣。而负平生之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371903_comment'></div>伏惟有以鉴察。郡榻诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371903_comment'></div>戎旃故吏。推奖恩重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371903_comment'></div>生成感深。瞻望门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371903_comment'></div>未获拜谢。铭戴兢惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371903_comment'></div>莫知所裁。拳拳下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371903_comment'></div>纸墨难具。某再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371903_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1371903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年10月</a>　十月底，代李巽上表贺生擒李锜。作品：《代李尚书贺生擒李锜表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第49页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李尚书贺生擒李锜表</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371874")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371874'>臣某言。臣得某官某乙状报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371874_comment'></div>伏承今月十二日夜。浙西将士张子良等相率效顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371874_comment'></div>生擒李锜者。天讨有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371874_comment'></div>国无稽诛。夷夏同欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371874_comment'></div>飞沈咸跃。臣某中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371874_comment'></div>臣闻炎气方蒸。伏阴不能藏其沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371874_comment'></div>必疑战发泄。以彰正阳之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371874_comment'></div>至化方融。大奸无所隐其慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371874_comment'></div>必陵犯诛夷。以耀圣人之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371874_comment'></div>沴不尽消。生德不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371874_comment'></div>奸不尽发。圣功不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371874_comment'></div>盖自然之明徵。而必至之恒理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371874_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下光膺峻命。恢纂鸿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371874_comment'></div>仁育群生。义征不譓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371874_comment'></div>无与让而诞修文德。不得已而有此武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371874_comment'></div>日者周岁之间。大刑再举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371874_comment'></div>朔陲叛将。献首于九庙之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371874_comment'></div>益部凶渠。伏锧于万人之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371874_comment'></div>被发左衽。且犹知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371874_comment'></div>肖形含气。孰不革心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371874_comment'></div>贼锜身齿人伦。家承国籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371874_comment'></div>三朝任遇。五族光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371874_comment'></div>而独藏祸谋。密聚奸党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371874_comment'></div>枭琳之牙旗尚在。忽巳发狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371874_comment'></div>戮辟之刃血未乾。敢兹拒命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371874_comment'></div>陛下重难戎事。深悯远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371874_comment'></div>先示招谕。后加讨伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371874_comment'></div>方伯严兵。有司调食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371874_comment'></div>经略才下。形势巳张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371874_comment'></div>果得义勇叶心。鬼神假手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371874_comment'></div>大旆回指。长戟合围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371874_comment'></div>兵火之气天运。金鼓之声海动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371874_comment'></div>曾不终夜。遂擒元凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371874_comment'></div>巷有居人。市无改肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371874_comment'></div>滔天之逆。踰月而平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371874_comment'></div>去岁西征。则善阵不战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371874_comment'></div>今兹东伐。则善师不阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371874_comment'></div>有以见睿略天纵。神武日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371874_comment'></div>圣道久而投刃皆虚。德泽深而用力弥寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371874_comment'></div>从此氛穷沴尽。俗变风移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371874_comment'></div>百蛮成冠带之乡。五兵为耒耜之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371874_comment'></div>溥天同轨。比屋可封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371874_comment'></div>古今一时。尧舜何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371874_comment'></div>臣谬膺重寄。时荷殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371874_comment'></div>载逢河海之清。三睹鲸鲵之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371874_comment'></div>志深除恶。义切同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371874_comment'></div>欢忭之诚。倍万恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371874_comment'></div>无任手舞足蹈屏营之至。谨奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371874_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1371874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年10月</a>　十月底后，代武元衡作谢表。作品：《代武相公谢枪旗器甲鞍马表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第50页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span>《代武相公谢借飞龙马表》<span "吕温", "poem_title_1371875")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371875'>臣元衡言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371875_comment'></div>今日中使某乙至臣宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371875_comment'></div>奉宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371875_comment'></div>赐臣枪旗器甲鞍马并锦彩等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371875_comment'></div>礼殊其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371875_comment'></div>物备其容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371875_comment'></div>肃以将威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371875_comment'></div>焕以昭宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371875_comment'></div>云泽濡体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371875_comment'></div>天光照门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371875_comment'></div>抃骇失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371875_comment'></div>兢惶罔据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371875_comment'></div>臣某诚荷诚感顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371875_comment'></div>臣才无可取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371875_comment'></div>进不因人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371875_comment'></div>陛下怜其小心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371875_comment'></div>知其尽节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371875_comment'></div>特纡宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371875_comment'></div>谬委台司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371875_comment'></div>匡辅之益无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371875_comment'></div>将明之效靡著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371875_comment'></div>方俟严谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371875_comment'></div>忽被殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371875_comment'></div>寄重西南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371875_comment'></div>任兼中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371875_comment'></div>封开大郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371875_comment'></div>秩正黄枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371875_comment'></div>登坛于六符之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371875_comment'></div>被衮为三军之帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371875_comment'></div>古今盛典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371875_comment'></div>尽在兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371875_comment'></div>人臣宠贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371875_comment'></div>并集微躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371875_comment'></div>岂臣孱庸所克负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371875_comment'></div>非臣陨越所能上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371875_comment'></div>重锦名马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371875_comment'></div>元甲朱旂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371875_comment'></div>王事靡盬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371875_comment'></div>俨有行色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371875_comment'></div>天颜咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371875_comment'></div>忽当远离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371875_comment'></div>感恋徬徨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371875_comment'></div>拜受涕咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371875_comment'></div>折冲分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371875_comment'></div>愧非式遏之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371875_comment'></div>荣耀自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371875_comment'></div>猥辱专征之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371875_comment'></div>无任感恩激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371875_comment'></div>谨奉表陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1371875_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1371881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代武相公谢借飞龙马表</a><span class='authorDate'>（807年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371881")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371881'>臣元衡言。伏蒙圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371881_comment'></div>借飞龙马若干匹。至京兆府界首者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371881_comment'></div>臣谬处台司。将明薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371881_comment'></div>自忝方任。恩礼特加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371881_comment'></div>奖谕绸缪。宠锡辉焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371881_comment'></div>寒衣病药。悉出圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371881_comment'></div>匹马一人。咸经御选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371881_comment'></div>远览图史。近徵耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371881_comment'></div>如臣蒙幸。未见其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371881_comment'></div>实有何功。敢当斯遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371881_comment'></div>尽节竭诚。在臣子之本分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371881_comment'></div>杀身致命。报君亲之常道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371881_comment'></div>竟将何力。上答殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371881_comment'></div>空保丹诚。以致灰粉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371881_comment'></div>王程靡处。天驷言旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371881_comment'></div>仰服皂之有期。恨违颜之方始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371881_comment'></div>精魂自越。顾步莫留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371881_comment'></div>权奇之姿。向云阙以骧首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371881_comment'></div>悃款之恋。与星影而共驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371881_comment'></div>瞻望天庭。罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371881_comment'></div>无任感戴彷徨之至。谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371881_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1371881_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年11月</a>　十一月，制放浙西租赋，吕温代文武百僚上表以贺。作品：《代文武百僚贺放浙西租赋表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第42页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年12月</a>　十二月，制许百僚游宴，不得奏报。吕温代百僚上谢表。作品：《代文武百僚谢许游宴表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第42页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　下半年，代辛将军作书。作品：《代辛将军与普润刘尚书书》<span
