"poem_title_1371906")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371906'>某性质鄙昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371906_comment'></div>智能无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371906_comment'></div>承藉门绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371906_comment'></div>早蒙驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371906_comment'></div>尽瘁军府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371906_comment'></div>备尝艰险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371906_comment'></div>徒竭犬马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371906_comment'></div>讵济弓裘之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371906_comment'></div>家构未克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371906_comment'></div>国恩未酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371906_comment'></div>而谬典禁司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371906_comment'></div>职惟侍卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371906_comment'></div>良时自晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371906_comment'></div>宿志莫申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371906_comment'></div>愤血犹刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371906_comment'></div>忧发先白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371906_comment'></div>加以禀性寡合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371906_comment'></div>知音实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371906_comment'></div>甘心此生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371906_comment'></div>长鸣靡托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371906_comment'></div>岂料尚书推宏深之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371906_comment'></div>启特达之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371906_comment'></div>爱念不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371906_comment'></div>眷知益重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371906_comment'></div>昨者四牡来觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371906_comment'></div>万乘虚襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371906_comment'></div>旁求将帅之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371906_comment'></div>伫清至公之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371906_comment'></div>然则萧何之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371906_comment'></div>必在韩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371906_comment'></div>孝文有问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371906_comment'></div>宜荐云中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371906_comment'></div>而丹墀对扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371906_comment'></div>首及庸琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371906_comment'></div>敷陈本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371906_comment'></div>奖饰逾涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371906_comment'></div>达其忠义之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371906_comment'></div>许其远大之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371906_comment'></div>虽躬论志业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371906_comment'></div>自沥肺肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371906_comment'></div>纤悉周详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371906_comment'></div>岂能及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371906_comment'></div>遂使郁堙之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371906_comment'></div>允达于宸聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371906_comment'></div>樗朽之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371906_comment'></div>式孚于帝念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371906_comment'></div>言发九天之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371906_comment'></div>声闻四海之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371906_comment'></div>行得舟航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371906_comment'></div>坐生羽翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371906_comment'></div>虽管鲍在齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371906_comment'></div>载深知我之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371906_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1371906", 1371906, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>王贡</span>仕汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371906_comment'></div>有切弹冠之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371906_comment'></div>方诸今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371906_comment'></div>未足为喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371906_comment'></div>不图知己之至于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371906_comment'></div>义激血诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371906_comment'></div>恩缠骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371906_comment'></div>每一念至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371906_comment'></div>不觉涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371906_comment'></div>殒首糜躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371906_comment'></div>岂能报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371906_comment'></div>唯当竭诚砥节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371906_comment'></div>服义怀仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371906_comment'></div>奉以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371906_comment'></div>居之造次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371906_comment'></div>贞松得地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371906_comment'></div>方见于岁寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371906_comment'></div>皦日在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371906_comment'></div>愿明其心誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371906_comment'></div>死生幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371906_comment'></div>属有负薪之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371906_comment'></div>未申拜赐之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371906_comment'></div>瞻荷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371906_comment'></div>感惧兼深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371906_comment'></div>拳拳下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371906_comment'></div>未知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371906_comment'></div>稍任行李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371906_comment'></div>即冀趋谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371906_comment'></div>伏惟照察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1371906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　本年，代兵部侍郎李巽作贺表。作品：《代李侍郎贺雨雪感应表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第48页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年1月</a>　春，正月，群臣上尊号曰睿圣文武皇帝。吕温代百僚上尊号表。作品：《代文武百官上尊号第三表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第41页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年2月</a>　二月左右，吕温代百僚进农书表。作品：《代文武百僚进农书表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷4第43页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年4月</a>　四月，崔琮卒，吕温为其撰行状。作品：《唐故银青光禄大夫、守工部尚书致仕上柱国、中山郡开国公、食邑二千户、赠陕州大都督博陵崔公行状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第56页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕上柱国中山郡开国公食邑二千户赠陕州大都督博陵崔公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371962")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371962'>唐故银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕上柱国中山郡开国公食邑二千户赠陕州大都督博陵崔公。曾祖讳承福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝太中大夫广越二府都督。祖讳先意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝朝议大夫邓州刺史。父讳巘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝朝议大夫郑州长史。赠左散骑常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371962_comment'></div>状。斧藻天理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371962_comment'></div>立为人极。敬终端本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371962_comment'></div>彼所以将就诚明。褒殁劝存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371962_comment'></div>此所以砥砺名教。然而以道行巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371962_comment'></div>晦而弥光。大君子之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371962_comment'></div>以法考行。直而无党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371962_comment'></div>贤有司之职也。且曰献状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371962_comment'></div>则惟所知。公讳淙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371962_comment'></div>清臧而和。博厚而敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371962_comment'></div>岐嶷而夙茂。羁丱而老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371962_comment'></div>情约性充。静专动直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371962_comment'></div>出入孝悌。周旋忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371962_comment'></div>始以经明上第。调佐夏阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371962_comment'></div>次以词丽甲科。超尉王屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371962_comment'></div>事迫于官而举。言迫于事而扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371962_comment'></div>欲藏智而蒙滞来求。不近名而声华见逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371962_comment'></div>故相左仆射张公时尹洛京。首得才实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371962_comment'></div>洎镇荆蜀。致于幕庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371962_comment'></div>再兼理官。专领记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371962_comment'></div>捷笔良画。三邦有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371962_comment'></div>旋遘内艰。毁瘠仅立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371962_comment'></div>善居得礼。族党称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371962_comment'></div>免丧之岁。天子南狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371962_comment'></div>大尉西平王大会兵车。将图匡复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371962_comment'></div>公首膺辟命。浚发义心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371962_comment'></div>琴未成声。屦及于路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371962_comment'></div>感激而将星芒怒。谋谟而兵祲廓清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371962_comment'></div>翠华既还。优典斯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371962_comment'></div>拜殿中侍御史。时有宠臣为京兆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371962_comment'></div>政以暴闻。吏有冤弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371962_comment'></div>公表陈枉直。伏阁待旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371962_comment'></div>言忠主悟。事寝风生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371962_comment'></div>以绳违称职。转侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371962_comment'></div>以求瘼慎选。为华原令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371962_comment'></div>大兵之后。旱岁为虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371962_comment'></div>公劳徕不倦。弛张以宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371962_comment'></div>复流庸于润屋。辟旷土为多稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371962_comment'></div>俄改歙州刺史。地杂瓯骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371962_comment'></div>号为难理。下车而简其约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371962_comment'></div>期月而明其信誓。然后破散溪聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371962_comment'></div>剪锄山豪。既去害群之奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371962_comment'></div>遂宁挺险之俗。徵拜长安县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371962_comment'></div>威声先路。不肃而理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371962_comment'></div>铓刃馀地。所投皆虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371962_comment'></div>擢同州刺史。图歉于丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371962_comment'></div>量赈为籴。号里仓者三百所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371962_comment'></div>而凶年备矣。戒以暴骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371962_comment'></div>谕之速朽。成薄葬者九百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371962_comment'></div>而奢俗惩矣。群人有豪夺乡茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371962_comment'></div>阴持吏失。朋搆讼狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371962_comment'></div>累政患之。公断以寻斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371962_comment'></div>破其囊橐。人乐其杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371962_comment'></div>而法制行焉。郡城自御寇之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371962_comment'></div>复隍殆尽。朝贡所经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371962_comment'></div>夷夏何仰。公悦使襁负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371962_comment'></div>大兴版筑。下不知役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371962_comment'></div>而扃固立焉。其馀则去思有碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371962_comment'></div>详在篆述。可覆视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371962_comment'></div>朝议陟明。迁于陕服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371962_comment'></div>封介晋楚。寄分函洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371962_comment'></div>而戎备不修。兵库虚闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371962_comment'></div>公乃鸠工以利器。阅实以练卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371962_comment'></div>金革中度。义勇知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371962_comment'></div>既而有淮西之役。晨命暮具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371962_comment'></div>凛然而可观矣。河出城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371962_comment'></div>造舟为梁。经费僝工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371962_comment'></div>败决相继。公乃沉石而双固中沚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371962_comment'></div>省舰而三分巨流。水与意会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371962_comment'></div>势若天成。既而有奔涛之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371962_comment'></div>智胜功显。终然而无害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371962_comment'></div>其馀则三降玺书。就加爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371962_comment'></div>是明徵也。移疾入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371962_comment'></div>贰职冬官。归载不过图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371962_comment'></div>留府盈乎粟帛。丰公约私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371962_comment'></div>于是乎在。既至陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371962_comment'></div>以尚书致仕。室不交要路之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371962_comment'></div>口不言当代之事。就阴委顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371962_comment'></div>谈者多之。公自解巾至于撤乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371962_comment'></div>思不踰矩。动无越思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371962_comment'></div>以忠贞为仕模。以勤俭为家训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371962_comment'></div>身居侯邸。清节如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371962_comment'></div>男降王姬。素风愈励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371962_comment'></div>羁孤聚室。人各忘其亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371962_comment'></div>布褐分庭。士不知其贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371962_comment'></div>体温柔而事至能断。性坦易而物莫能窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371962_comment'></div>当官不务于名声。所去必遗其功利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371962_comment'></div>氓谣尚在。时论可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371962_comment'></div>巳踰书葬之期。谨举易名之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371962_comment'></div>谨状。元和三年四月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371962_comment'></div>故银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕赠陕州大都督博陵崔公从外甥朝议郎行尚书司封员外郎上骑都尉赐绯鱼袋吕温谨上尚书考功。夫立身之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371962_comment'></div>始于君亲。中于其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371962_comment'></div>终于其身。若府君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371962_comment'></div>居丧有闻。临难有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371962_comment'></div>善其始也。勤于官业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371962_comment'></div>惠于鳏寡。敬其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371962_comment'></div>家事以理。年至而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371962_comment'></div>谨其终也。率是三懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371962_comment'></div>光于前训。以咨谥法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371962_comment'></div>无愧至公。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371962_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_103_1371962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年4月</a>　本年四月，吕温仍守官司封员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　四月至十月间，吕温自司封员外郎转刑部郎中，兼侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　夏，张弘靖有《直夜思闻雅琴》诗，吕温、张籍、权德舆、李益和之。鲍溶继有和作。作品：《奉和张舍人阁中直夜思闻雅琴因书事通简僚友》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第5页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和张舍人阁中直夜思闻雅琴因书事通简僚友</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18471")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_18471_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_18471'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4799, "poem_allusion_18471")'>南薰</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4963, "poem_allusion_18471")'>禁垣清切</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_18471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18471'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18471'>迢递天上直，寂寞丘中琴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18471'>忆尔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_18471", 18471, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>山水韵</span>，起予仁智心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18471'>凝情在正始，超想疏烦襟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18471'>凉生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_18471", 18471, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>子夜</span>后，月照禁垣深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18471'>远风霭兰气，微露清桐阴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18471'>方袭缁衣庆，永奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4799, "poem_sentence_5_18471")'>南薰</span>吟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18471'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_18471_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年9月</a>　九月十二日，肃宗第二女大长公主薨，吕温撰墓志铭。作品：《大唐故纪国大长公主墓志铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷7第76页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐故纪国大长公主墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371959")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371959'>公主讳某。字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371959_comment'></div>睿宗大圣真皇帝之曾孙。玄宗明皇帝之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371959_comment'></div>肃宗宣皇帝之第二女也。皇唐骏启成明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371959_comment'></div>再造生人。定四海以为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371959_comment'></div>统三灵而传庆。介圭作瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371959_comment'></div>外强磐石之宗。汤沐疏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371959_comment'></div>内广关雎之化。兰芬玉振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371959_comment'></div>垂二百年。公主女宿降神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371959_comment'></div>坤元毓粹。荷文武之馀烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371959_comment'></div>资任姒之积德。禀灵胎教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371959_comment'></div>丽浦之生夜光。钟美天姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371959_comment'></div>䌽云之捧朝日。生知信顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371959_comment'></div>长习诗礼。士女之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371959_comment'></div>有闻必践。保姆之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371959_comment'></div>不肃而成。乾元二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371959_comment'></div>年若干。许笄从周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371959_comment'></div>筑馆于鲁。辎軿将其百两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371959_comment'></div>环佩出乎九重。以降于驸马都尉荥阳郑君曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371959_comment'></div>官至特进左散骑常侍。博学能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371959_comment'></div>善交好施。门多长者之辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371959_comment'></div>室有圣人之书。朝野钦叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371959_comment'></div>名声籍甚。公主辅佐君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371959_comment'></div>周旋礼经。尽志以奉舅姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371959_comment'></div>降心以谐姻族。夙兴夜寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371959_comment'></div>能服浣濯之衣。殷祭大宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371959_comment'></div>必躬蕴藻之事。恒自砥砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371959_comment'></div>未尝以箫歌废日。动循法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371959_comment'></div>曾不以嚬笑为容。事叶母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371959_comment'></div>言成内则。考诸图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371959_comment'></div>罕见其伦。洎乎曳杖晨歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371959_comment'></div>帷堂昼哭。誓柏舟之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371959_comment'></div>尽袪繁华。洗清莲之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371959_comment'></div>坐归空寂。一男曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371959_comment'></div>茂学懿文。夙成时秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371959_comment'></div>选尚顺宗次女普安长公主。拜驸马都尉秘书少监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371959_comment'></div>其择邻之义笃欤。一女字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371959_comment'></div>淑质妙工。婉为邦媛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371959_comment'></div>适将作少监武功苏某。其结缡之戒明欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371959_comment'></div>于戏。以顺成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371959_comment'></div>柔立之操。茂正家道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371959_comment'></div>宣美国风。历奉五朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371959_comment'></div>殆将六纪。赐金之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371959_comment'></div>无恃宠以私求。食租之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371959_comment'></div>不与人以争利。淑慎吾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371959_comment'></div>聿观厥终。信戚里之高标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371959_comment'></div>天人之秀出者也。宜其崇享五福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371959_comment'></div>远逾三寿。辅时阴教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371959_comment'></div>为国女师。竟昧与善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371959_comment'></div>忽焉遘疾。御医驰诊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371959_comment'></div>阴阳之⿱<span class='inlineComment2'>（冖祋）</span>已深。中使相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371959_comment'></div>药祷之诚无及。以元和二年九月十二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371959_comment'></div>薨于长兴里之私第。享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371959_comment'></div>少监驸马痛殷创巨。杖起成丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371959_comment'></div>以三年某日月哀奉裳帷。合祔于某县某原先常侍之旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371959_comment'></div>礼也。以某学于<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺）</span>旧见托斯铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371959_comment'></div>姑阅之盛<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>其文曰。奕奕纪国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371959_comment'></div>发祥圣源。祖武宗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371959_comment'></div>父乾母坤。肃宗爱女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371959_comment'></div>玄宗贵孙。伣天之妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371959_comment'></div>大历加恩。问我诸姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371959_comment'></div>实惟贞元。迄于我皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371959_comment'></div>圣敬弥敦。纪国之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371959_comment'></div>如玉其温。纪国之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371959_comment'></div>如何浑浑。哲夫令望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371959_comment'></div>身殁道存。有子克家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371959_comment'></div>鸣玉晨昏。冢妇之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371959_comment'></div>普安在门。人生极休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371959_comment'></div>胡可胜言。礼为藩兮俭为宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371959_comment'></div>神所劳兮宜寿考。俨高堂兮去何早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371959_comment'></div>风白杨兮露秋草。出青门兮墓田道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371959_comment'></div>镂德音于沉础。传风树于遗老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371959_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1371959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月</a>　十月，为杜黄裳夫人撰墓志铭。作品：《故河中节度使检校司空平章事杜公夫人李氏墓志铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷7第77页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故河中节度使检校司空平章事杜公夫人李氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371961")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371961'>粤元和三年岁在八月某朔某日。河中晋绛等州节度使检校司空平章事邠国公夫人赵郡李氏薨于公宫之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371961_comment'></div>享年若干。有子五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371961_comment'></div>长曰载。河南府功曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371961_comment'></div>次曰翁归。前太常寺奉礼郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371961_comment'></div>次曰宝符。前河南府参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371961_comment'></div>次曰义符。宏文馆明经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371961_comment'></div>有女二人。长适监察御史武功苏德舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371961_comment'></div>次适故相国崖州员外司马京兆韦公执谊。命载等以其年十月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371961_comment'></div>奉輤车裳帷。备春秋葬君夫人之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371961_comment'></div>卜定于某县之某原。俾门下士刑部郎中兼侍御史东平吕某著之于志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371961_comment'></div>李著姓也。其因生启允之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371961_comment'></div>若旸谷出日。岷山导江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371961_comment'></div>光流派别。百代可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371961_comment'></div>赵之东祖。尤贵州乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371961_comment'></div>缨组蝉联。布在家牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371961_comment'></div>太宗革昏隋室。毓德秦邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371961_comment'></div>裒衣侍学。十有八士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371961_comment'></div>夫人之高祖天策府仓曹参军曰守素在焉。与申公士廉刊定氏族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371961_comment'></div>该明条贯。天下宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371961_comment'></div>大王父稷山令讳延祖。王父赵城丞讳仲将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371961_comment'></div>考菀邱令讳映。皆以懿文通经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371961_comment'></div>雅度清节。卒负天爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371961_comment'></div>沦于下寮。泌之洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371961_comment'></div>亦流恺悌。夫人即菀邱府君之第五女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371961_comment'></div>积善馀庆。未归后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371961_comment'></div>自他有耀。女德挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371961_comment'></div>常山炳其阴灵。大陆资乎秀气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371961_comment'></div>在娠而卜。光有贵繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371961_comment'></div>垂发之岁。蔚其德容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371961_comment'></div>蕴沉明之识。含柔立之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371961_comment'></div>生知敬爱。性合图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371961_comment'></div>顾复长之。如滋芳兰之易茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371961_comment'></div>姆师教之。如琢美玉之易成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371961_comment'></div>年甫二十。归我邠公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371961_comment'></div>爰自缘衣。至于陶翟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371961_comment'></div>率履一贯。星纪四周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371961_comment'></div>尽瘁德义之门。辅建公侯之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371961_comment'></div>祭服非手出不荐。宾馈非躬具不陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371961_comment'></div>非门内之事不询。非女工之物不视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371961_comment'></div>言契诗教。动归礼防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371961_comment'></div>不失信于儿童。无惰容于闇室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371961_comment'></div>抚宁孤贱。膏雨之沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371961_comment'></div>叶比宗姻。阳春之感畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371961_comment'></div>式是家道。刑于国风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371961_comment'></div>盖母仪之高标。内则之全致者巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371961_comment'></div>宜其风信顺之祐。迈期颐之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371961_comment'></div>抱孙高堂。视子华发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371961_comment'></div>而未跻中寿。未极殊休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371961_comment'></div>辍琴瑟于春堂。委繁华于朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371961_comment'></div>莫诉之酷。可胜言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371961_comment'></div>夫人始封赞皇县君。进封真定郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371961_comment'></div>又为真定夫人。从夫之贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371961_comment'></div>夫人始家蒲城。司空委禽之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371961_comment'></div>实参汾阳王军事。数十年外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371961_comment'></div>来为小君。鱼轩昼游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371961_comment'></div>里闬如旧。稀代之荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371961_comment'></div>呜呼。荣与阅水俱逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371961_comment'></div>贵与朽壤同堙。唯柔芳与懿问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371961_comment'></div>贯终古而不泯。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371961_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1371961'>仁为源。义为藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371961_comment'></div>启华冑。立清门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371961_comment'></div>代济美兮。娟清明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371961_comment'></div>昵柔启。月之出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371961_comment'></div>桃之华。天钟是兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371961_comment'></div>容在礼。言顾诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371961_comment'></div>工务本。德从宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371961_comment'></div>佐君子兮。富而约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371961_comment'></div>贵而降。宜象服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371961_comment'></div>封大邦。邈未始兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371961_comment'></div>荣何晚。落何先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371961_comment'></div>郁遐庆。摧中年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371961_comment'></div>懵神理兮。迁于堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371961_comment'></div>祖于庭。篆幽础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371961_comment'></div>閟泉扃。永垂范兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371961_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1371961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月</a>　十月，为刘澭撰神道碑铭。作品：《唐故金紫光禄大夫检校兵部尚书使持节都督秦州诸军事、兼秦州刺史、御史大夫，充保义军节度陇西经略军等使、上柱国彭城军开国公、食邑二千户、赠尚书右仆射中山刘公神道碑铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷6第63页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故金紫光禄大夫检校兵部尚书使持节都督秦州诸军事兼秦州刺史御史大夫充保义军节度陇西经略军等使上柱国彭城郡开国公食邑二千户赠尚书右仆射中山刘公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371956")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371956'>武有七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371956_comment'></div>以先九伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371956_comment'></div>圣王所以经邦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371956_comment'></div>战有六器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371956_comment'></div>以先五兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371956_comment'></div>贤侯所以述职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371956_comment'></div>然德威并运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371956_comment'></div>仁勇相宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371956_comment'></div>功业见乎礼义之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371956_comment'></div>将帅出乎诗书之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371956_comment'></div>若有览古成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371956_comment'></div>与时行藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371956_comment'></div>道惟忠贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371956_comment'></div>权利变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371956_comment'></div>兵机生于尽性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371956_comment'></div>师律本乎修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371956_comment'></div>饰怒之鈇钺有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371956_comment'></div>当仁之疆场不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371956_comment'></div>考诸名实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371956_comment'></div>何代无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371956_comment'></div>公讳澭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371956_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371956_comment'></div>其先帝尧之允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371956_comment'></div>事夏后者曰累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371956_comment'></div>随会之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371956_comment'></div>处咸阳者为刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371956_comment'></div>秦灭六雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371956_comment'></div>迁于丰沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371956_comment'></div>汉有四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371956_comment'></div>别封河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371956_comment'></div>公即孝景帝子中山靖王胜之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371956_comment'></div>遭晋丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371956_comment'></div>流寓幽平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371956_comment'></div>旧燕赵之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371956_comment'></div>不绝如线。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371956_comment'></div>十一代祖后魏尚书左仆射燕郡公灵助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371956_comment'></div>始有大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371956_comment'></div>建兹元社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371956_comment'></div>遂为范阳人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371956_comment'></div>厥后逶迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371956_comment'></div>世有潜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371956_comment'></div>详在家牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371956_comment'></div>略而不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371956_comment'></div>曾祖特进检校司卫卿临洮军使赠宋州刺史讳宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371956_comment'></div>恢持重之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371956_comment'></div>抚宁洮罕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371956_comment'></div>王父特进检校右金吾卫大将军太常大斗军使赠扬州大都督讳贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371956_comment'></div>厉摧坚之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371956_comment'></div>震叠互羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371956_comment'></div>烈考开府仪同三司幽州大都督府长史带正省兵吏刑户四尚书左右仆射平章事兼御史大夫幽州卢龙军节度使累赠太师太保讳怦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371956_comment'></div>以正有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371956_comment'></div>以宽得众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371956_comment'></div>书伐盟府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371956_comment'></div>拥旄本邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371956_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371956_comment'></div>以二特进之志略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371956_comment'></div>用而不贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371956_comment'></div>以太保之忠勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371956_comment'></div>贵而不寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371956_comment'></div>水积而深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371956_comment'></div>纵壑之鳞跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371956_comment'></div>风积而厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371956_comment'></div>垂天之翼奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371956_comment'></div>庆灵久郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371956_comment'></div>必有勃兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371956_comment'></div>公即先太保之次子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371956_comment'></div>今侍中之介弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371956_comment'></div>伯也嗣职幽都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371956_comment'></div>仲也扬威陇坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371956_comment'></div>虎旂龙节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371956_comment'></div>交萃于一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371956_comment'></div>开国承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371956_comment'></div>并登于九陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371956_comment'></div>倬绝天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371956_comment'></div>辉动人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371956_comment'></div>勃焉之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371956_comment'></div>斯可信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371956_comment'></div>公长源浚发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371956_comment'></div>自天钟美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371956_comment'></div>直尾箕之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371956_comment'></div>别禀精英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371956_comment'></div>生峘崵之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371956_comment'></div>得其全气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371956_comment'></div>显仁藏智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371956_comment'></div>勤孝朴忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371956_comment'></div>大略小心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371956_comment'></div>寡言敏行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371956_comment'></div>虎抱崖屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371956_comment'></div>莫能象其深沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371956_comment'></div>鹗声青冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371956_comment'></div>未足拟其超远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371956_comment'></div>幼挺奇节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371956_comment'></div>长有雄姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371956_comment'></div>森武库之锋铓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371956_comment'></div>错文昌之光色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371956_comment'></div>悦礼之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371956_comment'></div>惇诗之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371956_comment'></div>观易象之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371956_comment'></div>得春秋之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371956_comment'></div>申商之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371956_comment'></div>摭实而除苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371956_comment'></div>孙吴之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371956_comment'></div>取权而去诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371956_comment'></div>行有馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371956_comment'></div>则遣词比兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371956_comment'></div>多中于雅音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371956_comment'></div>材之旁通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371956_comment'></div>则骑射剑击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371956_comment'></div>皆穷其妙用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1371956_comment'></div>真所谓多能博识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1371956_comment'></div>允武允文者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1371956_comment'></div>公弱冠之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1371956_comment'></div>朱滔败归幽陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1371956_comment'></div>狼顾未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1371956_comment'></div>先太保时为行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1371956_comment'></div>用公之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1371956_comment'></div>与滔定计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1371956_comment'></div>戢兵彻警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1371956_comment'></div>洗舋归诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1371956_comment'></div>致父于曲突之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1371956_comment'></div>拯人于坠涂之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1371956_comment'></div>由是山东侯伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1371956_comment'></div>始闻其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1371956_comment'></div>是岁孟秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1371956_comment'></div>滔卒于镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1371956_comment'></div>幽人怀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1371956_comment'></div>推奉太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1371956_comment'></div>方执谦志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1371956_comment'></div>未允诚求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1371956_comment'></div>公以为幽燕本负气之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1371956_comment'></div>豪杰陷失节之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1371956_comment'></div>自新无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1371956_comment'></div>从乱如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1371956_comment'></div>安危生于俯仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1371956_comment'></div>逆顺决于指顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1371956_comment'></div>权必有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1371956_comment'></div>不可以假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1371956_comment'></div>贵不为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1371956_comment'></div>岂嫌于在巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1371956_comment'></div>趋庭诤谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1371956_comment'></div>决策指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1371956_comment'></div>正颓波于众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1371956_comment'></div>回白日于王命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1371956_comment'></div>重氛载廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1371956_comment'></div>阖境昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1371956_comment'></div>由是汉庭公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1371956_comment'></div>始重其节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1371956_comment'></div>太保既婴危疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1371956_comment'></div>侍中时镇莫州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1371956_comment'></div>公总兵中权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1371956_comment'></div>尝药内寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1371956_comment'></div>弛张在手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1371956_comment'></div>上下宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1371956_comment'></div>而见利不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1371956_comment'></div>临事能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1371956_comment'></div>推至公于门内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1371956_comment'></div>度德惟钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1371956_comment'></div>申大义于军中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1371956_comment'></div>以长则顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1371956_comment'></div>于是陟岗长望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1371956_comment'></div>飞驲潜迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1371956_comment'></div>劝辍哭于创巨之晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1371956_comment'></div>托理命于纲纪之仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1371956_comment'></div>军府立定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1371956_comment'></div>家国乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1371956_comment'></div>然后退就丧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1371956_comment'></div>而泣柴毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1371956_comment'></div>三军感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1371956_comment'></div>四邻耸慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1371956_comment'></div>子之道弟之道备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1371956_comment'></div>孝之难友之难至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1371956_comment'></div>既而侍中泣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1371956_comment'></div>金华无避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1371956_comment'></div>吾岂获巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1371956_comment'></div>手足相卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1371956_comment'></div>尔何自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1371956_comment'></div>遂奏起公为涿州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1371956_comment'></div>未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1371956_comment'></div>转领瀛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1371956_comment'></div>东负沧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1371956_comment'></div>南驰诸夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1371956_comment'></div>地饶俗杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1371956_comment'></div>久号难理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1371956_comment'></div>公乃简其约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1371956_comment'></div>峻其堤防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1371956_comment'></div>均其有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1371956_comment'></div>一其劳逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1371956_comment'></div>心听而方断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1371956_comment'></div>身践而后言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1371956_comment'></div>令下于流水之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1371956_comment'></div>化行于偃草之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1371956_comment'></div>盗奔他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1371956_comment'></div>人复先畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1371956_comment'></div>亦既富庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1371956_comment'></div>聿观礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1371956_comment'></div>日用吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1371956_comment'></div>于何不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1371956_comment'></div>其年兼御史中丞充本道节度瀛州兵马留后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1371956_comment'></div>又兼御史大夫行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1371956_comment'></div>丁越国夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1371956_comment'></div>至性继酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1371956_comment'></div>终天穷感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1371956_comment'></div>杖而后起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1371956_comment'></div>殆不胜丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1371956_comment'></div>军士泣留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1371956_comment'></div>王人逼谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1371956_comment'></div>起复旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1371956_comment'></div>敬恭新命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1371956_comment'></div>孝在方寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1371956_comment'></div>能尽其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1371956_comment'></div>政有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1371956_comment'></div>不愆于素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1371956_comment'></div>服阕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1371956_comment'></div>加银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1371956_comment'></div>馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1371956_comment'></div>公高视前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1371956_comment'></div>志齐古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1371956_comment'></div>疾没世不称之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1371956_comment'></div>慕其次立功之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1371956_comment'></div>见去病无用家为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1371956_comment'></div>卷常三复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1371956_comment'></div>闻耿弇不以贼遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1371956_comment'></div>坐惜分阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1371956_comment'></div>必欲悬旌黑山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1371956_comment'></div>饮马西海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1371956_comment'></div>气定百胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1371956_comment'></div>身先七擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1371956_comment'></div>讨冒顿之慢书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1371956_comment'></div>复犬戎之侵地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1371956_comment'></div>有怀未果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1371956_comment'></div>若耻在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1371956_comment'></div>爰因大阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1371956_comment'></div>乃告于众曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1371956_comment'></div>吾剖符别统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1371956_comment'></div>行已十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1371956_comment'></div>训齐之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1371956_comment'></div>不下一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1371956_comment'></div>而靡衣鲜食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1371956_comment'></div>销锐刓锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1371956_comment'></div>徒籍父兄之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1371956_comment'></div>莫申丝发之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1371956_comment'></div>永言及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1371956_comment'></div>何以为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1371956_comment'></div>且东胡之强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1371956_comment'></div>吾兄既雄其式遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1371956_comment'></div>西丑之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1371956_comment'></div>鄙志必期于殄歼。<div id='poem_sentence_248_1371956_comment'></div>游于地下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1371956_comment'></div>无负先公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1371956_comment'></div>谁居谁行。<div id='poem_sentence_253_1371956_comment'></div>一呼三跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1371956_comment'></div>童儿奋臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1371956_comment'></div>女子褰裳。<div id='poem_sentence_258_1371956_comment'></div>彀骑八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1371956_comment'></div>组甲五千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1371956_comment'></div>次舍案部。<div id='poem_sentence_300_1371956_comment'></div>割扶风之普润县以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1371956_comment'></div>倚为长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1371956_comment'></div>镇我近辅。<div id='poem_sentence_305_1371956_comment'></div>屝屦资粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1371956_comment'></div>同北军之宠士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1371956_comment'></div>而犹未赐齐履。<div id='poem_sentence_310_1371956_comment'></div>所以观自致之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1371956_comment'></div>假领侨郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1371956_comment'></div>所以激必取之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1371956_comment'></div>先皇将将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1371956_comment'></div>厥有深旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1371956_comment'></div>公由是感悟神动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1371956_comment'></div>精诚涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1371956_comment'></div>荷知臣之明。<div id='poem_sentence_320_1371956_comment'></div>激昂雄图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1371956_comment'></div>而地狭一同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1371956_comment'></div>众才十旅。<div id='poem_sentence_325_1371956_comment'></div>因深为隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1371956_comment'></div>即险增垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1371956_comment'></div>剪蓬伐木。<div id='poem_sentence_330_1371956_comment'></div>以开屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1371956_comment'></div>俸禄不入于私家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1371956_comment'></div>子弟必从于公役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1371956_comment'></div>缣缃之寻尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1371956_comment'></div>咸在军装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1371956_comment'></div>金铁之锱铢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1371956_comment'></div>尽归兵器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1371956_comment'></div>无歌僮舞女之玩。<div id='poem_sentence_340_1371956_comment'></div>而骁果是务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1371956_comment'></div>加以推诚待下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1371956_comment'></div>爱士如身。<div id='poem_sentence_345_1371956_comment'></div>字孤养老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1371956_comment'></div>骨肉何先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1371956_comment'></div>遂令千夫一心。<div id='poem_sentence_350_1371956_comment'></div>未见敌而争为前登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1371956_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1371956_comment'></div>众知吾深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1371956_comment'></div>其可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1371956_comment'></div>于是驰使阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1371956_comment'></div>请牧隍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1371956_comment'></div>出自凶门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1371956_comment'></div>入于死地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1371956_comment'></div>衽席过兵之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1371956_comment'></div>咽喉制敌之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1371956_comment'></div>威怀启闭之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1371956_comment'></div>耕战疾徐之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1371956_comment'></div>莫不封章定计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1371956_comment'></div>裂素成图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1371956_comment'></div>德宗览之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1371956_comment'></div>废食兴叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1371956_comment'></div>属戎渠悔祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1371956_comment'></div>朝议许盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_480_1371956_comment'></div>继立家道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_481_1371956_comment'></div>二南所美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_482_1371956_comment'></div>无以尚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_483_1371956_comment'></div>有子五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_484_1371956_comment'></div>长曰锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_485_1371956_comment'></div>朝议太子洗马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_486_1371956_comment'></div>周旋经训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_487_1371956_comment'></div>斧藻身文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_488_1371956_comment'></div>确有端操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_489_1371956_comment'></div>雅多奇略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_490_1371956_comment'></div>有识之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_491_1371956_comment'></div>知其大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_492_1371956_comment'></div>次曰师贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_493_1371956_comment'></div>前右武卫仓曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_494_1371956_comment'></div>次曰师礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_495_1371956_comment'></div>前商州司仓参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_496_1371956_comment'></div>次曰税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_497_1371956_comment'></div>前钦王府参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_498_1371956_comment'></div>次曰兑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_499_1371956_comment'></div>门子出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_500_1371956_comment'></div>桂殊姿而共芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_501_1371956_comment'></div>圭璋异质而同润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_502_1371956_comment'></div>百祥之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_503_1371956_comment'></div>其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_504_1371956_comment'></div>洗马等相与谋曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_505_1371956_comment'></div>夫步星气者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_506_1371956_comment'></div>无出于冯相之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_507_1371956_comment'></div>考钟律者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_508_1371956_comment'></div>必求于伶伦之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_509_1371956_comment'></div>我先人之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_510_1371956_comment'></div>非志士不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_511_1371956_comment'></div>以某早纂功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_512_1371956_comment'></div>常窥阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_513_1371956_comment'></div>辨用心之所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_514_1371956_comment'></div>识行事之会归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_515_1371956_comment'></div>俾垂斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_516_1371956_comment'></div>以示来哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_517_1371956_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_518_1371956_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_519_1371956'>至精氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_519_1371956_comment'></div>为勇为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_520_1371956_comment'></div>将昭文德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_521_1371956_comment'></div>有此武臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_522_1371956_comment'></div>猛而不残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_523_1371956_comment'></div>灵而能驯。<div id='poem_sentence_526_1371956_comment'></div>源由尧兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_527_1371956_comment'></div>派自汉启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_528_1371956_comment'></div>承光祖考。<div id='poem_sentence_531_1371956_comment'></div>达乐知礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_532_1371956_comment'></div>行归有方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_533_1371956_comment'></div>用入无体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_534_1371956_comment'></div>中襟汤汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_535_1371956_comment'></div>应变弛张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_536_1371956_comment'></div>开则雷电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_537_1371956_comment'></div>闭为金汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_538_1371956_comment'></div>能求敌情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_539_1371956_comment'></div>善用已长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_540_1371956_comment'></div>威不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_541_1371956_comment'></div>惠不可忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_542_1371956_comment'></div>静言未宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_543_1371956_comment'></div>忠愤慷恺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_544_1371956_comment'></div>翻翻燕海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1371956_comment'></div>固护秦塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1371956_comment'></div>车无停轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_547_1371956_comment'></div>衣不解带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_548_1371956_comment'></div>勤王万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_549_1371956_comment'></div>瞻我大旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1371956_comment'></div>左汧右泾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1371956_comment'></div>克壮其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1371956_comment'></div>目尽西极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1371956_comment'></div>尘沙不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_554_1371956_comment'></div>行人如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_555_1371956_comment'></div>战士且耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_556_1371956_comment'></div>陇首烽断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_557_1371956_comment'></div>原川草生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_558_1371956_comment'></div>方提金鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_561_1371956_comment'></div>恢复旧宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_562_1371956_comment'></div>促运僭夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_563_1371956_comment'></div>奇功莫睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_564_1371956_comment'></div>殁而不瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1371956_comment'></div>足感明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_566_1371956_comment'></div>诏葬九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_567_1371956_comment'></div>宠昭幽魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_568_1371956_comment'></div>介士班剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_569_1371956_comment'></div>送于都门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_570_1371956_comment'></div>草陈霜来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_571_1371956_comment'></div>树拱烟昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_572_1371956_comment'></div>万物有尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_573_1371956_comment'></div>唯石独存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_574_1371956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　本年被贬前，在长安代郑絪作状请删定施行六典开元礼。作品：《代郑相公请删定施行六典开元礼状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第55页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑相公请删定施行六典开元礼状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371899")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371899'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371899_comment'></div>臣闻化人成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371899_comment'></div>莫大于礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371899_comment'></div>垂统建中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371899_comment'></div>必资于制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371899_comment'></div>然而忠敬有弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371899_comment'></div>质文异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371899_comment'></div>群儒之得失蜂起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371899_comment'></div>历代之沿革丝棼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371899_comment'></div>或荣古而陋今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371899_comment'></div>名实交丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371899_comment'></div>或违经而便事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371899_comment'></div>本末相忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371899_comment'></div>或烦杂以为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371899_comment'></div>或阔略以为要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371899_comment'></div>未闻折衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371899_comment'></div>以叶通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371899_comment'></div>国家与天惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371899_comment'></div>改物视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371899_comment'></div>太宗拯焚溺之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371899_comment'></div>粗立统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371899_comment'></div>玄宗承富庶之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371899_comment'></div>方暇论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371899_comment'></div>爰敕宰臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371899_comment'></div>将明睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371899_comment'></div>集儒贤于别殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371899_comment'></div>考古训于秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371899_comment'></div>以论材审官之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371899_comment'></div>作大唐六典三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371899_comment'></div>以道德齐礼之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371899_comment'></div>作开元新礼一百五十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371899_comment'></div>网罗遗逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371899_comment'></div>芟剪奇邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371899_comment'></div>亘百代以旁通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371899_comment'></div>立一王之定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371899_comment'></div>草奏三复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371899_comment'></div>祗令宣示中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371899_comment'></div>星周六纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371899_comment'></div>未有明诏施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371899_comment'></div>遂使丧祭冠婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371899_comment'></div>家犹异礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371899_comment'></div>等威名分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371899_comment'></div>官靡成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371899_comment'></div>不时裁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371899_comment'></div>贻弊方远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371899_comment'></div>伏惟睿圣文武皇帝陛下恢纂鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371899_comment'></div>允升大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371899_comment'></div>雷霆奋有截之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371899_comment'></div>日月廓无私之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371899_comment'></div>三叛就戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371899_comment'></div>四夷来宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371899_comment'></div>牛马放于农郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371899_comment'></div>兵革藏于武库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371899_comment'></div>严禋上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371899_comment'></div>祗受鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371899_comment'></div>惟怀永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371899_comment'></div>不自满假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371899_comment'></div>昧爽听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371899_comment'></div>子夜读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371899_comment'></div>处成功而弗休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371899_comment'></div>率至理若不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371899_comment'></div>每怀经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371899_comment'></div>则知贞观之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371899_comment'></div>言念持盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371899_comment'></div>思复开元之盛。<div id='poem_sentence_66_1371899_comment'></div>无能辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371899_comment'></div>已负于恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371899_comment'></div>有所建明。<div id='poem_sentence_71_1371899_comment'></div>圣朝所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371899_comment'></div>郁而未用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371899_comment'></div>奉扬遗美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371899_comment'></div>允属钦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371899_comment'></div>然或损益之间。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371899_comment'></div>将贻永代之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371899_comment'></div>必俟不刊之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371899_comment'></div>臣请于常参官内选学艺优深理识通远者三五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371899_comment'></div>就集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371899_comment'></div>各尽异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371899_comment'></div>量加删定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371899_comment'></div>然后敢尘睿览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371899_comment'></div>特降德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371899_comment'></div>明下有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371899_comment'></div>著为恒式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371899_comment'></div>使公私共守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371899_comment'></div>贵贱遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371899_comment'></div>苟有愆违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371899_comment'></div>必正刑宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371899_comment'></div>如此则职官有制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371899_comment'></div>将兴济济之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371899_comment'></div>风俗大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371899_comment'></div>坐致熙熙之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371899_comment'></div>见可而献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371899_comment'></div>知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371899_comment'></div>辄渎宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371899_comment'></div>伏增陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371899_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1371899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　本年被贬前，在长安代郑絪作状谢赐戟。作品：《代郑相公谢赐戟状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第55页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑相公谢赐门戟状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371897")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371897'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371897'>门戟十二竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371897_comment'></div>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371897_comment'></div>今日中使某乙至臣私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371897_comment'></div>奉宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371897_comment'></div>赐臣前件戟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371897_comment'></div>臣伏以国朝之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371897_comment'></div>名器尤慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371897_comment'></div>吏考三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371897_comment'></div>始秩银青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371897_comment'></div>战勋十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371897_comment'></div>乃号柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371897_comment'></div>必资具美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371897_comment'></div>方锡殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371897_comment'></div>于是有命服以朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371897_comment'></div>加戟于户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371897_comment'></div>将劝劳而责实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371897_comment'></div>亦驭贵而崇名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371897_comment'></div>上无谬恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371897_comment'></div>下不虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371897_comment'></div>臣迹非奇致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371897_comment'></div>擢自诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371897_comment'></div>先皇以廉谨赐知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371897_comment'></div>密勿踰于一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371897_comment'></div>陛下以勤忧过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371897_comment'></div>委遇首于群僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371897_comment'></div>叨据枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371897_comment'></div>亟移星岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371897_comment'></div>雷霆用武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371897_comment'></div>曾无犬马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371897_comment'></div>日月垂文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371897_comment'></div>岂有萤烛之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371897_comment'></div>徒以侍祠清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371897_comment'></div>拜舞鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371897_comment'></div>累逢庆赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371897_comment'></div>骤假勋秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371897_comment'></div>礼异其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371897_comment'></div>物盛其容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371897_comment'></div>新其闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371897_comment'></div>赐之棨戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371897_comment'></div>衡门燕雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371897_comment'></div>乍相贺于朱楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371897_comment'></div>武库<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1371897", 1371897, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>龙蛇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371897_comment'></div>忽追飞于陋巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371897_comment'></div>焜耀当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371897_comment'></div>宠灵自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371897_comment'></div>聚族知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371897_comment'></div>杀身匪报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371897_comment'></div>无任荷惧屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371897_comment'></div>谨奉状陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1371897_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月15日</a>　十月十五日，吕温因与窦群劾奏宰相李吉甫交通术士，贬为均州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，复贬为道州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月</a>　十月，吕温追贬道州刺史后，与弟恭花下共饮，感而作诗。作品：《楚州追制后舍弟直长安县失囚花下共饮》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第15页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。诗题中“楚州”疑为“均州”之误。）</span><div id='poem_18501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18501")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18501'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18501'>天子收郡印，京兆责狱囚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18501'>狂兄与狂弟，不解对花愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
大名（魏州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dedac50c7a6947478cacf644b931f3d8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dedac50c7a6947478cacf644b931f3d8");'><span id='dedac50c7a6947478cacf644b931f3d8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>，21岁</div><div id='dedac50c7a6947478cacf644b931f3d8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=792&endYear=792')">792年</a>　继祖母卒，其父吕渭守制洛下。吕温奉父命，至魏州将祖母之坟迁于洛阳。<br /></div>
