-----title
运城（平陆）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab92f02362484674b70a271ab3b51c9f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab92f02362484674b70a271ab3b51c9f");'><span id='ab92f02362484674b70a271ab3b51c9f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年</a>，22岁</div><div id='ab92f02362484674b70a271ab3b51c9f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年</a>　约于下半年，自长安往洛阳参加次年的河南府试，过虞虢，有文。作品：《傅岩铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第83页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>傅岩铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（793年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371948")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371948_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371948'>昔殷高宗恭默思道。至诚动天。天将报之。以说为瑞。王在于寝。降神梦中。审形旁求。实得于此。曾不待敷奏以言。明试以功。脱刑人之衣。被公衮之服。授受之际。君不疑。臣不惭。大哉邈乎。殷之所以兴也。若非武丁之心。同乎天地。傅说之德。通乎神明。何感动䜣合。如此其易。厥后惟文王以兆用太公。自渔父而登国师。白旄一麾。光定天下。抑其邻欤。由兹而还。莫不先显后幽。右资左德。勒以汉秩。束于周行。使特达自致之士无闻焉。吁可叹也。夫以天骥之才。而造父驭之。则必翼轻轩。淩高衢。风翔电迈。一日千里。若制非其人。服非其车。志权奇。务牵束。挫盛气。顿逸足。使遵乎循常之躅。则终岁疾驱。望驽骀而不及矣。遇与不遇。又何疑哉。呜呼。见贤非难。知之难。知之非难。用之难。用之非难。特达难。君人者苟以特达为心。假无殷宗之梦。必自得说。不然。则虽使咎夔稷契。尽入其庭。亦叶公之见龙。反疑惧矣。况氤氲之中乎。恍惚之际乎。贞元九年。予自镐徂洛。息驾于虞虢之间。升墟瞰原。髣髴其地。远迹虽昧。清风若存。想说命三篇。几堕秦火。百代之后。德音如何。乃作铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371948'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371948'>赫赫汤德，如日不灭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371948'>滔滔商祚，如海不竭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371948'>发祥播气，世祚圣哲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371948'>国诞武丁，野生傅说。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371948'>说始胥靡，武丁即祚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371948'>德通神交，忽梦如悟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371948'>若帝导我，期于颢素。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371948'>有无之间，邂逅相遇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371948'>宵衣而起，爰得其人。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371948'>貌符心冥，如旧君臣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371948'>飞龙在天，山川出云。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371948'>感激自致，其间无因。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1371948'>舍筑傅岩，脱鳞鹏升。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1371948'>作霖时和，奋楫川澄。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1371948'>金在吾砺，木从吾绳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1371948'>君何言哉，殷道中兴。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1371948'>元凯攀尧，微舜曷阶。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1371948'>阿衡要汤，抱鼎徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1371948'>会合之际，厥惟难哉。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1371948'>何如梦中，天授神开。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1371948'>惟贤是登，道贵特达。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1371948'>匪次勿用，才其壅遏。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1371948'>高宗得说，乃在恍惚。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1371948'>揭铭摛光，万古不没。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1371948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1371948'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1371948_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
灵宝（虢州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3eee6726136e4d688fe65fc81a3ba2e3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3eee6726136e4d688fe65fc81a3ba2e3");'><span id='3eee6726136e4d688fe65fc81a3ba2e3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年</a>，22岁</div><div id='3eee6726136e4d688fe65fc81a3ba2e3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年</a>　约于下半年，自长安往洛阳参加次年的河南府试，过虞虢，应请作文。作品：《虢州三堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷10第109页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虢州三堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（793年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371921")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371921'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371921'>应龙乘风云。作雷雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371921_comment'></div>退必蟠蛰。以全其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371921_comment'></div>君子役智能。统机剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371921_comment'></div>退必宴息。以全其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371921_comment'></div>力全则神化无穷。性全则精用不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371921_comment'></div>深山大泽。其所以蟠蛰乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371921_comment'></div>高斋清地。其所以宴息乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371921_comment'></div>虢州三堂者。君子宴息之境也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371921_comment'></div>开元初。天子思二南之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371921_comment'></div>并选宗英。共持理柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371921_comment'></div>虢大而近。匪亲不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371921_comment'></div>时惟五王。出入相授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371921_comment'></div>承平易理。逸政多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371921_comment'></div>考卜惟胜。作为三堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371921_comment'></div>三者明臣子在三之节。堂者励宗室克构之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371921_comment'></div>岂徒造适。实亦垂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371921_comment'></div>居德乐善。何其盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371921_comment'></div>然当时汉同家人。鲁用王礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371921_comment'></div>栋宇制度。非诸侯居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371921_comment'></div>后刺史马君锡。因其颓陊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371921_comment'></div>始革基构。丰而不侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371921_comment'></div>约而不陋。以琴尊诗书之幽素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371921_comment'></div>易绮纨钟鼓之繁喧。惟林池烟景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371921_comment'></div>不让他日。观其广踰百亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371921_comment'></div>深入重扃。回塘屈盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371921_comment'></div>沓岛交映。溟渤转于环堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371921_comment'></div>蓬壶起于中庭。浩然天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371921_comment'></div>孰曰智及。春之日众木花折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371921_comment'></div>岸铺岛织。沈浮照耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371921_comment'></div>其水五色。于是乎袭馨撷奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371921_comment'></div>方舟逶迤。乐鱼时翻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371921_comment'></div>飘蕊雪飞。溯沿回环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371921_comment'></div>隐映差池。咫尺迷路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371921_comment'></div>不知所归。此则武陵仙源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371921_comment'></div>未足以极幽绝也。夏之日石寒水清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371921_comment'></div>松密竹深。大柳起风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371921_comment'></div>甘棠垂阴。于是乎濯缨涟漪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371921_comment'></div>解带升堂。畏景火云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371921_comment'></div>隔林无光。虚甍沈沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371921_comment'></div>皓壁如霜。羽扇不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371921_comment'></div>南轩清凉。此则楚襄兰台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371921_comment'></div>未足以涤炎郁也。秋之日金飙扫林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371921_comment'></div>蓊郁洞开。太华爽气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371921_comment'></div>出关而来。于是乎弦琴端居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371921_comment'></div>景物廓如。月委皓素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371921_comment'></div>水涵空虚。鸟惊寒沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371921_comment'></div>露滴高梧。境随夜深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371921_comment'></div>疑与世殊。此则庾公西楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371921_comment'></div>未足以澹神虑也。冬之日同云千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371921_comment'></div>大雪盈尺。四眺无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371921_comment'></div>三堂虚白。于是乎置酒褰帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371921_comment'></div>凭轩倚楹。瑶阶如银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371921_comment'></div>玉树罗生。日暮天霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371921_comment'></div>云开月明。冰泉潺潺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371921_comment'></div>终夜有声。此则子猷山阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371921_comment'></div>未足以畅吟啸也。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371921_comment'></div>不离轩冕。而践夷旷之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371921_comment'></div>不出户庭。而获江海之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371921_comment'></div>趣近悬解。迹同大隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371921_comment'></div>序阅四时之胜。节宣六气之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371921_comment'></div>贵而居之。可曰厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371921_comment'></div>若知其身既安。而思所以安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371921_comment'></div>其性既适。而思所以适物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371921_comment'></div>不以自乐而忽鳏寡之苦。不以自逸而忘稼穑之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371921_comment'></div>能推是心。以惠境内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371921_comment'></div>则良二千石也。方今人亦劳止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371921_comment'></div>上思乂息。州郡之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371921_comment'></div>重如廷臣。由是南阳张公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371921_comment'></div>辍挥翰之任。受剖符之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371921_comment'></div>游刃而理。此焉坐啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371921_comment'></div>静政令若水木。閒人民如鱼鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371921_comment'></div>驯致其道。闇然日彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371921_comment'></div>小子以通家之好。获拜床下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371921_comment'></div>且齿诸子。侍坐于三堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371921_comment'></div>见知惟文。不敢无述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371921_comment'></div>捧笔避席。请书堂阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371921_comment'></div>俾后之人知此堂非止燕游。亦可以观清静为政之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371921_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1371921_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0ceb405cdb1e4772bee49c24a65dac6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ceb405cdb1e4772bee49c24a65dac6e");'><span id='0ceb405cdb1e4772bee49c24a65dac6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>，24岁</div><div id='0ceb405cdb1e4772bee49c24a65dac6e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>漫游中登虢州阌乡望思台，有感作文。作品：《望思台铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第84页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望思台铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371949")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371949_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371949'>望思台者。汉武帝思戾太子之所建也。事具汉书。夫立人之道。本乎情性。生而知曰性。感而动曰情。性虽生情。情或灭性。是以圣人患其然而为之节。诚而明之。中而庸之。建以大伦。统以至顺。伦莫极于父子。顺莫先于慈孝。然而全之者正也。慈不得其正则失子。孝不得其正则失亲。救失之术。存乎善教。昔者三王之教世子也。如周公乃为太傅。如召公乃为太保。如太公乃为太师。左右前后。罔非端士。礼以专其目。乐以一其耳。仁以制其气。义以凝其情。故非僻之心。无自入也。谗慝之口。莫能间也。父子君臣之道。所以全也。汉则不然。世子非三代之贤。保傅无二南之老。左右前后。惟刑馀罪人。目流于靡慢。耳溺于惉滞。气溢于宠渥。情荡于骄奢。于是非僻之心。得以入矣。谗慝之口。得以间矣。父子君臣之道。所以离矣。向使太子师友尊严。左右端肃。虽江充之诈。岂敢以不义而加之耶。向使太子孝德彰闻。仁声茂著。虽武帝之惑。岂遽以大逆而疑之耶。向使太子早服师训。少知教义。岂忍一朝之忿。弃其亲而忘其身耶。由是言之。其所以陷于此者渐矣。殆哉当时之势也。国亡冢嗣。武老昭弱。京师喋血。天下疑动。若无霍光受负图之寄。秉不夺之节。斥昏建明。镇翊鸿业。则必庶孽寻戈。起商参之祸。奸臣乘衅。行羿浞之事。汉家之祀。岂及三七哉。此有社稷者之所宜深戒也。乙亥岁。予经于湖。登兹荒台。望古太息。以为遇夫一物。有可以垂训于世者。秉笔之士。未尝阙焉。乃作铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1371949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371949'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371949'>人伦大统，天性是宝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371949'>虽曰自然，亦资斧藻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371949'>汉皇父子，一失其道。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371949'>四海为家，不能相保。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371949'>荒台岿而，千古之悲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371949'>悔目空断，冤魂不归。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371949'>疑生于微，祸积于基。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371949'>苟有明义，谁其间之。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371949'>嗣维邦本，本动邦危。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371949'>于呼后王，鉴兹在兹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371949'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1371949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>漫游中登虢州阌乡登望思台，有感作诗。作品：《望思台》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第11页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望思台作</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18458")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_18458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18458'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18458'>浸润成宫蛊，苍黄弄父兵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18458'>人情疑始变，天性感还生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18458'>宇县犹能洽，闺门讵不平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18458'>空令千载后，悽怆望思名。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18458'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_18458'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(18458)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永济（河东）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d2e6ef16dd724841a6d45572c2912e6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2e6ef16dd724841a6d45572c2912e6e");'><span id='d2e6ef16dd724841a6d45572c2912e6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>，24岁</div><div id='d2e6ef16dd724841a6d45572c2912e6e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年11月1日</a>　八月后，出关漫游。十一月，拜谒河东舜庙，有文。作品：《谒舜庙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第86页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒舜庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年11月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371963")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371963'>唐贞元十一年岁次乙亥十一月一日。东平吕温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371963_comment'></div>敢盥沐斋洁敬谒于舜帝之神。恭惟至仁无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371963_comment'></div>大孝不匮。德馨升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371963_comment'></div>允釐百揆。以圣授圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371963_comment'></div>犹言历试。择人之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371963_comment'></div>良不可易。圣功无全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371963_comment'></div>相待而宣。雷驱四凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371963_comment'></div>灵起八元。太冶陶土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371963_comment'></div>璿玑转天。垂衣岩庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371963_comment'></div>万物浩然。是称至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371963_comment'></div>是曰帝者。混成雍熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371963_comment'></div>永锡大嘏。乃眷南顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371963_comment'></div>苍梧之野。归尧鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371963_comment'></div>付禹天下。茫茫推迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371963_comment'></div>邈万斯年。三代之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371963_comment'></div>谁为圣贤。政如颓波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371963_comment'></div>俗若坏山。韶乐犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371963_comment'></div>薰风不还。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371963_comment'></div>道有通变。事有同异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371963_comment'></div>官帝家王。随时之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371963_comment'></div>揖让而禅。固非力致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371963_comment'></div>所以识者。存而不议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371963_comment'></div>若辅相之宜。财成之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371963_comment'></div>焕乎文章。百代可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371963_comment'></div>九官惟旧。七政有彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371963_comment'></div>宏道在人。太平无时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371963_comment'></div>如何后王。曾莫是思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371963_comment'></div>甚易甚简。舍而弗为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371963_comment'></div>历山岿然。河水东注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371963_comment'></div>唐虞日远。杨墨谁拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371963_comment'></div>瞻彼历山。薄言往诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371963_comment'></div>庶几精诚。必我依据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371963_comment'></div>假我以灵。俾飞曾云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371963_comment'></div>行神之道。以致吾君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371963_comment'></div>不然归来。鸟兽为群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371963_comment'></div>敢竭微志。托于明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371963_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1371963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年11月</a>　孟冬，经蒲津关河亭，有诗。作品：《孟冬蒲津关河亭作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第11页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18447' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18447")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18447'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18447'>息驾非穷途，未济岂迷津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18447'>独立大河上，北风来吹人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
荥阳（汜水）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2585c8a2c8fd4d9aaa109aee82c694ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2585c8a2c8fd4d9aaa109aee82c694ef");'><span id='2585c8a2c8fd4d9aaa109aee82c694ef_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=795&endYear=795')">795年</a>　漫游中凭览成皋故地，瞻仰故洛城，有文。作品：《成皋铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第85页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>成皋铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（795年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371950")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1371950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371950'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371950'>芒芒大野，万邦错峙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1371950'>惟正守国，设险于此。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1371950'>呀谷成堑，崇巅若累。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1371950'>势轶赤霄，气吞千里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1371950'>洪河在下，太室傍倚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1371950'>冈盘岭蹙，虎伏龙起。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1371950'>锁天中区，控地四鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1371950'>出必由户，入皆同轨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1371950'>拒昏纳明，闭乱开理。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1371950'>昔在秦亡，雷雨晦冥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1371950'>刘项分险，扼喉而争。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1371950'>汉飞镐京，羽斩东城。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1371950'>德有厚薄，此山无情。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1371950'>维唐初兴，时未大同。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1371950'>王于东征，烈火顺风。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1371950'>乘高建瓴，擒建系充。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1371950'>奄有天下，斯焉定功。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1371950'>二百年间，大朴既还。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1371950'>周道如砥，成皋不关。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1371950'>顺至则平，逆来惟难。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1371950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1371950_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
汝州（梁县）
-----detail

-----title
巩义（巩县）

-----title
城固
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='123d61c744254a80be6f7aeb1b3c1024_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("123d61c744254a80be6f7aeb1b3c1024");'><span id='123d61c744254a80be6f7aeb1b3c1024_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>，27岁</div><div id='123d61c744254a80be6f7aeb1b3c1024' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年7月25日</a>　本年七月，自长安经子午谷入兴元府，谒诸葛武侯庙，有文。作品：《诸葛武侯庙记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷10第110页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸葛武侯庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年7月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371920")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371920'>天厌汉德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371920_comment'></div>俾绝其纽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371920_comment'></div>群生坠涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371920_comment'></div>四海飞水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371920_comment'></div>武侯命世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371920_comment'></div>实念皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371920_comment'></div>魏奸吴轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371920_comment'></div>未获我心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371920_comment'></div>胥宇南阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371920_comment'></div>坚卧不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371920_comment'></div>三顾虽晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371920_comment'></div>群雄初定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371920_comment'></div>必也彗扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371920_comment'></div>是资鼎立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371920_comment'></div>变化消息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371920_comment'></div>谋成掌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371920_comment'></div>战龙元黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371920_comment'></div>再得云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371920_comment'></div>于是右揭如天之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371920_comment'></div>左提用武之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371920_comment'></div>因山分力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371920_comment'></div>与水合势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371920_comment'></div>蟠亘万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371920_comment'></div>张为龙形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371920_comment'></div>首吞咸镐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371920_comment'></div>尾束河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371920_comment'></div>翼出中夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371920_comment'></div>飞跃天衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371920_comment'></div>然后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1371920", 1371920, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鱼驱</span>句吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371920_comment'></div>东入晏海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371920_comment'></div>大勋未集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371920_comment'></div>天夺其魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371920_comment'></div>至诚无忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371920_comment'></div>炳在日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371920_comment'></div>烈气不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371920_comment'></div>长为风雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371920_comment'></div>英雄痛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371920_comment'></div>六百年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371920_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371920_comment'></div>以武侯之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371920_comment'></div>知已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1371920", 1371920, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>托国</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371920_comment'></div>土虽狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371920_comment'></div>国以勤俭富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371920_comment'></div>民虽寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371920_comment'></div>兵以节制强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371920_comment'></div>魏武既没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371920_comment'></div>晋宣非敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371920_comment'></div>而戎马荐驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371920_comment'></div>不复中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371920_comment'></div>或曰奇谋非长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371920_comment'></div>则斩将覆军无虚举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371920_comment'></div>或曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1371920", 1371920, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>馈粮</span>不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371920_comment'></div>则筑室反耕有成算矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371920_comment'></div>尝试念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371920_comment'></div>颇赜其原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371920_comment'></div>夫民无恒归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371920_comment'></div>德以为归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371920_comment'></div>抚则思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371920_comment'></div>虐则忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371920_comment'></div>其思也不可使忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371920_comment'></div>其忘也不可使思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371920_comment'></div>当汉道方休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371920_comment'></div>哀平无政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371920_comment'></div>王莽乃欲凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1371920", 1371920, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>戚宠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371920_comment'></div>造符命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371920_comment'></div>胁之以威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371920_comment'></div>动之以神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371920_comment'></div>使人忘汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371920_comment'></div>终不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371920_comment'></div>及高光旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371920_comment'></div>与世衰远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371920_comment'></div>桓灵流毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371920_comment'></div>在人骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371920_comment'></div>武侯乃欲开兴图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371920_comment'></div>振绝绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371920_comment'></div>论之以本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371920_comment'></div>临之以忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371920_comment'></div>使人思汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371920_comment'></div>卒亦不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371920_comment'></div>向使武侯奉先主之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371920_comment'></div>告天下曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371920_comment'></div>我之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371920_comment'></div>匪私刘宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371920_comment'></div>唯活元元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371920_comment'></div>曹氏利汝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371920_comment'></div>吾事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371920_comment'></div>曹氏害汝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371920_comment'></div>吾除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371920_comment'></div>俾虐魏偪从之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371920_comment'></div>耸诚感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371920_comment'></div>然后经武观衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371920_comment'></div>长驱义声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371920_comment'></div>咸洛不足定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371920_comment'></div>奈何当至公之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371920_comment'></div>而强人以私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371920_comment'></div>此犹力争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371920_comment'></div>彼未心服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371920_comment'></div>勤而靡获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371920_comment'></div>不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371920_comment'></div>乃知务开济之业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371920_comment'></div>未能审时定势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371920_comment'></div>大顺人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371920_comment'></div>而克观厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371920_comment'></div>吾不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371920_comment'></div>惜其才有馀而见未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371920_comment'></div>述于遗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371920_comment'></div>以俟通识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371920_comment'></div>唐贞元十四年七月十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371920_comment'></div>东平吕温记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_108_1371920_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='790bfe1fb48140459ac52ee4a92da755_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("790bfe1fb48140459ac52ee4a92da755");'><span id='790bfe1fb48140459ac52ee4a92da755_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>，28岁</div><div id='790bfe1fb48140459ac52ee4a92da755' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　时父吕渭任湖南观察使、潭州刺史。吕温及第后南下赴潭州省亲，途中出襄樊，有赋。作品：《由鹿赋并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷1第1页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>由鹿赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371866")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371866_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1371866'>贞元丁卯岁，予南出襄樊之间，遇野人絷鹿而至者，问之，答曰：此为由鹿，由此鹿以诱致群鹿也。备言其状，且曰：此鹿每有所致，辄鸣嗥不饮食者累日。予喟然叹曰：虞之即鹿也，必以其类致之；人之即人也，亦必以其友致之。实繁有徒，古之然矣。嗟乎，鹿无情而犹知痛，伤人之与谋宴安残酷者，彼何人斯。物微感深，遂作赋曰：</div><div id='poem_preface_1371866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371866'>鹿之生兮亦秉亭，毒备齿角以无竞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371866_comment'></div>循性情而自牧，姑有昧于行止，尚焉知乎倚伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371866_comment'></div>舍尔崇林，轻游近麓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371866_comment'></div>偶巧网之生致，蒙主人之全育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371866_comment'></div>饮以渫井，饲于芳庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371866_comment'></div>寝卧筌柔，腾倚兰馨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371866_comment'></div>露往霜来，日安月宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371866_comment'></div>虽矫性而非乐，终感恩而不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371866_comment'></div>曾不知养非玩物，用有深意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371866_comment'></div>命曰由鹿，俾陷其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371866_comment'></div>凉秋八月，爽景清气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371866_comment'></div>羁致山阿，縻于蹊遂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371866_comment'></div>设伏以待，翳丛而伺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371866_comment'></div>同气相求，诱之孔易，将必慕侣，岂云贪饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371866_comment'></div>呦呦和鸣，麌麌狎至，彼泯虑于猜信，此无情于诚伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371866_comment'></div>孰是仓卒祸生，所忽毒镝欻以星贯，潜机划其电发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371866_comment'></div>或洞胸而达腋，或折足而碎骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371866_comment'></div>望林峦兮非远，顾町疃兮未灭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371866_comment'></div>风嗥泽而北迅，日掩山而西没；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371866_comment'></div>走骇侣于岩烟，叫饥麛于涧月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371866_comment'></div>苟行路之闻者，孰不心摧而思绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371866_comment'></div>相尔由矣，野心而仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371866_comment'></div>望纯束兮惊惋，顾获车兮逡巡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371866_comment'></div>视鼎中之消烂，观机上之剖分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371866_comment'></div>忽哀鸣以感类，若沈痛之在身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371866_comment'></div>虽复处之密迩，享以丰珍，比槛猿之骇跃，同海鸟之愁辛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371866_comment'></div>敢择音而后死，思走险其何因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371866_comment'></div>痛无知以相陷，含惋毒而莫伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371866_comment'></div>客有感而言曰：物诚有诸，人亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371866_comment'></div>摭事或比，原心则殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371866_comment'></div>借如淮阴搆祸，冤在神理，通说且拒，豨谋宁起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371866_comment'></div>堂堂萧公，实曰知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371866_comment'></div>绐致钟室，胡宁忍此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371866_comment'></div>吕禄之难，谁非汉臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371866_comment'></div>交则不义，卖亦不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371866_comment'></div>彼美郦生，既为交亲，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1371866", 1371866, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>诱袭</span>军印，岂无他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371866_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371866_comment'></div>微兽伤类，如不自容忍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371866_comment'></div>人卖友而享其功，灭交道兮坠义风，曾麋鹿之不若，何仁信之可宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371866_comment'></div>已焉哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371866_comment'></div>谅此世之茫茫，吾未见其始终。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1371866_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3d509be9708e4b0b9c30b721b9fa0604_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3d509be9708e4b0b9c30b721b9fa0604");'><span id='3d509be9708e4b0b9c30b721b9fa0604_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>，37岁</div><div id='3d509be9708e4b0b9c30b721b9fa0604' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　赴贬途中过襄阳，受山南东道节度使裴均的热情款待。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
宝鸡（陈仓）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b786e758e6a0418baa270f3bb447cefe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b786e758e6a0418baa270f3bb447cefe");'><span id='b786e758e6a0418baa270f3bb447cefe_link' id='poem_sentence_6_1371890_comment'></div>战跼无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371890_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371890_comment'></div>臣孤陋无取。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1371890_comment'></div>万乘忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371890_comment'></div>特记微臣之命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371890_comment'></div>衣分内府。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1371890_comment'></div>遽冒濡鹈之刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371890_comment'></div>在笥增感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371890_comment'></div>抚躬若惊。<div -----title
兰州（金城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='27df0b5207524c62a64b9a0ac6f2e8e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("27df0b5207524c62a64b9a0ac6f2e8e4");'><span id='27df0b5207524c62a64b9a0ac6f2e8e4_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年6月21日</a>　六月二十一日，至薄寒山，受吐蕃使者迎接。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年7月5日</a>　七月五日，都监使薛盈珍返京，吕温代其作状文，奏吐蕃事宜。作品：《代都监使奏吐蕃事宜状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第54页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代都监使奏吐蕃事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（804年7月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371900")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371900'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371900_comment'></div>臣前月十四日至清水县西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371900_comment'></div>吐蕃舍人郭至崇来迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371900_comment'></div>便请将书诏先去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371900_comment'></div>臣以二十一日到薄寒山西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371900_comment'></div>去蕃帅帐幕二十馀里停止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371900_comment'></div>至二十三日方见尚绮里徐拨布论乞心热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371900_comment'></div>奉宣进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371900_comment'></div>兼付赐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371900_comment'></div>莫不祗奉圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371900_comment'></div>感悦过望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371900_comment'></div>部落欢抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371900_comment'></div>道路讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371900_comment'></div>加以接待殷勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371900_comment'></div>供亿丰厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371900_comment'></div>竭诚归化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371900_comment'></div>形状可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371900_comment'></div>臣亲睹蕃情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371900_comment'></div>不胜庆跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371900_comment'></div>绮里徐等固欲令臣与薛伾领蕃使却归奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371900_comment'></div>臣当时苦争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371900_comment'></div>请赴衙帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371900_comment'></div>自辰及午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371900_comment'></div>意竟不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371900_comment'></div>今日再见恳论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371900_comment'></div>尽词往复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371900_comment'></div>势既难拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371900_comment'></div>恐失事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371900_comment'></div>即于今月五日令臣与张荐分背便发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371900_comment'></div>彷徨中路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371900_comment'></div>忧惧实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371900_comment'></div>心魂震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371900_comment'></div>进退无据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371900_comment'></div>谨勒某官某乙陈奏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371900_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1371900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=804&endYear=804')">804年7月</a>　孟秋，行至薄寒山，代张荐作起居表。作品：《代张侍郎起居表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第51页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代张侍郎起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（804年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371891")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371891'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371891_comment'></div>孟秋犹热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371891_comment'></div>伏惟圣躬万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371891_comment'></div>臣以去月二十一日到薄安山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371891_comment'></div>见蕃胡尚绮里徐等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371891_comment'></div>同令盈珍等却回奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371891_comment'></div>令臣取今月发赴衙帐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371891_comment'></div>伏惟圣德柔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371891_comment'></div>皇明烛幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371891_comment'></div>蕃情大欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371891_comment'></div>酋帅知感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371891_comment'></div>虔奉朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371891_comment'></div>宾礼使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371891_comment'></div>迎劳肃躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371891_comment'></div>馈饩丰洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371891_comment'></div>益知向化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371891_comment'></div>弥表革心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371891_comment'></div>臣恭备单车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371891_comment'></div>不胜庆忭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371891_comment'></div>严程方始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371891_comment'></div>绝域未穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371891_comment'></div>白日在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371891_comment'></div>瞻仰如近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371891_comment'></div>青蒲之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371891_comment'></div>伏奏犹赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371891_comment'></div>感恋彷徨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371891_comment'></div>罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371891_comment'></div>无任犬马屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371891_comment'></div>谨因中使第五忠宪附表起居以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1371891_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

玉树

class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371958'>府君讳沅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371958_comment'></div>字君梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371958_comment'></div>河东人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371958_comment'></div>祖崇嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371958_comment'></div>高尚丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371958_comment'></div>不应徵辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371958_comment'></div>考从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371958_comment'></div>皇朝左赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371958_comment'></div>府君性重厚寡言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371958_comment'></div>志于文学而炫耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371958_comment'></div>尤好神景化之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371958_comment'></div>虽迫亲故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371958_comment'></div>时或从人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371958_comment'></div>而焚香鍊气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371958_comment'></div>常澹如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371958_comment'></div>与从子某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371958_comment'></div>少同游处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371958_comment'></div>有疏阮之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371958_comment'></div>洎某出守湘中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371958_comment'></div>府君以山水之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371958_comment'></div>远来依憩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371958_comment'></div>不幸遇暴疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371958_comment'></div>元和五年七月二十二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371958_comment'></div>终于衡州官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371958_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371958_comment'></div>知命之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371958_comment'></div>未娶无嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371958_comment'></div>家童护奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371958_comment'></div>旅榇单归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371958_comment'></div>追怀平昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371958_comment'></div>何可胜痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371958_comment'></div>以其年十月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371958_comment'></div>权厝江陵城北某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371958_comment'></div>以须通岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371958_comment'></div>归祔松槚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371958_comment'></div>姑具时日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371958_comment'></div>记于此石云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1371958_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
石首
-----detail

-----title
岳阳（巴陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a3aa359e20944fe18d9591a978f7e383_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a3aa359e20944fe18d9591a978f7e383");'><span id='a3aa359e20944fe18d9591a978f7e383_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>，37岁</div><div id='a3aa359e20944fe18d9591a978f7e383' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴贬途中至岳州，登岳阳楼，作诗怀古。作品：《岳阳怀古》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第11页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岳阳怀古</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18489")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18489'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18489'>晨飙发荆州，落日到巴丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18489'>方知刳剡利，可接鬼神游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18489'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_18489", 18489, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>二湖</span>豁南寖，九派驶东流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18489'>襟带三千里，尽在岳阳楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18489'>忆昔斗群雄，此焉争上游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_18489'>吴昌屯虎旅，晋盛骛龙舟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_18489'>宋齐纷祸难，梁陈成寇雠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_18489'>钟鼓长震耀，鱼龙不得休。<div id='poem_sentence_7_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_18489'>风雪一萧散，功业忽如浮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_18489'>今日时无事，空江满白鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_18489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_18489'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_18489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴贬途中舟过洞庭湖，感叹作诗。作品：《风叹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第22页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>风叹</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18478")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18478'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18478'>青海风，飞沙射面随惊蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18478'>洞庭风，危樯欲折身若空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18478'>西驰南走有何事，会须一决百年中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18478'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_18478_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

衡阳
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年7月5日</a>　七月五日，到衡州刺史任上。当日，为窦常作厅壁记。作品：《湖南都团练副使厅壁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷10第112页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖南都团练副使厅壁记</a><span "poem_title_1371919")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371919'>湘中七郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371919_comment'></div>罗压上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371919_comment'></div>右振牂蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371919_comment'></div>左驰瓯越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371919_comment'></div>控交广之户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371919_comment'></div>扼吴蜀之咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371919_comment'></div>翼张四隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371919_comment'></div>襟束万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371919_comment'></div>半天下之安危系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371919_comment'></div>圣唐理虽偃革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371919_comment'></div>制不去备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371919_comment'></div>消息变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371919_comment'></div>必惟其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371919_comment'></div>由是部分荆衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371919_comment'></div>复古南镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371919_comment'></div>轻其兵徒而重其统帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371919_comment'></div>易其将校而难其参佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371919_comment'></div>所以显仁藏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371919_comment'></div>明道晦权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371919_comment'></div>成师于礼乐之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371919_comment'></div>讲武于文章之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371919_comment'></div>雍容易简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371919_comment'></div>四十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371919_comment'></div>名迹风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371919_comment'></div>冠于当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371919_comment'></div>始则裴谏议虬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371919_comment'></div>以逸材奇略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371919_comment'></div>傲视而静荒寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371919_comment'></div>次则赵相公璟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371919_comment'></div>以高标雅望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371919_comment'></div>郁起而为国桢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371919_comment'></div>其馀冯郎中嶷之硕重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371919_comment'></div>房容州孺复之英达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371919_comment'></div>郑评事冽张著作季文之美秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371919_comment'></div>洎张和州惟俭卢侍御澥佐我先大夫宣慈明允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371919_comment'></div>实有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371919_comment'></div>是皆焯于朝论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371919_comment'></div>清在人谣者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371919_comment'></div>元和三年冬。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1371919_comment'></div>京兆之懿则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371919_comment'></div>廷赐大旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371919_comment'></div>俾绥衡湘。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1371919_comment'></div>用人如止水无私鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371919_comment'></div>始下车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371919_comment'></div>表前副使殿中侍御史扶风窦君常字中行以本官复职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371919_comment'></div>于是监察御史河南穆君寂。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371919_comment'></div>称为盛府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371919_comment'></div>中行感会知巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371919_comment'></div>竭其诚能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371919_comment'></div>黄钟音韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371919_comment'></div>调于嶰谷之竹。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1371919_comment'></div>其吟鸾凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371919_comment'></div>断犀兕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371919_comment'></div>不足怪也。<div id='poem_sentence_75_1371919_comment'></div>一居方伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371919_comment'></div>二列华省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371919_comment'></div>四在诸侯之馆。<div id='poem_sentence_80_1371919_comment'></div>以温近守支郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371919_comment'></div>且知故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371919_comment'></div>得请连帅。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年7月</a>　七月五日到衡州刺史任后，作谢上表。作品：《衡州刺史谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第52页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州刺史谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371883")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371883'>臣某言。伏奉五月一日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371883_comment'></div>授臣使持节衡州诸军事守衡州刺史。散官勋赐如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371883_comment'></div>谨以七月十五日到本州上讫。恭承宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371883_comment'></div>循顾庸虚。感忭失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371883_comment'></div>战跼无地。臣某诚感诚惧顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371883_comment'></div>臣闻三载陟明。虞书盛典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371883_comment'></div>六条<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1371883", 1371883, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>举最</span>。汉制宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371883_comment'></div>必在上允帝俞。俯谐师锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371883_comment'></div>臣谬领郡务。素无吏能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371883_comment'></div>虔守国章。布宣皇化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371883_comment'></div>匪宁夙夜。再换炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371883_comment'></div>仰奉陛下忧勤。以恤远人凋瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371883_comment'></div>虽检身肃下。不敢愧于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371883_comment'></div>而阜俗移风。竟未彰于绩用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371883_comment'></div>将何以特膺睿奖。简在宸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371883_comment'></div>当恺悌之旁求。副循良之慎选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371883_comment'></div>省躬增愧。殒首知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371883_comment'></div>谨当恪励精诚。策磨朽钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371883_comment'></div>冀立日新之效。少酬天覆之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371883_comment'></div>实望圣慈。照臣肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371883_comment'></div>臣无任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1371883", 1371883, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>感跃</span>屏营之至。谨差某官某乙奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371883_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1371883_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年7月22日</a>　七月二十二日，吕温房叔吕沆病卒于衡州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7a12e4cb785147679f5218fdbb59f9dc_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年10月</a>　十月，有文祭房叔吕沆。作品：《祭侯官十七房叔父》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第89页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭侯官十七房叔文</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371971")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371971'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371971'>维元和五年岁次庚寅九月戊戌朔三日庚子。堂妷男朝议郎使持节衡州诸军事守衡州刺史上骑都尉赐绯鱼袋某乡贡进士让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371971_comment'></div>致祭十七房叔侯官府君之灵。私门薄佑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371971_comment'></div>终鲜诸父。堂从之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371971_comment'></div>唯叔一人。少小相依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371971_comment'></div>笔砚同学。永言素契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371971_comment'></div>情实兼常。早表诚言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371971_comment'></div>见托身事。官孤力薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371971_comment'></div>卒用无成。惭负幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371971_comment'></div>兴言痛咽。叔无允嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371971_comment'></div>后效何伸。河中大茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371971_comment'></div>礼合葬祔。十五房尚寓淮甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371971_comment'></div>时力未并。且于江陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371971_comment'></div>谨议权厝。终期通岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371971_comment'></div>异壤同归。皦日在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371971_comment'></div>誓无二事。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371971_comment'></div>五湖三湘。前岁共入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371971_comment'></div>孤舟单旐。今日何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371971_comment'></div>恸决江津。倍增摧慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371971_comment'></div>式具祖奠。伏惟尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371971_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1371971_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年10月</a>　在衡州刺史任。有文祭奠输税途中溺死百姓，并代交赋税。作品：《衡州祭柘里渡溺死百姓文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第90页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州祭者里渡溺死百姓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371969")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371969'>维元和五年岁次庚寅十月戊辰朔十七日甲申。刺史吕某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371969_comment'></div>遣故衙前虞候何防。以豚酒蔬果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371969_comment'></div>致祭苏升陈演李宽泰陈甫鲁馀之灵。尔等五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371969_comment'></div>感余诚信。力输公税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371969_comment'></div>争赴先期。溪山阻深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371969_comment'></div>潦水暴至。不忍欺我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371969_comment'></div>忘其险艰。州令未明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371969_comment'></div>津渡不谨。致此沦逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371969_comment'></div>咎由使君。兴言涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371969_comment'></div>痛念何及。聊伸薄酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371969_comment'></div>兼致微赠。代纳残税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371969_comment'></div>皆余俸钱。魂而有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371969_comment'></div>谅此深意。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371969_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1371969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在衡州刺史任。抚育其小弟吕让。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在衡州刺史任。调查户籍，查获隐户一万六千七百，上奏文。核定户税，减轻百姓负担，打击地方贪吏与兼并势力。作品：《简获隐户奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此文。）</span><div id='poem_1371896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>简获隐户奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371896")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371896'>当州旧额户一万八千四百七。除贫穷死绝老幼单孤不支济等外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371896_comment'></div>堪差科户八千二百五十七。臣到后团定户税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371896_comment'></div>次简责出所由隐藏不输税户一万六千七百。伏缘圣恩录臣在道州微效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371896_comment'></div>擢授大郡。令抚伤残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371896_comment'></div>臣昨寻旧案。询问闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371896_comment'></div>承前徵税。并无等第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371896_comment'></div>又二十馀年。都不定户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371896_comment'></div>存亡孰察。贫富不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371896_comment'></div>臣不敢因循。设法团定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371896_comment'></div>简获隐户。数约万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371896_comment'></div>州县虽不增徵科。所由已私自率敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371896_comment'></div>与其潜资于奸吏。岂若均助于疲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371896_comment'></div>臣请作此方圆。以救凋瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371896_comment'></div>庶得下免偏苦。止不阙供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371896_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1371896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在衡州刺史任。为李景俭岳父韦武作神道碑铭。作品：《唐故银青光禄京兆尹兼御史大夫上柱国赠吏部尚书京兆韦公神道碑铭并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷6第71页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕上柱国中山郡开国公食邑二千户赠陕州大都督博陵崔公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371962")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371962'>唐故银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕上柱国中山郡开国公食邑二千户赠陕州大都督博陵崔公。曾祖讳承福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝太中大夫广越二府都督。祖讳先意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝朝议大夫邓州刺史。父讳巘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371962_comment'></div>皇朝朝议大夫郑州长史。赠左散骑常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371962_comment'></div>状。斧藻天理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371962_comment'></div>立为人极。敬终端本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371962_comment'></div>彼所以将就诚明。褒殁劝存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371962_comment'></div>此所以砥砺名教。然而以道行巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371962_comment'></div>晦而弥光。大君子之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371962_comment'></div>以法考行。直而无党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371962_comment'></div>贤有司之职也。且曰献状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371962_comment'></div>则惟所知。公讳淙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371962_comment'></div>清臧而和。博厚而敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371962_comment'></div>岐嶷而夙茂。羁丱而老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371962_comment'></div>情约性充。静专动直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371962_comment'></div>出入孝悌。周旋忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371962_comment'></div>始以经明上第。调佐夏阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371962_comment'></div>次以词丽甲科。超尉王屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371962_comment'></div>事迫于官而举。言迫于事而扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371962_comment'></div>欲藏智而蒙滞来求。不近名而声华见逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371962_comment'></div>故相左仆射张公时尹洛京。首得才实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371962_comment'></div>洎镇荆蜀。致于幕庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371962_comment'></div>再兼理官。专领记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371962_comment'></div>捷笔良画。三邦有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371962_comment'></div>旋遘内艰。毁瘠仅立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371962_comment'></div>善居得礼。族党称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371962_comment'></div>免丧之岁。天子南狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371962_comment'></div>大尉西平王大会兵车。将图匡复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371962_comment'></div>公首膺辟命。浚发义心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371962_comment'></div>琴未成声。屦及于路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371962_comment'></div>感激而将星芒怒。谋谟而兵祲廓清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371962_comment'></div>翠华既还。优典斯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371962_comment'></div>拜殿中侍御史。时有宠臣为京兆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371962_comment'></div>政以暴闻。吏有冤弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371962_comment'></div>公表陈枉直。伏阁待旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371962_comment'></div>言忠主悟。事寝风生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371962_comment'></div>以绳违称职。转侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371962_comment'></div>以求瘼慎选。为华原令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371962_comment'></div>大兵之后。旱岁为虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371962_comment'></div>公劳徕不倦。弛张以宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371962_comment'></div>复流庸于润屋。辟旷土为多稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371962_comment'></div>俄改歙州刺史。地杂瓯骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371962_comment'></div>号为难理。下车而简其约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371962_comment'></div>期月而明其信誓。然后破散溪聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371962_comment'></div>剪锄山豪。既去害群之奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371962_comment'></div>遂宁挺险之俗。徵拜长安县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371962_comment'></div>威声先路。不肃而理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371962_comment'></div>铓刃馀地。所投皆虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371962_comment'></div>擢同州刺史。图歉于丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371962_comment'></div>量赈为籴。号里仓者三百所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371962_comment'></div>而凶年备矣。戒以暴骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371962_comment'></div>谕之速朽。成薄葬者九百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371962_comment'></div>而奢俗惩矣。群人有豪夺乡茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371962_comment'></div>阴持吏失。朋搆讼狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371962_comment'></div>累政患之。公断以寻斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371962_comment'></div>破其囊橐。人乐其杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371962_comment'></div>而法制行焉。郡城自御寇之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371962_comment'></div>复隍殆尽。朝贡所经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371962_comment'></div>夷夏何仰。公悦使襁负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371962_comment'></div>大兴版筑。下不知役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371962_comment'></div>而扃固立焉。其馀则去思有碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371962_comment'></div>详在篆述。可覆视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371962_comment'></div>朝议陟明。迁于陕服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371962_comment'></div>封介晋楚。寄分函洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371962_comment'></div>而戎备不修。兵库虚闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371962_comment'></div>公乃鸠工以利器。阅实以练卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371962_comment'></div>金革中度。义勇知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371962_comment'></div>既而有淮西之役。晨命暮具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371962_comment'></div>凛然而可观矣。河出城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371962_comment'></div>造舟为梁。经费僝工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371962_comment'></div>败决相继。公乃沉石而双固中沚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371962_comment'></div>省舰而三分巨流。水与意会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371962_comment'></div>势若天成。既而有奔涛之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371962_comment'></div>智胜功显。终然而无害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371962_comment'></div>其馀则三降玺书。就加爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371962_comment'></div>是明徵也。移疾入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371962_comment'></div>贰职冬官。归载不过图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371962_comment'></div>留府盈乎粟帛。丰公约私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371962_comment'></div>于是乎在。既至陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371962_comment'></div>以尚书致仕。室不交要路之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371962_comment'></div>口不言当代之事。就阴委顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371962_comment'></div>谈者多之。公自解巾至于撤乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371962_comment'></div>思不踰矩。动无越思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371962_comment'></div>以忠贞为仕模。以勤俭为家训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371962_comment'></div>身居侯邸。清节如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371962_comment'></div>男降王姬。素风愈励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371962_comment'></div>羁孤聚室。人各忘其亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371962_comment'></div>布褐分庭。士不知其贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371962_comment'></div>体温柔而事至能断。性坦易而物莫能窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371962_comment'></div>当官不务于名声。所去必遗其功利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371962_comment'></div>氓谣尚在。时论可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371962_comment'></div>巳踰书葬之期。谨举易名之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371962_comment'></div>谨状。元和三年四月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371962_comment'></div>故银青光禄大夫守工部尚书致仕赠陕州大都督博陵崔公从外甥朝议郎行尚书司封员外郎上骑都尉赐绯鱼袋吕温谨上尚书考功。夫立身之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371962_comment'></div>始于君亲。中于其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371962_comment'></div>终于其身。若府君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371962_comment'></div>居丧有闻。临难有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371962_comment'></div>善其始也。勤于官业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371962_comment'></div>惠于鳏寡。敬其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371962_comment'></div>家事以理。年至而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371962_comment'></div>谨其终也。率是三懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371962_comment'></div>光于前训。以咨谥法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371962_comment'></div>无愧至公。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371962_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_103_1371962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在衡州刺史任。有文论“祭”作品：《祭说》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此文。）</span><div id='poem_1371953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭说</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371953")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371953'>吕和叔曰。祭先之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371953_comment'></div>自天子至于庶人。节文名物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371953_comment'></div>差等虽繁。然以礼事亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371953_comment'></div>其义则一。寝庙虽不崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371953_comment'></div>而修除不可不严。牲物虽不腆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371953_comment'></div>而享饎不可不亲。器皿虽不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371953_comment'></div>而濯溉不可不洁。礼虽不得为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371953_comment'></div>而诚意不可不尽。故斋宿荐彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371953_comment'></div>致爱与恭。岂可徇流俗燕亵之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371953_comment'></div>同鄙陋不经之事。然虽未能方古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371953_comment'></div>亦当略举春秋之荐。旬日具修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371953_comment'></div>三日斋戒。务在躬亲诚洁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371953_comment'></div>近世祭多及旁亲。虽近爱而无义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371953_comment'></div>礼惟殇与无后。始祭于宗子家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371953_comment'></div>自馀祭皆为祭非其鬼。盖致隆祖者不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371953_comment'></div>士大夫止当祭五祀耳。山川百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371953_comment'></div>皆国家所行。不可得而祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371953_comment'></div>近世流俗。妄行祭祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371953_comment'></div>黩慢莫甚。岂有受福之理哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371953_comment'></div>水旱之灾。止可相率祈祷里社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371953_comment'></div>至诚斋洁。奠以酒脯可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371953_comment'></div>若妄行望祀。合聚群小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371953_comment'></div>喧呼鼓乐。非士君子所宜为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371953_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1371953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在衡州刺史任。感怀作诗。作品：《冬夜即事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第21页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。赵荣蔚《吕温年谱》系此诗于元和六年，然元和六年八月吕温即卒，故系此诗于本年。）</span><div id='poem_18480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬夜即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18480")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18480'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18480'>百忧攒心起复卧，夜长耿耿不可过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18480'>风吹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_18480", 18480, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>雪片</span>似花落，月照冰文如镜破。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18480'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_18480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在衡州刺史任。早春，游黄溪，有诗。作品：《衡州早春偶游黄溪口号》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第16页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州早春偶游黄溪口号</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18504")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18504'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18504'>偶寻皇溪日欲没，早梅未尽山樱发。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18504'>无事江城闭此身，不得坐待花间月。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18504'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_18504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　在衡州刺史任。早春，游合江亭，有诗。作品：《衡州岁前游合江亭见樱蕊未坼因赋含彩吝惊春》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第15页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span>《合江亭槛前多高竹不见远岸花客命剪之感而成咏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第16页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18468' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　道、衡二州百姓自发地用各种形式，沉痛哀悼吕温病逝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年10月</a>　十月，吕温丧至江陵。二十四日，藁葬于江陵之野。时元稹、刘禹锡、柳宗元皆在贬所，有诗哭之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年10月</a>　十月，窦巩自黔州北归，至江陵，亦作诗哭吕温。<br /></div>

-----title
道县（营道）
