onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_18483", 18483, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>多露</span>悔，强进触藩羸。<div id='poem_sentence_20_18483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（一作生）</span>化，一失何驱驰。<div id='poem_sentence_22_18483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_18483'>不如任行止，委命<span id='poem_sentence_30_18483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>　在道州刺史任。上表贺册皇太子。作品：《贺册皇太子表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第52页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺册皇太子表</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371871")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371871'>臣某言。伏见十月十二日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371871_comment'></div>伏承皇太子以四月二十一日册命礼毕。光绍前典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371871_comment'></div>惟怀永图。神人允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371871_comment'></div>动植咸赖。臣某诚欢诚忭顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371871_comment'></div>臣闻燕翼贻谋。帝王之大孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371871_comment'></div>立嫡主器。礼易之明训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371871_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下克明峻德。恢纂鸿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371871_comment'></div>武功有成。文理既定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371871_comment'></div>然后宏三王之教谕。建万国之元良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371871_comment'></div>凡在生灵。孰不庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371871_comment'></div>臣守官荒服。称贺无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371871_comment'></div>窃忭岭隅。倍万恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371871_comment'></div>无任感悦屏营之至。谨奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371871_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1371871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在道州刺史任上。春，游城北欧阳家林亭，有诗记其事。作品：《道州春游欧阳家林亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第16页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_18500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/18500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州春游欧阳家林亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_18500")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_18500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_18500'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18500'>道州城北欧阳家，去郭一里占烟霞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18500'>主人虽朴甚有思，解留满地红桃花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18500'>桃花成泥不须扫，明朝更访桃源老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_18500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18500'>政成兴足告即<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>归，门前便是家山道。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18500'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_18500'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_18500_0'>⑴ 一作即告，又作则告</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_18500_comment'></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_18500'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(18500)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年5月</a>　五月，裴均集其父裴倩昔日避乱江西时与柳浑等唱和之诗为《裴氏海昏集》，吕温序之。作品：《裴氏海昏集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第31页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>裴氏海昏集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371917")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371917'>海昏集者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371917_comment'></div>有唐文行之臣故度支郎中专判度支事赠尚书左仆射正平郡公裴氏讳某字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371917_comment'></div>考地毓德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371917_comment'></div>会友辅仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371917_comment'></div>气志如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371917_comment'></div>英华发外之所由作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371917_comment'></div>初公违河洛之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371917_comment'></div>以其族行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371917_comment'></div>攀大别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371917_comment'></div>浮彭蠡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371917_comment'></div>望洞庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371917_comment'></div>徘徊乎湓流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371917_comment'></div>眄仰乎海昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371917_comment'></div>有欧山之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371917_comment'></div>修江之清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371917_comment'></div>阳溪之邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371917_comment'></div>汤泉之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371917_comment'></div>竹洞花坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371917_comment'></div>仙坛僧舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371917_comment'></div>鸡犬钟梵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371917_comment'></div>相闻于青岚白云中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371917_comment'></div>数百里不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371917_comment'></div>时也俗以远而未扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371917_comment'></div>地以偏而获宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371917_comment'></div>开元之遗老尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371917_comment'></div>犹歌咏乎太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371917_comment'></div>公悠然乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371917_comment'></div>遂与我外王父故屯田郎中集贤殿学士河东柳公讳某外叔祖故相国宜城伯讳浑洎故太常卿兰陵萧公定故秘书少监范阳卢公虚舟故左庶子陇西李公勋为尘外之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371917_comment'></div>极心期之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371917_comment'></div>唯故给事中汝南袁公高故将作监河南元公亘以后进预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371917_comment'></div>江左搢绅诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371917_comment'></div>望之如神仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371917_comment'></div>邈不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371917_comment'></div>每赋一泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371917_comment'></div>题一石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371917_comment'></div>毫墨未乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371917_comment'></div>传咏巳遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371917_comment'></div>其为物情所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1371917", 1371917, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>注慕</span>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371917_comment'></div>无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371917_comment'></div>朝廷命公盈虚东南漕引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371917_comment'></div>吴楚中原百万之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371917_comment'></div>仰食于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371917_comment'></div>人不堪烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371917_comment'></div>我若无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371917_comment'></div>往往佩联印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371917_comment'></div>拥大盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371917_comment'></div>枉道而过旧山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371917_comment'></div>林壑之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371917_comment'></div>琴诗不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371917_comment'></div>心计颐指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371917_comment'></div>而军国饫赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371917_comment'></div>其大雅之全才者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371917_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371917_comment'></div>太尉侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371917_comment'></div>勤劳王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371917_comment'></div>惠于生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371917_comment'></div>至公再世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371917_comment'></div>又以盛德屈于年运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371917_comment'></div>庆如壅川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371917_comment'></div>其决必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371917_comment'></div>由是焜耀之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371917_comment'></div>重集于我郇公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371917_comment'></div>郇公始以大孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371917_comment'></div>中以大用显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371917_comment'></div>次以大忠升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371917_comment'></div>藩屏三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371917_comment'></div>出入二揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371917_comment'></div>述先职而掌邦赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371917_comment'></div>修祖德而践台衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371917_comment'></div>理荆之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371917_comment'></div>篆在乐石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371917_comment'></div>定蜀之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371917_comment'></div>藏在册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371917_comment'></div>汉南之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371917_comment'></div>方洽于人谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1371917_comment'></div>加以优游艺文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1371917_comment'></div>惇悦经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1371917_comment'></div>身被华衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1371917_comment'></div>门全素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1371917_comment'></div>不畏强御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1371917_comment'></div>不侮孤贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1371917_comment'></div>久要皆当代长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1371917_comment'></div>推毂必一时俊杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1371917_comment'></div>海内士大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1371917_comment'></div>如鳞羽之归龙凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1371917_comment'></div>君子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1371917_comment'></div>宪公忠献公之勋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1371917_comment'></div>节公之雅道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1371917_comment'></div>为不亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1371917_comment'></div>郇公以霜露之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1371917_comment'></div>泣编遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1371917_comment'></div>思所以垂诸不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1371917_comment'></div>以为节公消息出处之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1371917_comment'></div>始于海昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1371917_comment'></div>遂于正集外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1371917_comment'></div>别次当时唱和游览饯劳之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1371917_comment'></div>凡九十六篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1371917_comment'></div>勒为海昏集上下卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1371917_comment'></div>不远三千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1371917_comment'></div>授简于小生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1371917_comment'></div>俾酌归趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1371917_comment'></div>而为序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1371917_comment'></div>某尝备中台之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1371917_comment'></div>实辱至公之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1371917_comment'></div>闻命巳哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1371917_comment'></div>敬不敢文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1371917_comment'></div>为姑陈古义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1371917_comment'></div>用赞风训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1371917_comment'></div>昔者三代陈诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1371917_comment'></div>以观民风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1371917_comment'></div>诈信淫义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1371917_comment'></div>躁静刚柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1371917_comment'></div>于是乎取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1371917_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1371917_comment'></div>吉凶存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1371917_comment'></div>于是乎观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1371917_comment'></div>兆于此必应于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1371917_comment'></div>成乎终必见乎始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1371917_comment'></div>诗不可以为伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1371917_comment'></div>魏公子为南皮之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1371917_comment'></div>以浮华相高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1371917_comment'></div>故其诗傲荡骄志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1371917_comment'></div>胜而专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1371917_comment'></div>勤而不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1371917_comment'></div>晋名士为金谷之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1371917_comment'></div>以邪侈相扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1371917_comment'></div>故其诗滥溺淫志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1371917_comment'></div>冶而缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1371917_comment'></div>往而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1371917_comment'></div>正平公为海昏之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1371917_comment'></div>以礼义相诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1371917_comment'></div>故其诗恬淡退志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1371917_comment'></div>庄直立志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1371917_comment'></div>退以独全其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1371917_comment'></div>立以兼济于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1371917_comment'></div>立而不矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1371917_comment'></div>退而不怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1371917_comment'></div>适而不放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1371917_comment'></div>乐而不荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1371917_comment'></div>亲而不比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1371917_comment'></div>数而不黩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1371917_comment'></div>如切如磋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1371917_comment'></div>婉而有直体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1371917_comment'></div>曰比曰兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1371917_comment'></div>近而有深致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1371917_comment'></div>仁者见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1371917_comment'></div>遁世而无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1371917_comment'></div>知者见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1371917_comment'></div>爱身而有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1371917_comment'></div>暧乎若冬阳之煦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1371917_comment'></div>油乎若春泽之浸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1371917_comment'></div>其诱人也易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1371917_comment'></div>其感人也深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1371917_comment'></div>卒不知其所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1371917_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1371917_comment'></div>则观南皮之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1371917_comment'></div>应刘焉得不夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1371917_comment'></div>魏祚焉得不短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1371917_comment'></div>观金谷之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1371917_comment'></div>潘石焉得不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1371917_comment'></div>晋室焉得不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1371917_comment'></div>观海昏之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1371917_comment'></div>裴氏焉得不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1371917_comment'></div>我唐焉得不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1371917_comment'></div>诗之时义大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1371917_comment'></div>天人家国之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1371917_comment'></div>其至矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1371917_comment'></div>为节公郇公之子孙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1371917_comment'></div>其无忘哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_168_1371917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年5月</a>　五六月间，在道州代郑絪拟谢上表。作品：《代郑南海谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷5第53页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑南海谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371884")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371884'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371884_comment'></div>臣自远离阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371884_comment'></div>晨夜奔涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371884_comment'></div>祗承宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371884_comment'></div>不敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371884_comment'></div>谨以某月某日到所部上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371884_comment'></div>仰宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371884_comment'></div>亲谕远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371884_comment'></div>酬恩之效未期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371884_comment'></div>恋主之诚已积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371884_comment'></div>臣某诚恐诚惧顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371884_comment'></div>臣本章句诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371884_comment'></div>器用无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371884_comment'></div>徒以小心畏敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371884_comment'></div>谬为先圣所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371884_comment'></div>趋奏禁闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371884_comment'></div>浸踰星纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371884_comment'></div>属内外危疑之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371884_comment'></div>是非剖判之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371884_comment'></div>实以艰贞自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371884_comment'></div>中立无倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371884_comment'></div>天高听近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371884_comment'></div>愚款获申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371884_comment'></div>神幽鉴明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371884_comment'></div>昌运斯属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371884_comment'></div>遂蒙陛下擢于侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371884_comment'></div>超冠等伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371884_comment'></div>用其忧国之寸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371884_comment'></div>委以代天之重务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371884_comment'></div>俯偻三命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371884_comment'></div>炎凉五周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371884_comment'></div>登车奉驭朽之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371884_comment'></div>假寐感宵衣之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371884_comment'></div>徒耗神用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371884_comment'></div>莫能将明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371884_comment'></div>箧盈谤而方赐駃騠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371884_comment'></div>鼎折足而未忘簪履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371884_comment'></div>竟以陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371884_comment'></div>遂其优容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371884_comment'></div>无绮季夏黄之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371884_comment'></div>而猥当调护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371884_comment'></div>无窦融贾复之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371884_comment'></div>而获奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371884_comment'></div>以此没齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371884_comment'></div>犹为负恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371884_comment'></div>岂意曾未踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371884_comment'></div>忽蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1371884", 1371884, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>抽奖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1371884_comment'></div>庙授鈇钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1371884_comment'></div>廷赐旌旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1371884_comment'></div>俾臣懦夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1371884_comment'></div>当此大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1371884_comment'></div>节制五岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1371884_comment'></div>幅员万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1371884_comment'></div>伏波之铜柱犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1371884_comment'></div>永谢奇功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1371884_comment'></div>士燮之鼓吹日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1371884_comment'></div>弥惭武干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1371884_comment'></div>将何以宣美皇化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1371884_comment'></div>振扬国威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1371884_comment'></div>洗愆责于千龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1371884_comment'></div>答生成于再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1371884_comment'></div>唯当举章修法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1371884_comment'></div>苦节清心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1371884_comment'></div>抚犷俗以思柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1371884_comment'></div>酌贪泉而无惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1371884_comment'></div>庶几万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1371884_comment'></div>仰副忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1371884_comment'></div>但以白日在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1371884_comment'></div>长安不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1371884_comment'></div>丹涯限地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1371884_comment'></div>溟海方深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1371884_comment'></div>顾蒲柳之前衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1371884_comment'></div>奉轩墀而尚远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1371884_comment'></div>无任感恋屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1371884_comment'></div>谨差某官某奉表陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1371884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在道州刺史任。重书元结《道州刺史厅壁记》于道州刺史厅中，并感而作后记。作品：《道州刺史厅后记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷10第111页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州刺史厅后记</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371918")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371918'>壁记非古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371918_comment'></div>若冠绶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1371918", 1371918, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>命秩</span>之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371918_comment'></div>则有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1371918", 1371918, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>格令</span>在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371918_comment'></div>山川风物之辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371918_comment'></div>则有图牒在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371918_comment'></div>所以为之记者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371918_comment'></div>岂不欲述理道列贤不肖以训于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371918_comment'></div>庶中人以上得化其心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371918_comment'></div>代之作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371918_comment'></div>率异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371918_comment'></div>或誇学名数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371918_comment'></div>或务工为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371918_comment'></div>居其官而自记者则媚巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371918_comment'></div>不居其官而代人记者则媚人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371918_comment'></div>春秋之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371918_comment'></div>盖委地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371918_comment'></div>贤二千石河南元结字次山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371918_comment'></div>自作道州刺史厅事记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371918_comment'></div>既彰善而不党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371918_comment'></div>亦指恶而不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371918_comment'></div>直举胸臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1371918_comment'></div>用为鉴戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1371918_comment'></div>昭昭吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1371918_comment'></div>长在屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1371918_comment'></div>后之贪虐放肆以生人为戏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1371918_comment'></div>独不愧于心乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1371918_comment'></div>予自幼时读古循吏传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1371918_comment'></div>慕其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1371918_comment'></div>以为士大夫立名于代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1371918_comment'></div>无以高此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1371918_comment'></div>前年冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1371918_comment'></div>由尚书刑部郎中出为此州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1371918_comment'></div>虽履剧自课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1371918_comment'></div>而未能逮其意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1371918_comment'></div>往刺史有许子良者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1371918_comment'></div>辄移元次山记于北牖下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1371918_comment'></div>而以其文代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1371918_comment'></div>后亦有时号君子之清者莅此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1371918_comment'></div>熟视焉而莫之改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1371918_comment'></div>岂是非之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1371918_comment'></div>如是其难乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1371918_comment'></div>予也鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1371918_comment'></div>安知其他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1371918_comment'></div>则命圬而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1371918_comment'></div>俾复其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1371918_comment'></div>且为后记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1371918_comment'></div>以广次山之志云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1371918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年5月</a>　在道州刺史任。五月，吕温为减除“政令之弊”，使官吏和百姓知法守法，与法吏何洛庭一起修定《道州律令要录》，并亲为作序。作品：《道州律令要录序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷3第31页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州律令要录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371913")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371913'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371913'>某顷累忝官尚书省御史台。遍观诸曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371913_comment'></div>多书令式格律于其屋壁。苟非以宦游为情而奉其职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371913_comment'></div>皆得日夕省览。卧起出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371913_comment'></div>目存心悟。累累然如贯珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371913_comment'></div>如循环。吏无以欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371913_comment'></div>临事不惑。决繁滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371913_comment'></div>举枉直。而协于大中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371913_comment'></div>中人以上。固可驯致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371913_comment'></div>吾不知其谁首之。何前贤处心恤事之周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371913_comment'></div>若州县者。卑而近于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371913_comment'></div>远而切于得失。动有悬人命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371913_comment'></div>关风俗。而惰者委成于一吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1371913_comment'></div>望空而署。勤者检阅而山积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1371913_comment'></div>神愤气沮。卒无所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1371913_comment'></div>致政之弊。不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1371913_comment'></div>此州法吏何洛庭。良吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1371913_comment'></div>与之撮其要。讲其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1371913_comment'></div>书于厅事之左。某不深于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1371913_comment'></div>犹虑未尽。后来君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1371913_comment'></div>其究成之。此长人者之所急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1371913_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1371913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在道州任上以法治州，派遣官吏缉逮强盗，侦破案件，严厉打击刑事犯罪之徒，为受害百姓伸冤，整顿地方治安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　吕温治理道州，仅仅一年，即实著效绩。御史中丞、湖南团练观察使李众表荐吕温为衡州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在道州任，奏请立舜庙于州西之九嶷山。作品：《请立舜庙表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（丛书集成初编本《吕衡州文集》未收此文。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年</a>　在道州任，作文祭百姓。作品：《道州祭百姓邓助、费念文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷8第89页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_1371970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1371970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1371970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州祭百姓邓助费念文</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14605, "中唐", "吕温", "poem_title_1371970")'>吕温</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1371970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1371970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1371970'>维元和五年岁次庚寅五月庚子朔七日景午。刺史吕某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1371970_comment'></div>遣衙前虞候蒋沼。以酒脯之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1371970_comment'></div>告邓助费念之灵。使君受命牧汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1371970_comment'></div>不能庇护。使贼孟鸾等敢作不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1371970_comment'></div>酷加杀害。是用疚心疾首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1371970_comment'></div>万计讨擒。廉使仁明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1371970_comment'></div>不贷凶恶。穷泉冤痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1371970_comment'></div>今日方申。惭念无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1371970_comment'></div>潸然泣下。故令于汝殁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1371970_comment'></div>陈贼之尸。魂而有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1371970_comment'></div>歆此告酹。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1371970_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1371970_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年5月11日</a>　五月十一日，因吕温治有善状，诏改衡州刺史。吕温离道州前夕，巡察州内五县，有诗记事。作品：《道州弘道县主簿、知县，三年颇著廉慎，秩满县阙申使请留，将赴衡州，题其厅事》<span id='poem_content_18461'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_18461'>为理赖同力，陟明非所任。<div id='poem_sentence_0_18461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_18461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_18461'>烦君驻归棹，与慰不欺心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_18461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_18461'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_18461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_18412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_18412'>闻说慇勤海阳事，令人转忆舜祠山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_18412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年6月</a>　六月，自江华乘船沿营水北上衡阳，途中有诗。作品：《自江华之衡阳途中作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吕衡州文集》卷2第14页，中华书局1985年丛书集成初编本。）</span><div id='poem_18410' 永州（零陵）
